p begynneth lyf saint katherin senis blessid virgin p audi filia et vide doughter see fructuous example vertuous liuinge edyfycacio thy sowle co forte encrese thy gostly labour werkis pyte truste gracious yeftes oure lorde jhesu thy wyll sette plese hym hym secuyce holy excercise vertue obedyence vnder counseyll techinge thy gostely gouernours moche fele longe experyens inward affeccions inclynyng wyth pyte comforte haue nede bothe lyuyng dede therfore strengthe coforte thy wil al thi gostely sustere whiche lord hath graciously chose serue hym nyght day prayer meditacio laboure bodely tyme nede socour helpe seke poure purpos lordis mercy worshyppe wyth truste grace leue helpe prayer translate englysshe tongue legende blessid lyf holy mayde virgyn whiche callyd katheryn sene legende compyled worshypfull clerke fryer reymond ordre saynt domynik doctor deuynyte co fessour holy virgyn translacion leue two prologue whiche begynnyng clerke made latyn whiche passeth vnderstondyng touche alle mater longeth lernyng cause moche maner vertuous lyuyng shall rehersyd especial chapytres boke whiche generall wordes toucheth shortely prologue leue also poyntes diuynyte whiche passeth vnderston dyng touche mater yt longeth lernyng tha sayde begynning doughter see thou herest redest holy mayde vyrgyn thou yeue full credence shal wryte veryte may preuyd wythout ony feynyng biscryptures confessours verefyeng creature whiche late lyued erthe also vytnes purpose put ende eche chapytre worshypfull clerke dide whiche compyled boke latyn therfore werke begynne perfourmed name holy trynyte boke shall deuyded thre partyes eche parte boke shal departed diuerse chapyters whiche chapyters compyled gyder begynnyng manere kalendre ye mowe redely fynde matere boke ye desyre rede p fyrst parte boke shal byrth holy werkis mayde chyldhode tendre age time spoused merueylously gracyously lord p seconde parte conteyneth maner conuersacion tyme despousacion lord lord wrought tyme yt passyd world p thyrde parte shall shewe passyng world mayde myracles whiche lord wrought lyf thus bi mercy graunt lord almyghty werke shall termynyd lawde holy trynyte honour glorye euer wythout ende amen capitulum j fyrste chapytre fyrste parte forsayde blessyd mayde virgyn katheryn treteth progenyte mater whiche byfyll touchyng te openly abrode fader moder condycions c ij p byrthe merueylous werkynge whiche lord wrought shewed chylhode holy mayde vyrgyn c iij item vowe made vyrgynyte vertuous lyuynge myracles whiche befyll tyl came age abylyte wedded man wedded neuer wolde c iiij p item feruour deuocyon wythdrawe whiche lord suffred encrece grace folowyng stronge pacience wyth whiche pacience suffred faders hous many iniuryes c v p item victorie whiche hadde theym desesed culuer whiche fader sawe vysyon saint domynyk c vj p item hardenesse bodely penaunce afflyccion persecucion suffred therfore moder ca vij p item laste vyctorye hadde bathe toke habyte saint dominyk whiche longe desyred tofore ca viij p item begynnyge fondament relygyous state susteren penaunce saynt domynyke wherfore come maner liuynge susteren c ix p item wonderfull encrece profyted vertu holy lyuyng shold leuyd thynges whiche rehersed consessour grace doo lord c x p item noble doctryue notable whiche lord gaue begynnyng doctrynes whiche founded maner lyuynge capitulum xj item merueyll victorye temptacions another maner doctryne yeue lorde famylyaryte homlyhed whiche hadde lord whiche hath beherde fore c xij p item merueylous despousacio wyth whiche wedded faythe lorde oure lorde wyth arynge c xiij begynneth second parte whiche shewed capitulum j conuersacion holy mayde vyrgyn wyth men yeftes whiche receyued lorde pryuely enclosed wythin self openly shewed worlde firste lord bad sholde conuersaunt amonge men c ij item merueylous dedes whiche hadde excercise myracles whiche befyll begynnyng conuersacion amonge men c iij p item wonder whiche dyde helpe comfort necessyte poure nedy c iiij item merueylous dedes whiche dyde lowly besy seruyce theym seke c v p item synguler maner lyuinge desceyued grutched wyth merueylous fastynge capitulum vj p item wonderfull rauysshynge excess mynde hyr bodely wyttes grete reuelacions shewed hyr lord c vij p item somme myracles graciously wrought holy mayde virgin aboute helthe sowles c viij p item somme myracles doo hyr lyf hyr aboute lyf helpe mennys bodyes c ix p item myracles vrought thys holy mayde vyrgyn aboute delyueraunce whiche acombred vexed wyth fendes c x p item yefte prophecye yefte delyuerd many wymmen fro perylles bothe body sowle c xj p item myracles whiche oure lorde wrought holy mayde vyrgyn herbes breed wyne thinges hadde none lyf c xij item ofte resceyuynge holy sacrament aulter myracles whiche oure lorde dyde hyr touching holy sacrament holy relyques saintes ca xiij begynneth thyrde parte wherin rehersyd capitulum j deyeng holy mayde vyrgyn myracles shewed deth fyrst wytnesses whiche present hyr passyng enfourmed auctur boke whiche cap ij p item merueylous thynges whiche befyll yere half fore deth holy mayde vyrgyn martyrdome suffred bodely wycked fendes wherof ye laste hadde bodely dethe c iij p item holy mayde vyrgyn desyred vnbounde body wyth cryst preuyd deuoute prayer whiche made put ende another boke whiche made boke generally shortely wryten boke wyth oryson c iiij p item time passed whan passed worlde sermo whiche made gostely dyscyples susteren tofore passyng informed generall speciall shold gouerne theym whan go vysyon whiche shewed matrone houre passyng ca v p item token myracles whiche oure lorde wrought hyr dethe holy mayde vyrgyn bothe tofore beryeng saye myracles whiche knowe many knowe cap vj p item myghty stronge paciens whiche mayde vyrgyn shewed openly fyrst age yonge deth whiche vertu clerly preuyd ryghtfull worthy haue name holynesse goddes chirche erthe whan made fayre gloryous goddes chirche heuen chapytre recapitulacion sayd fore worthynes also werynes reders also yf eche man may haue al thys legende may haue substaunce martyr tofore compendyously rehersyd last chapytre p fyrst chapytre fyrst parte progenye holy mayde vyrgyn gloryous saint katheryn sene mater whiche befyll touchyng went openly abrode fader moder condycions theym capitulu primu cite geene italye prouynce tuskane ther man name janes jacob fader callyd comyn speche ye contree beuencasa james symple vertuous wythout fraude deceyte ony man dredynge god fleyng alle euyll deth fader moder toke wyf cyte name lapa woman wythout suche malyce vsed amonge men ben tyme full besy aboute longeth houshold meynye seruauntes knowen openly knewe whyle liued erthe whan bothe ioyned gyder matrymonye lyuyd vertuously symplycite suffycient habondaunce hadde temperall godes bothe gentyll commendable byrthe reuerende lorde blessyd lapa graciously fulfylled hyr plentuously wyth birthe chyldren habondaunt vyne hous jacob whiche husbond eche yere almost conceyued bare sone doughter ofte fythes ij sone two doughters tyme jacob passeth worlde lapa wyf synguler laude commendacion rehersyd saide mayster reymonde confessour holy mayde vyrgyn glorious martyr katheryn euer soo lyke dysposycion soo moderate worde occacion euer came trouble trybulacion exceded neuer speche hasty ne angrye worde whan saw ony meyny greued herd hem speke angerly bytter wordes anon comforted eche theym wyth glad sayde ye maner contree brother good day troubled speke suche wordes falleth ne semeth v speke p speciall lapa wyf wherseth whan tyme one neybours dysesyd hym wrongfully asked hym grete monye whiche owed none reason soo moche vexed hym symple wyth might frendes supplanted hym wyth grete wronges brought hym losse alle godes alle tyme good man myght neuer suffre presence man curse hym wronge ne speke hym harme noo wyse soo moche blamed wyf lapa wyth softe wordes sayd suffre dere wyf ye good day lord shall shewe hym therrour shall oure defendour whiche wordes founde southe afterward veryte shewed openly lyke myracle payne hadde conscyence delyuerd agayne moche hadde errid wrongfull persecucion good man jacob thyse wordes sayde lapa mayster reymonde who wordes yaue full truste knowe knewe soo moche symplenesse age xxiiij yere though wold haue lyed wde haue feyned suche lesyng soo commyn testymonye alle tho knewe husbonde jacob man ful symple innocencye ryghtfull alwaye fleyng euyll also good mannys softenes speche soo vertuous alle meyny namely wymmen dame sels taught soole myght speke ne noo worde semely dyshoneste moche one doughter whiche callyd bonauentura wedded yonge man whiche callyd nycolas cyte wyth whome conuersaunt many yong men hys age cause hadde nother fader ne moder thyse men wythout ony refreynynge tongue spake eche wyth wyth hym foule wordes dyshoneste mater bonauentura att laste toke therof soo grete heuynes fyll suche sykenes fro day daye waxed lene vanysshed almost awaye ryght feble husbonde sawe asked hyr cause heuynesse sekenesse answerd sayde norysshed myn faders hour neuer wonte suche wordes euery daye neuer taught fader moder wherfor knowe sothe dishoneste speche bee avoyded fro hous wythin shorte tyme ye shall see deed whan husbond herde bothe avoyded vngoodly langage felawshyppe therwyth edefyed moche euer well vertues lyuinge fader moder doughter wyf anone forbode felawes neuer speke suche maner wordes presens nomore dede soo softenes honeste jacob hous amendyd moderaunce dyshoneste nycolas hous whiche hadde weddyd jacob doughter p ferthermore ye shall vnderstonde ye jacob vsed crafte makyng colour wherwyth wollen wolle clothes ben dyed crafte vsed bothe sonys contree ben called dyer wherfore full wonderfully god ordeyned dyer doughter shol made spouse emperour heuen ye shall see goddes grace boke somme haue shewed chapytre knowe parte cyte confessour sayd mayde katheryn moder many relygyous person seculers whiche neybours kynrede jacob wyf p byrthe merueylous werkinge whiche lord wrought shewed chylhode holy vyrgyn mayde capitulu ij whan forsayd lapa whiche lyke fructuous vyne fulfyllyng wyne jacob husbonde bryngyng forth full ofte bothe sone doughters befyll aboute laste tyme berynge chyldren ordynaunce dy sposycyon lordis mercy conceyued brought forth two doughters freell febyll nature moche freell bodely strengthe semed outward strengthe stabylnesse hadde syght god p whan lapa moder besely behelde theym thought well suffysed nought nourysshe bothe forthe wyth owne mylke wherfore good auysement commytted one smother noryse wythhelde kepte stylle norysshed forth wyth owne mylke soo befyll ordynaunce lorde chosed doughter owne kepyng whiche lord euerlastynge tyme hadde chose vnto spouse bothe resceyued grace baptysme nombre goddes chose chyldren yet forsayd mayde called katheryn called johan later suster whan hadde receiued grace baptysme grace went forth heuen short tyme passed worlde katheryne abode stylle sukkyng moders brestes goddes ordynaunce shold drawe heuen longe cheyn soulis moche lapa ye moder consyderyd katheryn abode deed nourysshed dyligently hopyng chose abyde goddes chyld ofte sythes moder lapa wolde saye maister reymond confessour holy mayde louyd katheryn passyngly aboue alle sone doughters euer hadde sayde vnto hym also conceyued soo ofte myght neuer nourysshe ony chylde wyth owne mylke p katheryn nourysshed forth ye ende tyme yt neded vnder nourysshe alle tyme conceyued semed oure lorde doughter hadde graunted tyme reste traueylyng byrthe chyldren token myght come ende conceyuyng byrthe doughter whiche sholde ateyne gete ende alle perfection p yet moder lapa nouryssyng katheryn one conceyued bare doughter whiche called johan made ende beryng chyldren hadde bo en xxv chyldren whan mayde thus broughte forth halowed god whan hadde lefte mylke toke ete brede whyle wente aboute alone began soo acceptable soo byloued tho sawe soo wyse wonderfull wordes spake vnnethes moder myght holde owne hous eche man aboute neybours kynrede lad home wyth theym glad myght haue wyse speche myght haue felawshyp gladenesse yonge mayde soo maner gladdenesse passyng solace called owne ryght name katheryn eufrosyna meued calle soo wyst theym self afterward somme tyme wolde saye suppose mystery cause purposed folowe saynt eufrosyne lyuyng confessour wrote legende supposed yonge mayde chyldis speche vsed somme maner sownynge nyghed acorded n eufrosyne soo maner wolde reherce wordes called soo name neuertheles euer appieryd burgenyd chilhode tree ony suche shewyng fruyt brought forth afterward olde age wysdome prudence speche connyng swetenesse holy conuersacion myght rehersed wyth tongue lygthly wryte wyth penne theym knewe veryte thys whiche hadde experyence hadde also inward werkynge whyche shewed well speche co uersacion wher thorugh many mennys sowlis drawe god hadde thorugh grace grete lykyng sauour god somoche heuynesses excluded mennys hertes whiche conuersaunt wyth thinges noyed sowle put awaye also remembraunce eche noye angwysshe take awaye folowed eche man soo grete reste stabylnesse sowle whiche hadde byfore euery man woundred theym self made joye wyth newe maner gladdenesse eche man owne sowle cryed sayde good v make thre tabernacle dwellyng place none wouder douiles hydde inuysybly breste spouse whiche transfygured hylle saynt peter sayde appostles p ferthermore purpos chosen mayde full tender age soone began waxe coforted wyth holy ghost token sholde soone fulfylled wyth dyuyne wysdome aboute age fyue yere whan taught saye salutacion aungell aue maria recordyd besely sayde full ofte whan coude saye enspired fro heuen began grete oure lady goyng vpward stayere comynge douward stayere eche grees stayere worshyppe lady wyth aue maria tolde confessour afterward secret esse confession ye maye e fyrst begynnynge shewed forth fyrst plesyng acceptable wordes men yonge age began stye vp thynges inuysyble p holy begynnyng encresed euery daye pleasyd lord vyse ed wyth gracyous wounderfull vysyon stere shewe hyr gyftes grace holy ghoost shewe lytyll plante shold brought forthe soo nourysshed tree cidre moyster holy gost p aboute age vj yere befyll chosen mayde wyth brother steuen somme elder wente suster bonauentura whiche suster made mencion byfore perauentur someuer ende loke ferde maner frendes kynrede soo doo whan hadde doo bode doo goyng homward agayn waye whiche called tongue wallis piacta holy may lyfte vp eyen agaynste ouer chirche freer prechours sawe ayer full fayre chambre ryally aparayed wyth ryches honeste oure lorde ihesu cryste trone imperyall clothed wyth pontyfycall vesture hauyng hede myter papall wyth hym saynt peter saynt poule saynt johan euan gelyst whan behelde alle thys fyrst stonyd vysement stably stode styll wyth louyngyng herte deuoutly loked sauyour bothe wyth bodely gostely eyen anone lorde drewe loue hym mercy fully sette e en mageste vpon graiously louyngly wyth manneuer smylyng chere reched ryght arme toward ouer gaue blessyng wyth token holy crosse maner bysshoppes prelate p grace gyfte god spedfull soo effectuously putte anon transformed rauysshed spyryte vnto oure lord whome sawe behylde wyth soo greate gostely lykynge gooyng waye mynde fully hadde forgoten selfe ofte wente waye besyde men bestes nature dredfull sholde chylde euer eyen hede vpward abydyng vppon blysfull vysyon none doughte soo wolde haue abyde hadde touched take awaye somme body longe vysyon endured p la e whyles thys shewed mayde steuen broder helde forthe waye passed greate space wenyng folowed hym whan tourned hym sawe folowe tourned agayn sawe suster fer e hynde stondyng styll waye loke vp fyrmament p thenne cryed wyth alowde voys called answerde take none hede thenne wente nere cryeng afterher voys helped p woundred wente thenne drewe honde sayde doost thou comest thou forthr anon cast doune lytyll eyen hadde awaked heuy slepe sayde yf thou sawe sawe thou woldest haue lette holy vysyon anone said wordes lyft vp eyen agayne holde vp hadde seen vysyon alle wythdrawe cesyd wyll whiche aperyd fore myght bere wythout sharpe stroke sorowe anone vengyd self wyth sore wepynge sorowe caste doune eyen tyme houre yonge mayde vyrgyn saint katheryn began waxe olde vertues sadnesse maners haue wounderfull witte felyng body bot e grace nature soo moche dedes chyldysshe ne yonge woman semed rather alle men came wysedom greate worshypfull age soo anone shewed fyre dyuyne loue kyndeled herte whiche vertu intellection made clere wyll feruent memorye comforted alle outward werkyng shewed alle thynges rewle goddes lawe p sayd confessyon hyrconfessour full mekely lowely lerned knewe tyme wyth techyng ony body ony redynge heryng onely nfusyon holy ghoose leuyng maners foly faders egypte lyuyng many sayntes specyally lyfe saynt domynyk p hadde soo grete desyre folowe lyuyng holy fadres sayntes myghte noo thynge ellys thynke howe myght come therto p cause many newe thynges beganne holy mayde hyr holy lyuyng dedes broughte men wonder tyme sought oute myght haue pryue place abyde preuely whanne wolde vse bodely afflyccyons whanne wolde occupye hyr prayer holy medytacyons p place certeyne tymes scourged hyr lytell tender body wyth lytell scourge lefte maner pleye dysportes besely gafe hyr prayer medytacyons full stylle gaf alle scylence euery day ageynste condy cyon chyldren lasse bodely mete toke thenne wonte fore wonte falle chyldren wexynge exemplum exsaumple thys yonge mayde many damse y dwellyng nye hyr age steryd god grace gadred hyr holy gracyous wordys power folowe hyr holy werkys thorugh fyll alle tho chyldren att certeyne tymes amen gyder preuy place hir hows dwellyd hadde chosen fore hyr self alle scour gyd hem selfe dyde eche sayde certeyne pater noster aue maria katheryne bad h saye p alle werkyngee tokenys gretter meruaylles sholde folowe p hyr moder tolde full ofte mayster reymond p whan asked hyr myghte denye hyt full ofte goyng vpward dounward grees hyr faders hows vysybly alle syghte sawe hyr swyf ly wente ayre touched noo grees wyth fete thys fylle namely whanne wolde flee waye oute companye specyally syghte companye men moche gretely kynge begynnyng say hyr aue maria grete lady ther wyth goynge vp doune hyr faders grees therfore suppose thys myracle shewed rather thanne another place p forthermore moche knowynge lyfe holy faders egypte reuelacyon therfore wyth alle strengthes steryd gretely folow hem p moche ye yong tender age full feruentely desyred wyldernesse holy faders olde tyme myghte thynke hyr maner waye myght perfourme hyr desyre cause ordeyned god sholde dwell soo solytary place oure lorde suffred hyr stonde wytte hir proper nature myght nomore knowe sholde doo touchyng purpose hyr owne chyldes wytte wolde shewe hyr ryght befyll wyth hyr feruent wyll purpose ouercame tendrenesse frealte hyr age yet hadde parfyte vyctorye erly morowty de thought go deserte ellys wyldernesse abyde solytary place wherefor chyldys prouydence purueyed lofe brede forthe wente toward hyr susters hows wedded whyche hows faste gate clepyd gate saynt ansanye passyd hyr sustrer hows forthe wente gate dyd neuer afore soo passyd forthe tyll came waye cyte saw noo hows stonde nyghe dyde cyte thenne thought wel nyghe deserte yet wente somwhat forther laste founde lytel caue vnder banke whyche plesyd hyr well forth wente glad herte wenyng hyr hadde fonde wyldernesse whyche hadde desyred yet lorde almyghty god whome behelde long fore receyned hys holy blyssyng whyche gladly acceptyth holy desyres alle lord hadde dysposed hys spouse haue manere lyuyng yet wolde suffre dede dyde good desyre passe awaye wyth token sheweher dyd acceptable plesyng hym anone began praye feruently lyfte vp lytell lytell erthe body wente vp hyghe height caue wolde suffre stode prayer fro morow none thys mayde perceyued welle areryd erthe tyme wende ben wor hyng hyr enemye whyche wold wyth hys fraudes dysceytes lette hyr prayer desyre deserte cause besyed hir enforced hyr stablye feruently praye laste aboute houre day whan lord passy crosse take doun fro crosse descendyd lytell lytell ascendyd inspyracion lord hadde vnderstondyng knowyng tyme yet come sholde putte hyr body suche afflyccyon lorde ne sholde leue faders hows suche maner wherefor torned came whan wente sawe allone behelde gate cytee longe full fe age feblynesse dredynge also hyr fader moder shold wene loste coude beganne praye commytted hyr fully god anone shorte whyle ordynaunce myght lorde borne vp eyre sette gate cytee wyth ony harme anone wente home alle hast myght coude thys tolde cosyne here whyche callyd laxa hyr fader moder alle thys hydde vnknowen tyll came elder age wende hadde come fro hyr susters hows wedded thys shewed thys chapytre somme partye lapa hir moder tolde mayster reymond whyche hyr last confessoure somme partye self somme laxa hyr cosyne wythstondyng hadde grete swetenesse alle wrytton sayd fore saue laste bothe hyr fyrst confessour whyche nourysshed hyr faders hows many worshypfull trewe matro neyghbours nyghe besyde nygh hyr fader moder hyr p hyr vowe made virgynyte vertuous liuynge meruaylles whyche fyll tyll came age abylytee wedded man wedded ne neuer wolde capitulu iij moche vertue grace vysyon whyche rehersyd nexte hapytle fore worldly loue affeccyon wyth drawen herte thys holy yonge mayde onely holy loue goddys sone gloryous mayde moder lord ihesu cryste stylly stedfastly prented hyr herte wherfore sette alle thynge noughte soo myght ouely wynne lord hyr sauyour anone clere vnderstondyng techyng holy ghoost full semyng accordyng lorde maker nought serued wyth alle purytee lenues bothe body sowle wherfore desyred fully haue kepe clennesse virgynytee thought well knowynge hyr techynge god blessyd lady goddys moder fyrste founde lyf virgynytee wherefor thys mayde conceyued hyr herte vp mater wolde haue recourse lady helpe counseyll whan came seuen yere age took grete auysemente though hadde sadnesse xx yere age contynuelly prayed lady quene aungels virgynes wolde wouchesauf helpe hyr gete hyr lord parfyte waye techynge holy ghoost myght doo moost plesynge god moste spedefulle helthe hyr sowle eche prayer euer shewed hyr desyre lady sore desyred lyue aungelslyf lyf virgynytee alle thys tyme loue euerlastyng spouse feruent fro day day thys maydens herte whyche loue steryd alle hyr sowle wyth oute ony cessyng vnto heuenly liuynge whan thys wyse mayde sawe feruent spyryte desyre cause wolde quenche spiryte whiche freely gracyously hadde graunted asked hote kyndelyng desyre vpon day thanne chose hyr preuy place noo body myght hyr myght speke alle lowde wyth hygh voys euer wolde saye wyth lownesse body sowle thus spak lady sayde moost blyssedfull lady moost holy vitgyne whyche fyrste amonge alle wymmen thou halowedest euer thy virgynytee lord wyth makyng hym vowe whome thou made moder hys onely sone thy pyte whyche may spoke ne tolde tongue lowely beseche praye none merytes notwythstondyng myn vnworthynesse wouches auf gracyous lady moche grace thou spouse hym onely whome desyred wyth strengthes sowle thyn holy sone lord ihesu cryste make hym fulle promysse shall neuer take spouse shall kepe hym virgynyte vndefowled myghte poure loo maydens rede thys loo vere ye may se ordynatly alle yeftes vertuous werkyng dedys thys holy mayde dysposed ordeyned euerlastyng wysdome whyche myghtely dysposeth alle thynges softnes age syy yere sawe hir spouse wyth hyr bodely eye took hym hys blyssynge age seuen yere made vowe virgynyte taketh hede also auysement ordre kepte makyng hyr auowe p fyrste desyred askyd haue hym hyr spouse whome hyr sowle louyd desyre askyng forsoke euery maner spouse behotyng hym trouth feyth euer lastynge thys petycyon myght denyed taketh hede also whome prayeth prayed prayeth fyrste prayeth lady whyche hath properly inacte lyberalytee fredome alle grace euer graunte yeue grace man neuer fowle synne holdeth hyr selfe dettour alle bothe wyse vnwyse despyseth none opened hande eche man hath nede stretched hyr pawmes eche poure man sheweth hyr self folke well neuer faylled sholde gracyous lady lytell mayde innocent feruent whyche puttyth awaye hyr grace synfull men woman elder age sholde gloryous lady receyue purpose virgynyte holy mayde whyche gracyously fyrste amonge men founde holy clene lif virgynytee sholde mercyfull pyteuous lady denye thys lytell mayde hyr sone whyche drewe hym heuen erthe sholde gyue alle belyued hym ye haue seen thys mayde prayed sithe praye thou prayed askyd whiche self taughte aske whyche asked sought whyche byddeth alle men seke shall sought hym self shalle sought may put awaye ne put petycyon suche thynge must nedys haue grau te lordes promyse sayde askyth ye shall haue speketh ye shall fynde sayde also another place fyrste sekyth kyngdome god hys ryghtwysnesse therefore whanne thys mayde besely sought soo tymely tender chyldys age sone god whyche hym selfe kyngdome god manere myght sholde fynde soughte haue askyd ferthermore seeth manere prayed asked desyred ye shalle clerely see hyr prayer myghte doon awaye ne voydyd dysposed hyr selfe receyue askyd onely tyme alle tyme come remeuyd alle hyr obstacle clothed hyr wyth plesable clothynge pouerte hym euer whome askyd hyr desyre bonde hyrself oblysshed hyr wyth solempne vowe fore god soo straytely restrayned hyr selfe neuer world ne fende sholde lette hyr dysposycyon alle thys tyme ther faylled hyr condycyons whyche prayer sholde haue prayer muste nede herde asked hyr self asked fulle mekely helthefull alle helthe feythfully stood stedfastely represente hyr perseuerau ce made perpetuell vowe remeuyd alle shold obstacle hyr petycyon may ye sekerly conclude nedys moste herde lord thynketh thenne sekerly asked soo resceyued lorde took hyr lorde hyr loue hyr euerlastyng spouse hys blysfulle moder desyred bi helpe gloryous lady coupled euer hyr dere sone perpetuell vowe virgynyte shall proued wyth helpe lord clere token last chapytre fyrst partye ferthyrmore ye shall knowe thys vowe thys mayde began euery day wexe holy holy tender age began take batayll wyth hyr flesshe whyche yet began neuer rebell purposed take waye hyr flesshe flesshly mete moche myghte wherfore whanne flesshe leyde hyr fylle ofte eyther leyde stephen hyr brothyr preuely lytyll lytyll voyded body sholde perceyue contynued alwaye hyr dysplyens whyche spake fore encresed hem sharpely eyther allone hyr self wyth yonge maydens also grete wele othyr sowles helthe began kyndelyd hyr wonderfull suche chyldes herte syngulerly loued tho sayntes whiche laboured specyally boute helthe mannes sowle hadde also knowyng onely techynge god saynt domynyk ordeyned ordre frere prechours loue feythe holy chyrche helthe mannes sowle wherfore ordre moche reuerence whan sawe frerys ordre passyng forth waye hir faders se marked wel wente passyd fulle mekely deuoutely kyssed steppe theyr fete tyme forward wext grete desyre hyr sowle go vnto ordre myght profyte man ne sowle wyth brethern ordre cause sawe grete obstacle woman therfore thought folowe saynt eufrosyen clepyd hir childhode woderfully pronostycacion ryght saynt eufrosyen feyned hyr man went monastery monkes manere thys mayde purposed seyne hyr man go ferre contree knowe take abyte ordre frere prechours myght helpe sowles saue perysshyng yet wytfstondyng thought purpose abode longe hyr mynde lord suffred thought perfourmed dedene brought execucyon ye loue put hyr mynde another ende lord wolde also another maner fulfyll hyr desyre thys tyme thys mayde wexte fast body encreced age moche hyr sowle encreced vertue mekenes wext fast deuocyon encreced feyth clere hope gretely strengthed charyte multyplyed hyr feruour thys vertues gendryd vertuous worshypfull sadnes maneres relygyous putte syght al men whyche consydered hyr dedys fader moder astonyed brethern susteren wondred gretely alle meyne hyr faders hows meruaylled beholdyng perceyuynge soo hygh wysdome soo tendyr age amonge many notable wyse wordes dedys one wylle shewe comendacyon mayde p hyt befylle tyme seuen yere fore ten yere age deuocyon hyr moder hadde saynt anthonye wolde haue masse sayde worshyppe saynt wherefor clepyd katheryne hir doughter took hyr certeyne candelles certeyne syluer sayde goo doughter parysshe chyrche praye oure parysshe preest syng synge masse worshyp saynte anthonye offer thyse candelles thys money vp awtre p thys mayde gladde doo alle thynge myght torne worshyp god anone wente chyrche performed hyr moders byddyng deuocyon hadde masse abode stylle ende masse whan alle wente home ageyn hyr moder wende wolde comen anone ageyn anone made oblacyon preest p moche doughter taryed longe hir semyng whan sawe come thought blame hyr doughter sayd cursyd wycked togues sayd thou sholdeste nomore come ageyne thys manere somme men saye langage name taryed longe thys mayde thenne grete wysdome herde hyr moder sayde helde hyr stylle whyle spake noo worde ageyne good space thys mayde drewe hir modre fyde wyth grete sadnes hyr mekely spak hir modre seyde p lady modre euer trespas agast youre biddyng bete ye wyth rodde thynketh best ware another time worthy ryght full ye thyng praye defautes curseth neuer good man ne badde semyng degree full grete affliccion herte hyr modre herde wordys sche wondrid gretely merueill lytill doughter teche wysely enforme hir somoche hadde spirite blame hyr tyme wysdom sawe yonge alitill thynge neuer le wolde hyr doughter hadde knowe therfor suwhat thoughte speke ageyne turned hir doughter seyde longe doughter seyde mekely ageyne modre herde masse yebadde goo whan doone turned home ageyn wythout ony tarieng abode nowhere till come home ageyne thoo modre tho wordis edyfyed fore went hyr husbonde seyd thus thus hath thi yonge doughter spoke good man gafthankynges god bare stylle priuely hys herte seyde noughte ageyne loo ye maydens rede thys book thys oo poynt yt one leste yet mowe ye wele perceyue lorde encreceth hys grace weye thys yonge mayde till come ye yeres abilitee weddyd whyche yeres ye shalle see next chapytre thys chapitre make ende p yet ye shall vnderstonde thyse conteyned thys chapytre mayde partye somme hadde modre dwellyng hyr fadres hows whyse age p hyr feruente deuocyon drawe whyche lord suffred encrece grace folowyng hyr stronge pacyence wyth whyche pacyens suffred hir fadres hows many iniuryes capituluqrtu wonderfull vertuous cours lyuyng fyrst yeres thys maydens tender age lordes wyll somme lyghte defaute suffre hyr fall suffred fulle ofte somme hys holy sayntes entent sholde myghtely aryse vp ageyne lyue warly strenght hem atteyne ryght waye heythe perfeccyon gloryously haue vyctorye fende whyche euer enemye mannes sowle p wordes saye whanne came age yeres abylyte wedded saye twelthe yere hyr age lytel thenne manere contree abode styll home came hyr fadres hows fader moder thenne hyr frendes kynne cause knewe may den purpose bethought hem besyed hem seke aboute thys mayden myght worshypfully parfy tably wedded prosone hyr moder supposed grete wysdome hyr doughter sholde haue wedded somme man grete kyneede besyed hir fast aboute bodely apparayll araye hyr doughter taught hyr wasshe ofte hyr face kembe ofte hyr hede make hyr fayre voyde alle thynge sholde dyshoneste sholde make foule hyr face hyr necke whan ony man came aske hyr maryage sholde semely fayrer thys holy mayde alle another purpose made another vowe alle shewed hyr fader ne moder wherfor vtterly thoughte noo thynge hyr moder bad hyr touchyng suche curyosyte besyed wyth alle hyr strengthes plese god man wyse whanne hyr moder hadde aspyed wylle maner lyuynge dysplesed clepyd hyr bonauenture hyr doughter whyche late wedded bad hyr trete soo hir suster myght araye hyr bodely apparayll manere wymen contre sholde maryed doo hadde bad hyr doo fore hyr moder knewe welle katheryne loued bonauenture fulle tenderly supposed sholde broughte lyghtely hyr suggestyons thanne ony soo ye shalle see suffraunce oure lorde broughte inne thorough speche example hyr suster bonauenture many maner wayes laste assentyd hyr besynesse apparaylle hyr body wylle hyr moder wythstondynge stably kepte hyr purpose neuer haue husbonde grau te hyr sustre folowed hyr wylle suche araye maad soo moche sorowe whanne confessyd therof wyth terys sobbyng eche body shold suppose hadde somme greuous synne vsed ofte confessyd generally alway wha came ye poynt accused selfe full harde wyth wepyng sore sobbyng confessour alle knewe vertue god lowely sowles see self defaute none lytyll semeth hym full grete neuerthelesse asmoche accused self demed worthy euerlastynge payne synne sauyng mercy god asked whether purposed wylled tyme agaynst vowe sayde nay came neuer herte also asked agayne whether dyde plesaunce ony man speciall plesaunce men answerd sayde ther none somoche payne holde men seyne men men shold fynde wherfore faders men yt lerned dyer crafte faders hous came ony place chambre fledde faste awaye adder hadde come soo men wondred wold neuer goo wyndowe ne dore hows see men wente waye thene sayd deserued ye dede whiche bodely ornamente euerlastyng payne namely whan apparelle excessyuely answerd sayde excessyuely loued suster thought tha god tyme wherfore wepte wythout remedye dyd harde penau ce confessour wold haue replyed agayne sayde alle bee ther somme maner excesse loue lytyll dede self doo noo wycked euyl entencion vayne plesaunce tyme agaynste precepte god herde confessour replyed lyft vp eyen god wyth lowde voys cryed sayde lorde god ghostely fader haue nowe whiche excuseth synnes wyth sore grutchynge agaynst self tourned confessour sayde fader thynke ye wretchedfull mooste vnworthy creature god whiche hath receyued maker nought soo many gracyous yeftes wythout labour wythouten ony meryte shold occupye ony tyme arraye vayne apparelle roten flesshe whiche myght induce dedely synne wene sayde helle suffyseth punysshe hadde pyte god doo gracyously mercyfull wyth thyse wordes confessour durst nomore speke mater besyed knowe yf blessyd sowle euer lyf kept wythouten ony spot e dedely synne soo hadde kepte fully hole vyrgynyte body sowle synne flesshely steryng also alle maner synne p knewe vertuous clene sowle hadde wytnesse recorde bare conuersacion sayd wrote coude neuer perceyue ne fynde nother generall confessyon ne speciall confessyon ofte euer confessyd ryght ofte hadde offendyd agaynst precepte lorde yf tolde afore whiche myght suppose agaynste byddynge god ne trowed none dyscrete man wold suppose also sayde founde euer soo clene fro venyall synnes vnnethe coude perceyue bi cotydyan confessyon ony maner offe ce openly knowen confessours knewe conscyence conuersaunt neuer seldon offended worde eyther occupyed tyme prayer contemplacion elli good edyficacion neyghbours tyme slepyng vnnethes wolde grauute quarter houre whan sholde ete mete yet may called mete euer prayed thought holy medytacyons thynkyng thynges hadde lerned lord sowle confessyon mayster reymound bereth trewe recorde tyme yt knewe hadde cure conscience payne ete mete hungry man wythdrawe hys mete grete tourmente body tyme hadde ete comely fenerous man rennyng offhis feuer one cause wolde ete mete shall declared wythin forthe tourmente put payne body maner trespaas myght suche sowle occupyed alwaye occupyed soo wyth lord god yet wythstondyng suche good occupacions accused self soo sharpely confession soo wyttyngly put selfe trespaas offense yf hee cofessour hadde knowe conuersacyon myght haue supposed hadde trespased trespased rather deseruyd mede loo ye maydens heren reden boke alle processe thynge ellys sayde ye perceyuen lytyll defaute whyche holy mayde yelde self soo mekely gylty ye maye vnderstonde therby per feccyon sheweth therafter gracyous yefte lorde whiche confessour reherseth wyse bonauentura ryght besy afore araye holy mayde worlde asketh ryght soo eftsones besyed enduce suche araye counseyll apparaylle myght noo wyse inclyne may den herte nother generall nother specy sholde shewe bodely presence wylfully syghte man entent oonly sholde desyred soner wedded though feruour prayer swetenesse medytacio slaked wythdrewe tyme att laste oure lorde wolde lenger suffre hys spouse whiche soo specyally chosen sholde withdrawe taryed hys speciall seruyce wythdrewe wyse tyme whan bonauentura suster holy mayde sholde brynge forthe chylde yet yonge nough age bere chyldren take hede maydens therfore see thys oure lorde displesed wyth theym ben aboute lette wythdrawe theym wolde serue hym specially maydenhode chastyte lyuynge thys bonauentura rehersyd alwaye full honeste maner lyuyng bothe worde dede cause besyed drawe suster wordly thynges whiche desyred serue lorde specyally smyten hym punysshed wyth full sharpe deth neuerthelesse lord yet wrought full mercyably wyth hyr shewed afterward reuelacyon thys holy mayde purgatory suffred many greuous paynes prayer hir delyuered payne restored blysse shewed afterward preuely hyr confessour p whanne hyr suster bonauenture passyd thys worlde thanne thys blessyd mayde katheryn clerely perceyued vanyte thys worlde ganne feruentely gredylye trewely torned louely ghostly clyppyng hyr endeles spouse jhesu cryste claymyng accusynge hyr self gylty wyth marye magdalene fallyng doune full streyte fete oure lorde plenteuously shedyng terys axynge inwardly hys mercy praynge thynkyng vncessably hyr synnes myght deserue hyr wyth marye magdalene wordes confort lorde sayde marye thus p remittutur tibi peccata tua p saye doughter thy synnes foryeue beganne haue synguler affeccyon mary magdalene thanne tyme enforsed hyrself wyth alle hyr myghtys conferme hyr marye magdalene haue grace forgyuenes hyr synnes therfore afterward encrece deuocyon thys folow therof lord god spouse holy sowles hys blessyd moder lady saynt marye gaue mary magdalene thys blyssyd mayde maystresse moder shall declared openly wyth inne forth helpe jhesu p thys fende enemye alle mankynde sorowyng thus pray wythdrawe delyuerd alle hole hys power whyche lytell lytell enforced drawe hym also consyderynge thys holy mayde encreced renne quyckely tabernacle mercy hyr spouse jhesu thought felly wylely lette hyr hyr ghostly purpose meyne hyr faders howsholde besyeng hym aduercytees persecucyons drawe hyr holy worlde sholde occupyed suche ghostly excercyse puttyng mynde hir fader moder also hyr brethern alle wyse sholde wedded myght hyr mene purchace somme manere kynrede aboute thys besynesse fende enduced hem hyely asmoche one hyr doughters passyd thys world sholde aboute recouer harme hyr dede hyr lyue ferforth aboute seke husbonde thys holy mayde p whan thys mayde perceyued consydered wyles hyr ghostly enemye inspyracyon lord jhesu none myghtely besyly contynued prayer medytacyon excercyses penaunce haue grace flee conuersacyon men soo shewed open tokenys hyr frendes noo wyse purpose wedded dedely ne corruptyble spouse syth taken gracyously hyr spouse hir yonge tender age vndedely kyng endeles blysse whanne fader moder kynne perceyued veryly thys holy may de shewed perseuerautly bothe token worde wylled neuer wedded none erthely man thought bowe hyr herte nother mene consente theyr purpose callyd frende therys frere prechour whyche loued specyally prayed hym entyrly wolde goo counseyll holy mayde sholde consente wylle whome frere answerde sayde wolde myght whan came thys mayde communycacyon founde hyr stedfast purpose maydenhode conscience enduced gyue hyr holsum counseylle sayde syth thou arte dysposed serue lorde god maydenhede ageynst whyche purpose thy frendes ben aboute lette shewe stedfastnesse thyn holy purpose cutte waye alle thyn thy hede peraduenture wold cesse pursuyte soone thys blessyd mayde herdethys hys counseyll wrought though hadde herde god took peyre sherys anone cutte awaye hir herys whiche supposed synned greuously hated moche cutte awaye ryght gladly fast de whanne couerd hyr hede wyth coyf wente forthe alle ageynst comyn custome maydens worlde wyth kerchyf hyr hede ye doctryne saynt powle whan hyr moder lapa aspyed thys hyr doughter katheryn vsed thus couer hyr hede customably asked hyr dyd thys mayden gaf none clere answer cause wolde nethyr lye ne telle trouthe wyth moder wente thys maydens hede took hyr kerchyfe wyth hyr owne hondys ceyued yt hyr cut awaey thane moder sorowfull hyr herte bycause hyr fayre cutte awaye waylynge cryenge thys wyse aa doughter haste thou doo anone mayde keuered hyr hede efte sone wente syde crye moder came bothe fader chyldren meruayllyng myght whanne knewe cau hyr cryeng hugely ameuyd ageynste maide whiche trouble begonne secounde bataylle ageynst mayde sharper thene fyrst yet thys mayden lord gaff vyctorye thoo thynges whyche semed lettyng hyr holy purpose hyr grete helpe meruayllously knytte hyr lord myghtely therefore pursued hyr openly rebukyng hyr thretyng hyr worde dede sayeng thus thou wretched creature trowest thou escape thus thou shalt fulfyll wylle thou hast cutte awaye thyn hyt shall growe ageyn wyll thou nyll thou though thyn herte sholde breste yet shalt yu haue husbonde thou shalt neuer haue reste vnto tyme thou haste consented wylle wyth made ordynaunce katheryne shold nomore haue pryue chambre hir self dwelle inne sholde openly occupyed comyn seruyce hows place tyme prayeng vnyeng knyttyng jhesu hir spoufe sholde vtterly wyth drawe hir also shold see hyr self moche despyte made comyn seruaunte thys ordynaunce thys holy mayde putte alle manere fylthe besynesse fowle kechyn suffryng euery day repreues euery day also wronges rebukyng dyspytable wordes multeplyed ageynst hyr moste alle ouercomen wymmenys hertys hyt supposed hyr fader hyr moder brethern hadden fonde yong man who kynrede gretely well apayde therefor steryd inpugnyd hyr sharpely myght sonner bowed theyr consent oure ghostly enemye fende who wyckednes tretcherous werkes thyse thynges wrought doune wende wyth drawe thys mayde hyr clene purpose helpe god made moost strengest noo wyse meuyd ne stered alle doone hyr made hyr pryue chaumbre helpe holy ghoost hyr owne sowle fro whyche pryue chaumbre made ordynaunce hyr self neuer go manere besynesse done dede whyche fyrste hadde outward chaumbre assygned hyr somtyme stood wyth somtyme wente oute afterwarde whan made hyr selue hyr sowle pryue chaumbre myght take hyr creature erthe went neuer thes ben tho heuenly vyctoryes may taken awaye fro crystis specyall erthe ouercomynge wyth ony doubte alle stylly enemyes holy wrytte seyth regnum dei infra no est saye kyngdome heuen wythin v also prophete dauyd seyth ioye lordes doughter wythin forthe wythin v wyth ony doubte clere vnderstondyng fr wylle retentyf mynde wythin v also gracyous infusyon holy ghoost whiche maketh perfyte ghoostly myghtys rehersed afore ouercometh throweth vnder foot alle outward aduersytres wythin v yf ben trewe vylners vertue dwelleth ghest whyche sayde seyth confidite ego vici mundum trusteth feythfully ye shall ouercome enemyes haue ouercome worlde grete enemye blessyd lord thys holy mayde katheryn trustyd hyghely made hir wyth inne hyr self chambre hys helpe who loue charged lese chambre made mannes handes wythout forth p one thynge shall saye mayster reymond confes sour thys holy mayde beryth recorde whan sholde walke outward cause whyle grete outward besynesse occupacyon nedys must done thys holy mayde oftymes warned hym sayde shold make wythin hys sowle pryuee celle whyche pryue cell sholde neuer goo alle vnderstonde hyr ouerly lyghtely yet neuerthelesse afterwarde whan consydered wyttely hyr wordes wordes saynt johan sayde gospell felle hys mynde rehersed crystys dyscyples thys wyse hoe autem non cognouerunt discipuli eius primum sed quando glorificatus est ihesus tune recordatisunt crystys dyscyples knewe alle thynge hym touchyng hys passyon fyrst onely tyme whan reysen fro deth lyue gloryfyed thanne knewe openly clerely soo manere wyse bothe mayster reymond hyr confes sour tho conuersaunt wyth hyr happyd meruayllously perceyued openly clerely bothe dedys hyr wordes afterwarde whenne wyth hyr presently p yette shall telle another holy conseyt blessyd ymagynacyon thys holy mayde holy ghoost taught hyr whyche ouercome alle wronges despytes tolde pryuely hyr confessour axyng hym mekely myght perfytly gladde amonge soo many despytes thanne brake sayde hadde suche ymagynacyon hyr self hyr fader represented lorde ihesu cryste oure sauyour hyr moder oure blessyd lady saynt marye hyr brethern many housholde betokeneth holy appostles oure lorde dyscyples hys thys blessyd ymagynacyon serued hem alle gladdely soo alle meruaylled therof thys blessyd ymagynacyon wan another grete profyte oftr serued made mynystracy euer hadde mynde hyr hyr spouse ihesu cryste whome hyr thought serued soo beyng bodely kechyn alle waye wyth holy place callyd sanctum sancto rum ofte serued atte mete soo ofte fedde hyr sowle wyth presence oure sauyour hyghe rychesse endeles counseyll many dyuers meruayllous wayes delyuerest trusten alle maner dy bryngest hauen endeles reste delyueryng bothe pytte swolowe whan alle thys done thys holy mayde consyderynge euyr hyr sowle ye mede rewarde ordeyned hyr holy ghoost suffred gladly nought paynfully alle wronges putte hyr also encreced contynually cours hyr labour myght haue full ioye hyr sowle cause suffred hyr haue chambre hyr self haue hyr chambre openly hadde p therefore holy uysement chose chambre stephen hyr brother hadde nether wyf ne chyldren dayes tyme whanne absente myght allone nyghtes tyme whan slepte prayed hyr desyre soo nyght daye soughte see face hyr spouse ihesu cryste knockyng dore hys ghoos ly tabernacle wyth cessyng prayed lord vncessably wolde wouche sauf keper hyr virgynytee sayeng syngyng sowle wyth saynt cecylye thys holy verse dauyd prophete fiat cor meum domine et corpus meum immaculatum lorde ihesu praye myn herte body kepte clene vnderfowled soo scylence hope made stronge lord ryght meruayllously torment persecucyon hadde wyth forth fulfylled wyth ghoostly ioyes wythin forth soo ferforth hyr brethern perceyueng hir stedfastnesse sayden betwyne seluen thus ouer come hyr fader innocente alle consyderyng pryuely hyr dedes perceyued ladde euery daye holy ghoost nought lyghtnes yonthe alle thyse ben rehersed thys chapytre hyr confessour mayster reymond reuelacyon lapa thys maydens moder lyxa brother wyf also hyr faders hows thynges folke myght knowe knewe tellyng thys holy mayde confessyon p vyctorye whyche hadde desesed hyr culuer whiche hyr fader sawe vysyon ynt domynyk ca v mene whyle thys holy mayde putte suche reproue shame happyd vp daye entred chambre hyr yonge brother stephen prayed deuoutly leuyng dore vnshett forboden hyr hyr fader moder sholde shette dore casuelly thenne happened fader entred chambre sekynge certeyne thynge hys sone nede loked aboute sawe hys doughter goddes doughter thanne hys prayng corner knelyng lytell whyte culuer restynge vp hyr hede whyche culuer fledde chambre wyndowe whan fader entred chabre thought anone fader axed doughter culuer myght fledde chambre doughter answerd sayde neuer sawe culuer ne byrde chambre thenne hadde fader grete meruaylle kepte thyse wordes pryuely hys herte fro tyme forwarde beganne gracyously encrece holy maydens sowle holy desyre whyche neuerthelesse begonne reherced fore hyr chyldehode afterward renewyd tuycyon dysease kepyng hyr maydenhode virgynytee desyre thynge ellys receyue habyte ordre frere prechours whyche ordre saynt domynyk bothe foundour fader prayed bothe daye nyght lord wouchesauf fulfyll hyr desyre therto grete deuocyon saynt domynyk rehersed fore worthy fruytfull louer sowles almyghty god therefor sawe wysely myghtely hys doughter yong knyght faught batayll wyth feruour deuocyon besyed hyr plese hym wyth alle hyr desyre wolde wyse dysceyue hyr ne defraude hyr hyr holy purpose sekernesse comforted hyr wyth suche vysyon p holy mayde tyme vysyon hir slepe sawe many holy faders many dyuers foudours ye ordre ye frere prechours amonges saw saynt dominyk knewe wel holdyng hys honde fayre whyte lylye whyche lylye semyng hir fyre ye busshe yt moyses saw yet brennyd whan holy faders al general eche speciall gaf hir couseyll hir mede yt shold chese oo relygion ordynauce ye whiche relygion myght yelde due seruyce god torned hir self hole saynt dominik saw spyryt yt ye holy fader saynt dominyk came hir brought honde habyte sustris whyche susters ben called sustres penaunce saynt domynyk ye whiche susters ther ne yet lytell nobre ye cyte senee whan thys holy fader saynt domynyk cam mayde coforted hir suche wordes sayde dought good cofort drede manere peryll ryght yu hast desyred habyte thought receyued thankyd almyghty god worthy confessour saynt domynyke wyth lytyll gladnesse wyth ioyefull teres soo perfyghtely hadde co forted soo wyth wepyng awoke restoryd bodely wyttes p whan awaked caught comforte bodely strength vysyon toke soo grete boldenes truste hadde lorde daye called fader moder bretheren togyders sayde theym boldely wyse somtyme ye sayde vnto tretyd longe tyme therof sholde bee wedded corruptyble dedely man though hadde abhomynacion suche weddyng myn herte ye myght clerly perceyue many dyuerse tokenes ye hadde wolde yet reuerence sholde shewe fader moder bydyng god vnto tyme excused neuer clerly cause may noo lenger styl shall declare openly myn herte purpoos whiche purpoos conceyued newe chyldhode vnto tyme therfore wyl ye knowe myn chyldhode made avowe virgynyte serue oure lorde sauyour alle worlde blessyd moder gloryous vyrgyn marie gloryous lady chyldely wyth sa longe avysement grete cause made avowe also shold neuer take husbond hym alone therfore syth come sufferaunce oure lord perfyght age knowleche vnderston dyng wytte wete ye ryght well purpoos whiche soo myghty stroonge myn sowle possyble hard flynt stone rather made nesshed myn herte shold wythdrawe fro holy pnrpos therfore ye laboure aboute thys thynge tyme ye lese wherfore counseyll ye leue alle maner suche tretyng weddynge touchyng myn persone therin shall neuer fulfylle wyll cause sholde rather obedyent god man therfore yf ye wylle haue suche one hous serue god purpoos commyn seruaunt serue redy may doo seruyce gladly yf ye wylle receyue cause ye wylle putt hous doo well wete noo wyse myn herte may wythdrawe fro holy purpos p haue husbond spouse cryste jhesu soo rychely soo myghtely yt wyll suffre noo wyse lacke thyng wyll mynystre nedeth whan hadde sayde alle thyse wordes alle herde speke fyll wepyng cause plentnously syghynge sobbynge myght time gyue none answer consyderid holy purpos thys holy mayde ye whyche myght wyth saye ne wythstonde behylde also styll mayden kepte clene pure vnto yt tyme bodely declared consciens wordes grete prudence also ouer sawe openli rather diposed forsake faders hous breke holy purpoos soo hadde nomore truste weddyng wherfore lyked theym better wepe gyue answer wythin lytyll whyle whan hadde cesyd wepynge fader yt loued soo tenderly dredde god dred god soo hyghely hadde mynde coluer sawe many good dedes whiche vsed whiche dedes gretely merueylyng gaue suche answere sayde dere doughter god forbede sholde ony thynge wylle desyre agaynste wyll god whiche wyll fro whiche wyll knowe well thys holy purpoos cometh fro therefore soo ben taught longe experyence openly see thou art steryd herto lyghtenesse chyldhode feruent charyte god make thy vowe therfore frely doo lyketh holy ghoost techeth p fro tyme forward shall neuer lette thyn holy purpoosne thyne ghostely excercise praye v besely maye bee made worthy promys byheste thyn ghoostely spouse thou haste chose specyall grace thyn tender age p thenne tourned hym hys wyf chyldren sayde none tyme forward ne dere donghter greuous none soo hardy tyme forward let ony wyse suffer serue spouse freely praye v sely myght neuer haue founde better husbond thenne whiche vochesauf nere kynde wedde doughter haue wyf therfore haue none cause pfayne v sythe soo haue receyued dedely man vndedely god man spouse p whan fader hadde sayde thyse wordes wyth wepynge wyth weylyng bothe theym selfe also herde theym hym speke namely ye moder louyd mayde maner flesshely thene holy maide katheryn ioyefully thanked oure lorde brought vyctorye also fader moder wyth alle maner lowenes dysposyng self vse profytably lycence grau ted ende chapytre p wylle ye knowen redyn heren booke mayster reymound confessour holy mayde knewe neuer reuelacion fader sawe coluer whiche restyd blessyd maydens hede fader deed tha mayster reymoud knewe blessyd mayde knewe reuelacio cosyns dwellyd faders hous whiche cosins recorded bare wytnes fader sawe suche culuer wyth ofte tymes therfore hadde greate reuerence wold noo wyse hadde lettyd troublyd p vysyon sawe saynt domynyk bothe mayster reymound confessour afore hym knewe tellyng holy mayde whan mayster reymound examyned ye wordes sayde laste fader moder brederen byhad pesecucions tolde hym alle ordre mekely p hardenesse bodely penau ce afflyction persecucion fuffred therfore moder capitulu vj whan deuoute mayde hadde receyued large lycence graunted longe tyme desyred afore beganne ryght quyckely dyspose merueylously alle lyf seruyse god p att begynnyng asked haue lytyll chambre self de wherin purposed tourmente body wyth penaunce wyldernesse myght haue fredome sowle serue lord moche harde penaunce vsed tourmentyng body grete loue hadde seyng hyr spouse lytyll chambre maye noo tongue suffre telle neuertheles haue rehersed som generall grete penaunce purpose telle maydens speciall vnder fewe wordes hardnesse penaunce soo ye grete vertuous herbes holy lyuyng maye taste somwhat fruyte growen aboute herber bothe fyrst laste condycions kyndis fruyt shall declared helpe god afterward cause place rehersyd fruyte full vertuous lyuing nothynge ellys maydens sholde able redyer ghostely excercyse lytyll cha bre graunted ofte tymes consydered swetely ghostely werkis old faders egypte ghostely werkys soo moche merueylous hadde trewe knowleche therof faders hous wythout ensample doctryne fyrst shall telle abstinence mete drynke fro chyldehood tyme came age ete full seldom flesshe rehersed afore whan come age speciall fredom forsoke vtterly etyng flesshe soo fer forthe belonge custome vse hadde forsakyng lyght payne smelle told confessour preuely confessyon cause ye shold haue none gretter merueylle herof shall telle another grete abstynence whan confessonr perceyued tyme gretly wasted feblyd body receyued none suche mete drynke febyll folke sholde comforted wyth gaue counseyll sholde putte colde water dranke suger lytyl suger roset wherby spyrytys myght quyckenyd wyth touenyd confessour sayde lytyll lyf left wytt whiche semeth ye wolde vtterly quenchyd whan confessour hadde askyd knewe excusacion vnderstode wordes hadde soo vsed bytter mete vnsauory drinkys maner swete thyng noyous body cause dysposycion tourned custome soo etyng f esshe rehersed afore whan sholde drynke wyne contree foryeuyd tyme hadde lycence kepe chambre medlyd wyne soo wyth water loste taste sauour also grete parte colour afterward whan xv yere age lefte alle maner drynkyng wyne vsed drynke colde water maner soden mete taken brede alone wythdrewe fro lytyll lytyll euery daye somwhat wythin lytyl tyme helde brede rawe herbes p att lasie whan twenty yere age aboute lefte etyng brede helde rawe herbes thenne afterward came suche hyghe state lyuyng nonght vse kynde shall declared openly ynogh wythinforth helpe god oonly myracle alle body oppressyd gretely wyth many dyuerse sekenesse grete traueylles kyndly dygestyon body hadde noo place stomake also vsed myght vse offyce defyeng yet strengthes body notwythstondyng strengthe lyuyng mete drynke neuer febly er soo confessour recordeth alle lyf myracle myght neuer doo dede strengthe kynde physyens sayd tolde afterward confessour oonly myracle thyse thynges shall clerely play nely helpe god openly declared wythin boke afterward conclusyon abstynence fro tyme confessour mayster reymound knewe recordeth lyued wyth mete ne drynke nourysshynge ne hadde none comforte none kyndely strengthe yet neuertheles suffred gladly maner dy laboures came state lyuynge trowe ye trewely bodely excercyse vse rather fulnes ye spirite shall tel wise ye fulnes ye spirite tyme rebonudeth body made subiecte acordyng werkys spyryte spiryte gostely creature fedde wyth gyftes gostely grace body suffreth pacientli aboue naturall strengthe nedes wold dobute herof trowe none resonable creature whether martyr holy martyrdome suffred gladly aboue naturall strengthe tormente myserye theyr bodyes passyons trowe yeis fro whens cometh trowe ye fulnesse spyryte ofte tymes knowen experyens oure dayes yf man womman occupyed goddes seruyce deuoutly reketh neuer longe fasteth neuer speke wyth creature whan ceseth speciall deuocion occupyed outward bodely besynes harde hym faste doo dyde whens cometh grace oonly fulnes spyryte conforteth body whiche accordeth werkis alle gyfte aboue nature yet naturally spyryte otherwhyle communeth wyth body body wyth spyryte bothe good euyl thyse wordes denye ther ben somme whiche maye faste esely somme symply faste absteyne longe tyme togyder lyf semeth inpossyble bi nature thus moche rehersed grete abstynence tyme takyth hede also another thynge holy mayde tourmentyd body wyth besyde abstinence made bedde al bordes wythout ony stuff otherwhyles wolde sytte stonde holy medytacions whyle knele praye alwaye whan wolde slepe laye coun wythout ony doyng awaye weryng clothes weryd alwaye wollen bothe nexte body wythout tyme vsed hayre cilyce yt lefte afterward cause confessour supposed clene wythin eschewed vnclenes wythout engendred cilyce hayre hayre vsed yron chayne next body euyr syttyng faste sydes wythoute ony remeuynct ease vnto tyme endented skynne made marke ther vpon hadde forbrennyd ghostely doughters felawes tolde ward mayster reymond confessour whiche ghostely doughters felawes ofte tymes dyuerse sekenesses suffred constreyned chaunge clothes wasshe awaye swete therfore confessour afterward cause grete sekenesse suffred lytyl sholde deed constreyned obedyens sholde leue cheyne wolde doo hyr good wyll euermore contynued wakyng tyl daye dawed morowe shall declared opynly afterward lytyll lytyll lorde gaue grace ouercome slepe vnnethe wold slepe half houre two dayes vnnethys wolde receyue half houre sekenes coustreyned therto wolde saye otherwhyle confessour moost traueylle euer hadde ouercome slepe soo harde bataylle myght haue vyctorye yet ouer confessour recorded yf myght haue founde ony body cowde hadde vnderstonde commyned wyth hyr vertue goodnes god shold greue though hadde wythout mete drynke slepte hondred dayes hondred nyghtes sholde neuer haue wery rather fressher gladder tolde ofte tymes confessour neuer soo well refrysshed spyryt thys lyf whan myght fynde wyth whome myght commyne goodnes god knewe well tho whiche conuersaunt wyth p openly perceyued whan myght haue leyser speke god tho thynges vertu whiche hyd herte appieryd strongely ghostely gladnesse body outwarde p whan hadde noo leyser talke oure lorde thenne feble herof bereth wytnesse confessour mayster reymound worshyp god owne shame oftymes whan holy mayde wolde speke goodnes lorde greate myseryes shewed cause longe tyme contynuaunce spekyng also cause ferre louyng sayde hym selfe fyll slombryng alwaye contynued forthe spekynge reysyd vp loue breste oure lorde nothyng perceyuynge slepe tyll longe tyme afterward whan perceyued slepe wyth grete voys awoke hym sayde lese ye prouffyte sowle lytyll slepe speke walle yow p ferthermore desyred aboue alle folowe stappes holy fader saynt domynyke wyse receyued euery day theyes dyscyplyne wyth yron chayne fyrst dyscyplyne self seconde alle tho lyue thirde deed p thus rede legende saynt domynyk vsed contynually therfore vsed longe tyme afterward p tyme feblyd sekenes myght longer vse hyt p whanne hyr confessour axyd hyr pryuely wyse vsed manere penaunce wyth grete shamefastenesse knowleched hym p euery dysciplyne occnpyed houre halfe moost partye blode folowed foo sholdres doune fete p loo maydens perfeccyon thys holy maydens sowle thryes daye lete hyr self blood goddys loue shedyng hyr blood hys blood see ye vertue wyth ony exaumple informacyon ony man erthe vsed suche grete penaunce wyth hyr faders hows redeth sayntes lyues wrytyng holy faders egypte leueth none vnsought sercheth ouer espye whether ye fynde ony lyke hyr ye shall fynde saynt powse fyrst heremyte lyued longe deserte crowe brought hym euery daye half lof hys mete ye may also fynde saynt anthonye full holy lyuer dyd grete meruayllous penaunce yet wente dyuers ankrys aboute eche gadred somme floures vertue ye may also fynde saynt hyllaryon holy lyuer yet saynt jerome seyth fyrst enformed vertuous lyuyng saynt anthonye ro wente deserte myghtly ouercam hys enemyes ye may fynde also macharye arsenye many whyche longe telle techers vertuous lyuyng one moo bothe worde also exsaumple deserte relygion holy mayde nethyr hyr doctryne vertues relygyon nother deserte hyr faders hows wythout ony informacyon exaumple ony man erthe came grete perfeccyon abstynence notwythstondyn ge manyfolde lettyng whyche suffred hyr faders hows shall yet saye thys maydens commendacyon praye lystene lytel whyle shall telle holy wrytte maketh mencyon yt moyses fasted twyes fourty dayes wyth mete drynke ely one lord ihesu cryst also gospell sayth thei fasted many yeres contynued holy wrytte telleth saynt johan baptyst though deserte lyued hony soukeles herbes symply fasted fynde nowhere wryton marye magdelyne allone hyr storye maketh mencyon hyr lyf fastyd euery yere fourty dayes gyder wyth mete drynke thre thyrty yeres folowyng leuyng roche see trowe lord hye blyssed moder commytted hyr thys holy mayde hyr may stresse hyr moder somwhat touched afore shall clerely de declared afterward helpe god thys may ye knowe thys holy mayde specyall yefte synguler grace god preferryd holy lyuynge aboue alle sayntes whyche ben rehersed afore full odyous comparyson make suche lykenes bytwene sayntes among whiche sayntes sauyour ihesu cryst nempned whome lyken ony saynt comparyson holy lyuyng sholde euen wyth hym blasfemye al tho sayntes whyche ben named rehersed make lykenesse merites lyuyng ye shal consydere take hede fyrst grete magnyfycence lord ihesu cryst euery day hys gracyous plentuous largenes mult plyed hys newe yeftes grace wyth arayeth ghostly maketh perfyte hys chosen sowles another also ye shall consydere take grete synguler worthynesse hyr noo iniurye ne wronge sayntes holy chyrche syngeth seyth specyally syngulerly euery saynt hym self thes wordes salamon non est inue tus similis illi none founde lyke thys wordes muste vnderstonde grete myght large fredom lord makyng holy perfyte hys chosen sowles whyche may wylle endowe arraye euery saynt syngulerly wyth specyall yefte grace wyth ony wronge alle thys mater shall cesse procede forth fyrst purpose thyse condycyons abstynence thys holy mayde may vnderstode clerely lene body wyth many herdenes penaunce sharpe afflyccyon often tymes tamed make hyr body buxom subgett seruyce sowle tyme hyr moder lapa tolde mayster reymond hyr confessour thought hyr doughter tormented holy hyr body penaunce soo grete myght strenghte body wolde wyth ony greuaunce lyf vp hyr sholdres borthen hors bere bere vp hyghe garet aboue two longe steyers tyme sayde twyes soo grete body thanne afterward age xxxviij whan contynued soo grete penaunces hyt meruayll yf nought lord hadde kepte hyr myracle hyt hadde meruayll though hadde wastyd awaye tyme whan hyr confessour mayster reymond knewe hyr full slender creature meruayll spiryte encreced vertue weyker wexxd body though wer ouercome sowle wythstondyng alle thys wolde euer laboure gladdely namely helthe sowles suffred grete sekenesse hyr body spyryte whyche strong wythin susteyned comforted feble body wyth shall cesse torne ageyn fyrst mater thys chapytre whan thys holy mayde hadde full graunte lycence hyr frendes serue lord hyr lytell chambre assygned hir began full feruently styghe vp ghoostly hyr heuenly spouse serpent ol de enemye fende though ouercome hym dyuers tymes afore yet cessed assaylle hyr estesonys steryd eue hys doughter lapa thys maydens moder carnall loue hadde body hyr doughter hyr self lette hyr hyr penaunce tyme whan moder came hyr doughter aspyed howe bete hyr self wyth yren chayne cryed waylyng wyth lowde voys seyde doughter doste thou thou arte dede thou sleest thy self allas hath couseylled doughter herto hath steryd hyr thys soo wyth cryeng waylyng thys olde womman tormeted hyr self wood body wyth ryng hyr clothes hyr thought hyr doughter dede noyse thys cryeng neghbours styred aboute come inne see thys olde woman eyled whan cam sawe thys holy mayde made hyr bedde bare boordys rested wolde slepe wyth vyolence hyr moder took hyr chambre broughte hyr owne chabre laye thought wolde make slepe owne bedde wyth hyr whan thys holy mayden sawe thys wysdome spyryte shewed grete gladnes chere kneled doun fore hyr moder prayng mekely wyth esy wordes wolde wouchesauf put awaye alle hyr steryng vnpacyence esy redy obeye hyr wolde haue hyr redy lye wyth hyr wolde bydde hyr whan thus wysely p syd moder kepe hyr quyete layde hyr doune one syde bedde swete medytacyons wont haue tyme hir moder slepe rose vp pryuely wente agayne hyr holy ghostly excercyse fende eftsones hadde enuye herto sholde encrece vertue styred hyr moder seconde tyme ageyn hyr ageyn thys holy mayde vsed thys prudence cause wolde nomore make hyr moder sory wyth hyr took pryuely post leyde hyr bedde vnder shete clothes abouen moder whan wold comen vysyte hyr sholde suppose whyche laye vnder clothes yet neuer thelesse kepte hir comyn stome harde lyeng dyd fore hyt longe tyme moder aspyed thys well aspyed sayd hyr doughter thys wyse doughter see well alle laboure vayne may chaunge thy purpose ese lete ouer passe lyghtly therefor go slepe thou arte wont soo ouercomen wyth stedfastnes thys holy mayde suffred hyr euer afterwarde lyue holy ghoost styred hyr thus endeth thys chapytre somme thynges ther ben rehersed inne hyr confessour mayster reymond knewe hadde reuelacyon holy mayde katheryne hyr grete abstynence sharpenesse penauce hyr maner worchyng somme thynkes knewe reuelacyon hyr moder lapa som dyuers matron conuersaut som thynges knewe hym self namely hyr synguler gracyous yefte abstynence p laste vyctorye bathe took abyte saynt domynyk whyche long tyme desyred fore ca vij whan thys holy mayde restoryd ageyn hyr deuoute excercyse perceyued enemye mankynde besy lette hyr feruent hyr ghostly excercyse euery day wayled euery day wepte axynge prayng lorde deuoutly wold wouchesauf gyue hir grace resceyue abyte saynt domynyk long desyred whiche thorugh hys grete yt hote hyr holy fader saynt domynyk vysyon neuer seker hir self kepe purpose maydenhode vnto tyme resceyued holy abyte wyst well tyme arayed wyth abyte alle maner speche hyr weddyng shold cesse sholde suffred serue hyr ghoostely frely wherfore prayed hyr fader moder wold gyue hyr leue one susters penauce sayn domynyk ben called comyn speche cyte senee susters mant ouermore prayed sustres receyue hyr abyte amonge theyr holy nombre thys axyng mod well apayed alle sayde one nay euer aboute moche myght withdrawe hyr hyr grete penaunce vsed thys cause purposed tyme go hoot bath bathed hyr doughter wyth hyr assone thys holy mayde felte ony maner comforte solace body bathyng lytell lytell shold haue left hyr grete penaunce thys done wythout wyll fende whyche besyed hym myght wyth drawe suche feruent sowle ghostly callynge hyr heuenly spouse taught thys synfull woman lapa maydens moder full pryuely malycyous wylles neuerthelesse bi cause ther may counseyll preuayll ne haue maystrye ageynst couseyll god thys holy mayde armed wyth armere vyctorye bothe hyr ryght syde eke hyr lefte syde torned alle fende trecherous wylles grete profyt hyr sowle whan came bathe founde newe maner bathyng hyr sowle shold tormente hyr body amonge delycyous bathe went condyt hote water cam inne bathe satte naked suffred pacyently hote water brenne hyr tender naked flesshe whyche payne hyr thenne whan bete hyr wyth cheyne shall telle hyr confessour knewe tyme hyr moder lapa lde mayster reymond afore hyr doughter went bathed thenne thys mayde pryuely tolde hym bathed wysely asked leue hir moder whan myght bathed hyr self whan folke gone wyst well yf hyr moder seen hyr myght dyd thenne hyr confessour axyd hyr myght suffre grete te wyth peryll deth thys mayde answerd hym sayd full symply whan satte bathe thought besyly vpon paynes purgatorye hell prayng lord whome hyely offendyd wolde wouchesauf torne mercyably tho peynes deserued temperall payne suffred gladly hys mercy grete gladdenesse hyr herte peyne ryght swete hir therfore hyr body thynge hurte though felt peyne whan tolde thys tale hyr confessour wente home ageyne hir penauce wont vse whan hir mod yt ceyued hope tho hir chaungyng yet cessyd neuer wyth grutchyng penaunce vsed whyche grutchyng thys mayde hyr doughter lyghtt ly suffred hit ouer passe wyth defeere hauyng myude rather hir holy purpos excyted steryd hyr moder euery day hold go sustres penauce saynt domynyk praye thom hyr doughter myght receyue abyte penaunce long tyme desyred moder seyng myght haue reste hyr doughter wente susters penaunce prayed hyr doughter myght receyue abyte amonges answerd sayd hyr custome receyue maydens ne yonge wymmen abyte onely wedowes sadde age good name fame wold fully gyue hem goddes seruyse syth susters abyte enclosed vp eueryche lyued home hyr owne hows hyt full necessary eche suche sadde age yt myght coude gouerne self saddely cause susters penaunce answerd thus shall declared helpe god openly nough next chapytre sueth whan moder answere went home tolde hyr doughter whiche answere doughter full gladsome moder full heuysom neuerthelesse yet thys holy mayde mystrusted wy welle hyr purpose sholde fulfylled behot hir gloryous fader saynt domynyk therefore ef sone prayed hyr mod sholde cesse go thyse susters ageyn praye wyth asmoche instaunce coude myght receyue abyte moder dyd brought ageyn answer dyd fyrst ne sone happed thys mayde fyll seek body whyche sekenesse comynly yong folk ben vexyd wyth tha ne come sadde age yet p raduenture passynge sh suff ed hote bathe myght cause al wyl god yt shold skynne hyr body full bladder byles vnnethe myght knowe also strong feuer moder seyng hyr doughter soo seek though loued hir sone doughter tenderly yet thys doughter nourysshed wyth hyr owne mylke loued tenderly therefor sory hyr dysease knewe cause thys sekenesse cam suche sekenesse myght come abstynence rather supfluyte also tyme comyn sekenesse yong chyldren yong maydens therefor coude deme sekenesse came ese remedye myght dyd bothe wordes comfort also dede syttyng alle waye beddes syde hyr seker ye doughter body ye strenger hyr holy desyre wayteng leysyr constreng hyr mod manere pursewe fulfyll hyr desyre wysely swetly sayde hyr moder good dere moder yf ye wold hole ferd well praye beth aboute yt desyre may fulfylled receyue abyte penauce ellys wote well lord saynt domynyk whyche haue called seruyce woll ordeyne ye sholde longer haue thys lyf whan moder herde thys oft many tymes rehersed hyr beynge ferde lest sholde haue deyde went susters ageyn prayed entyerly abyte ouercome wyth hyr prayer grauted hyr thys wyse yf youre doughter noght ouer semely body ouer f beaute shall graun axyng receyue hyr yf fayre drede v peryll slandre malycyou lyuyng men thyse dayes thys cause dare consente receyue hyr noo wyse moder answerd sayde cometh see hyr eue ye dome whee fayre sente two dyscrete matron chosen amonge wyth lapa see thys mayde bothe dysposycyon hyr body also serche hyr desyre soule come founde thys mayde lyeng seek bedde therefor myght clerely knowe dysposycyon hyr body sekenesse neuerthelesse hyr wordes knewe hyr feruent desyre sowle seruyce god gretly astoyned also gladde seeng yong mayden passe vertuous yuyng many olde matron wherefor took leue ioyefully gretely edyfyed hyr wordes tolde theyr felawys grete ioye harde sawe whan thise susters herde thys counseyll frerys receyued hyr oo wyl one assent amoges sendyng worde moder also sone ye mayden hole shold brynge hir ye frere prechours myght r ceyue abyte saynt domynyk whyche long desyred presence brethern sust en abyte custome whan moder tolde wordys hyr dought gladde wepte ioye thanked lord saynt domynyk hadde fulfylled hys promys byh st thanne began preye god myght hole hyr bodely infyrmy fulfylle hir holy purpose receyuyng abyte lest shold lette delayed hyr desyre bodely seke sse fyrst gladde hir bodely sekenesse meke suffrau ce afterward heuy therof besekyng lord besy prayer wold wouchelauf delyuer hyr wyth ony taryeng sekenesse whiche letted purpose hyr desyre prayed lord grauted hir wyth fewe dayes afterward hole lord wold alway goodnesse denye axyng suche conferme euer wyth theyr besynesse fulfylle hys wyll euer axyd desyred referred loued wyth myghtes hir sowle seruyce offred hyr self hole body sowle whome restoryd bodely hele alle mod aboute tarye hyr hyr purpose lenger tyme made suche instau ce hyr moder day houre assygned whan sholde receyue hyr abyte whyche abyte receyued wyth grete ghostly gladnesse whanne moder doughter come gyder chyrche frere charge susters arayed holy mayde wyth maner abyte presence colour whyte blak token innocence kenesse whyche abyte holy faders saynt domynykes ordre ordeyned hadde soo whytnes vnderstonde innocencye blaknesse mekenes mayster reymond hyr confessour recordeth wryteth ther none abyte soo well accordyng hyr conuersacyon lyuyng bothe inward outward thenne thys mayden wyth alle hyr myght tyme forthward mortyfyed hyr body sleyng olde lust synne wyth alle hys braunches pryde wynnyng veray mekenesse whyche mekenesse betokeneth mantell blacke hadde receyued alsoo besyed hyr wyth alle hyr myghtes kepe innocencye virgynytee maydenhode onely body also sowle endeles spouse ihesu cryst whyche veray lyght receyue hym fayrenesse vertuous lyuyng whyche fayrenesse betokenyd whyte cote vnder mantell yf hyr abyte black alle whyte tho two thynges mekenesse innocencye myght properly vnderstonde therby yf hyr abyte hadde ben graye russeth myght represente mortyfycacyon properly puryte clennesse sowle thys cause susters begynnyng denyed hyr thys abyte lest hadde able bere mekenesse clennesse herte dredyng hyr yonge age whanne holy mayde hadde receyued abyte hyt become hyr better dyd matron therfor well hadde denyed hyr whyche abyte ordeyned fore holy faders token innocencye syth soo passyd clennes alle chastyte wedowhode one thynge hyr confessour mayster reymond recordeth wryteth abyte hadde neuer hys full perfeccyon cytee senee vnto tyme holy mayde hadde take vpon hyr hyt fyrst mayde cytee took vp hyr whyche many maydens afterward receyued also soo myght songe hyr verse dauyd prophete speketh adducentur regi virgines posteam lorde god endeles kyng many maydens shall brought inne thys holy mayde katheryne p thys mayden encreced shall declared afterward helpe god shall make ende thys chapytre procede forthe thys holy abyte beganne thys holy relygyous estate lest defaute knowyng opynyon fame thys holy maydens vertuous lyuynge myght lessenyd therby somme mennys hertys matere whyche reherced thys chapytre mayster reymond recordeth seyth hadde relacyon hyr moder hyr self abyte nedeth profe knowen openly ynough p begynnyng foundamente relygyous state susters penaunce saynt domynyk came manere lyuyng tho sustren capitulum viij alle tho wyll rede thys presente chapytre folowynge shall fynde wryten recorded many feythfull creature dyuerse partyes ytalye many worthy actys dedys holy fader saynte domynyk gloryous worthy confessour cryste tutor defendour feyth holy chyrche saynte domynyk also techer enfourmer good state perfyte lyuers ouercame myghtely bothe tholose also lombardye hym selfe hys brethern many heretykes tyme canonizacion rome prouyd openly holy fader pope hondred thousand heretykes tourned hys prechyng shewyng myracles lumbardye alone p neuertheles venemous doctryne heretykes hadde soo enfected peple sowles almoost possessyons holy chyrche laymennes hondes kepyng owne herytage caused bysshoppe goo aboute begge hadde none power neuer wythstonde ye defaulte temperall substaunce ne releue clerkys poure folke dewe offyce consydered holy fader saynt domynyke myght none wyse suffre myscheff holy chyrche grete entyrly loue hadde therto chaas worthy lyf pouerte hym selfe also theim shold folowers thenne beganne pursue forthe ryght holy chyrche assosyeng hym cert yn laye people ed god knew well comyned wyth theym ordeynaunce holy lyuyng sholde recouere againe rychesses holy chirche defended myghtely euer afterward faithfully agaynst heretikes comyn assent suche lyf soo graunted ordeyned p holy fader saynt domynyke founde ony well wyllynge folke suche lyuyng fyrst enduced theym swere sholde kepe obserue thynges shold reherced theym vterest putte goodes lyf therfore jeoperdye le te holy lyuynge sholde bee lette suche wedded made also wyues swere sholde also lette husbondes maynten suche poure lyuyng ryght holy chyrche rather sholde helpe theym power might eyther partye holy fader saynt domynyke byhote theym sykerly yf kepte purpoos endeles lyf mede p tho men toke holy lyf vppon called fryer crysico knyghthode neuertheles cause ey sholde beknowen fro somme token sholde haue somme maner besynes aboue vsage laye peple gaue colour owne habyte bothe men wymmen knyghthode ihesu cryst shold whyte blake soo eyther colour sholde apere outward token innocencye mekenes euermore assigned theym saye certeyn nombre pater nosters aue maria sholde occupyed euery houre diuyne seruyce day day whan tyme saynt domynyk passed worlde blysse heuen encresyng myracles canonyzed court rome f re suster yt fyrst called ye knyghthode ihu cyr amo synguler worshyp fouder saynt domynyk chauged name co mi as called f er susters penauce saynt domynyk ye cause thought yt fyrst name sholde chauged saw bi merytes myracles saynt domynyk prechyng ye fryer cursed heresye cause wherfore theym thought yt moche nedefull occupyed suche outward batayle prechyng rather wythinward batayle agaynst gostely enmyes chose therfore called fryer susters penauce ye last ye nobre fryer prechours encresyd hugely amonge one clere shynnyng sterre saynt peter bothe martyr mayde whiche martred heretykes ryght holy chyrche destroyed heretykes deth soo thys company wulues aboute destroye goddes vnite holy chyrche vtterly avoyded pea yelden holy chyrche wherfore cause name knyghthede sesyd channged name penaunce neuerthelesse maner state louyng descendeth remayneth men whyle ther wyues ben left soole lyuyng theym self relygyous lyf neuer afterward desyryng bee wedded cause relygyous kepte wyth husbondes fore state whiche began kepte lyues ende p consyderyd behelde wydowes purposed kepe theym wedowhode desiring folowe susters penaunce saynt domynyke remedye synnes prayed fryer prechours italye enforme maner lyuyng whiche ordeyned saynt domynyke cause maner lyuyng hard blessyd fader ordre whiche called munyo wrote maner lyuyng toke thyse wydowes whiche manere lyuyng daye callyd amonges theym rule thay may properly callyd soo moche encludeth wythin thre pryncypall vowes relygyous folke haue tyme nombre susters thus encresed dyuerse partyes italye holy fader pope tho dayes whiche called honoryus perceyued good lyuynge thyse susters graunted theym bulle tyme interdyction myght dyuyne seruyce amonges fryer prechours soo holy fader pope johan whiche came hym hadde made constytucions clementynis agaynste vyrgyns gardys declared bulle decretall constytucion sholde vnderstonde susters penaunce saynt domynyke decretall astate repreued ony wyse p loo maydens ye may vnder stonde state liuing fou de wymmen susters answerd soo att begynnynge moder holy mayde wounte receyue maydens state lyuyng oonly wydowes approuyd sadnes thyse thynges ben wrytten chapytre parte mayster reymound founde wryten im dyuerse place italye mater herde vnderstode theym wyth inquysycion many holy faythfull olde fryer susters saynt domynyke thus endeth chapytre p wonderfull encrece prouffyted vertu holy lyuyng sholde bee byloued thynges whiche rehersed confessour grace done lorde capl ix holy mayde receyuinge habyte made none byhest thre pryncipalle avowes relygyon cause estat asked nought
