rehersed afore yet neuerthelesse purposed kepefull stedfastly tho thre pryncypal avowes self vowe chastyte none doughte hadde made avowe maydenhode afore tender age touchyng obedyence purposed oonly bee obedyent fryer mayster susters pryoresse susters also confessour whiche obedyence kepte lyues ende p sayde lyue whan sholde passe worlde hadde neuer mynde brake oni obedyence neuerthels cause somme whiche hadde enuye holynesse bacbyters lyers sayde contrarye p doo vnderstonde maydens thowe holy mayde hadde none tourment whyle lyuynge erthe oonly vndyscrete byddyng mysseyng souereyns myght haue ben maner martyr grete pacience whiche suffred confessours vnderstood nonght ne gaue none credence many tymes excellent gyfte grace receyued god ne gaue none reuerence werkys lorde wrought merueylously therforre wold haue made lyuyng commyn lyuyng susters consyderyng ye opyn token grace shewed dyuerse tymes rather myghi lykened ye pharysens seyth opyn myracles whyche lord wrought yet grutched cause helyd man vpon sabat daye seyng thus p non est hic homo deo qui sabbatum non custodit man god hals kepeth sabat daye holy mayde whan hadde receyued habyte penaunce besyed cowde obeye souereyns therto durst forsake ye waye vertuous lyuynge whiche lord taught hym self soo bytwene thyse two sore angwisshed tourment ther maye none tongue telle ne penne wryte trought ye maydens martyrdome trowe yeis lorde god ofte sayde repref yt vysyons come nought god fende p notwythstondyng whiche sawe many merueylous werkes therto myght see lyf myracle shall declared clerely stronge martyrdome semeth p touchyng pouerte lynyng kepte soo perfyghtly vertu pouerte beyng faders hous housholde greate plente temperall goodes self toke thynge wolde gyue frely poure folke therto fader gaue specyall leue p loued soo moche pouerte sayde preuyly confessoure hadde neuer ioye faders hous cause temperall goodes soo plenteuosly vsed therin therfore prayed oure lord hertely wolde vochesauf tak awaye rychesse brynge hyr frendes pouerte seyng wyse lorde whether good aboundeth soo plentuously myn faders hous good sholde aske myn frendes nought oonly good euerlastyng knowe well lord amonges thyse temperall goodes moche peryll medeled amonge therfore wolde nought myn frendes encombred wyth theym p whan hadde thus prayed lorde goodnes herde prayer suffred hee frendes fader moder kynne falle ryght lowe pouerte many merueylous chaunces wythout ony trespaas theym well knowe tho knewe theym whyles lyued may ye knowe mayden kepte full dewely thre pryncipall vowes relygyon obedyence chastyte pouerte made none avowe openly whan receyued habyte penaunce shall telle perfection tyme hadde receyued habyte whan hadde receyued habyte holy fader saynt domynyke promysed began anone swete vertuous lyuynge sought occacions cause constreyne self streyghtly dyde afore myght deuoutlye loue spouse ihesu seyng self wyse lo thou hast take vp maner relygyon thou mayst nomore lyue thou hast doo thy seculer lyuynge goo newe relygyon come whiche reule thou must nedes reuled est thou colour thyn clothes nedeth fro time forward kepe perfyghtly pouerte clennesse body sowle whiche tokeneth bi whyte cote nedeth also dede worlde whiche betokenneth blake mantel therfore see thy self thou gouerneste thou muste goo streyte waye fewe walken ynne sekernesse therfore kepyng pouerte cle nesse p holy mayde purposed kepe sylence full streyte speke whan shold shryue confessour sayde wrote afore mayster reymound thre yere contynuelly kepte sylence whan wolde beshryue kepte also contynuelly chambre whan wolde goo chyrche mete hadde none nede goo lytyll soone doo vsed ete none maner mete made fyre taken breed alone rehersed afore p also made ordynaunce owne herte neuer come mete wyth wepyng soo euer afore mete wolde offre lord teres fede soule fyrst afterwarde wolde susteyne body wyth mete p faders hows wyldernesse deserte notwythstondyng confluence peple therin p besyde wakyng prayer medytacions teres vsed trowe none tongue cowde telle p made also ordynaunce self whan bretheren freer prechours stepte wolde wake whan frier hadde tonge ij peel matyns anone erst wolde seye spouse ihesu cryste wyse loo lorde myn bretheren thyn seruauntes haue rested tyme haue prayed theym thou sholdest kepe fro deuelys fro ouercomyng fendes p lorde aryse praye therfore lorde praye kepe theym gyue leue reste whyle soo laye doune vpon hard bordes stoke vnder hede stede bolster p lord ihesu gracious spouse seyng mayde whiche gaue thyse grace wolde suffer soo able soo dylygent dyscyple vntaught wythout perfyght mayter nother man ne angell hym self wolde informer vertu anone shett vp chambre oure lorde ihesu cryste well beloued spouse sauyour alle mankynde appieryd taught enformed fully tho thynges longeth helthe sowle self tolde priuely ward confessour sayde hym thyse wordes fader vnderstondeth trouthe neuer taught ne enformed ony thynge longeth helth sowle man ne woman oonly myn lorde ihesu spouse sowle inspyracion ellys hys open apperyng spekyng nowe speke p knowleched also confessour begynnyng vysyon whan apperyd openly bodely wyttes soo perceyued wyth bodeli erys voys began waxe ferd lest hadde deceyte fende ofte tymes transfygureth hym angell lyght whiche feer noo wyse dysplesyd lorde rather commended feer sayde longe man woman lyueth lyf sholde euer aferd soo thou mayst fynde wryten p beatus vir qui semper est pauidus saye blessyd man euer feerfull p ferthermore oure lorde ihesu cryste sayde doughter wylt thou shall teche thou mayste knowe myn vysyon vysyon fende holy mayde answerde full mekely prayed hym wolde vouchesauf teche thenne sayde oure lorde thyn soule may esely taught inspyracyon worde dyscerne bytwene one cause wolde myght prouffyghte well therfore shall teche worde p doctours holy chyrche whome haue taught trouthe seyn soothe myn vysyon begynneth wyth drede euer passyng setteth sowle greate reste sekernes begyneth wyth maner bytternes euermore wexith swete contrarye herte dothe vysyon fende gyueth begynnyng semeth maner gladdenes sykenes ellys swetenesse whan passeth awaye euer encreseth sowle dred bytternesse trewest knowleche knowe myn wayes fendes wayes p waye penauce kepynge myn preceptys commaundementes begynnyng semeth harde sharpe sowle prouffyteth kepyng theym esely waxith p waye synne begynnyng semeth full delectable euer encres therof sowle made dampnable p yet shall gyue another token knowe myn vysyon vysyon fende vnderstonde sothe sythe soo trouthe euer myn vysyons sowle man receyueth greate knowleche trouthe cause knowleche trouthe full necessarye soule well self may knowe self whiche knowleche passeth fro self settinge lytyll selfe honoureth worshyppeth whiche condycion properly called condycions mekenes therfore full nedefull sowle sholde thus knowe self soo made meke vysyon contrarye vysyon fe de sythe fende fader lesynge kynge chyldren pryde may gyue hathe lesyng pryde therfore visyo soule semeth moche self made glad joye whiche properly condycion pryde lefte swellyng bolnyng pryde thene therfore yf thou examyne dyscusse dylygently thy self mayste knowe whether vysyon come trouthe ellys falsenesse yf come trouthe maketh thyn sowle meke yf come falsenes desceyte maketh thyn sowle proude p thenne hooly mayde whan hadde herde thys kepte holsome doctryne full dylygently sowle tolde afterward confessour also edyfycacion shall rehersyd wythinforthe helpe god thenne began lorde shewed holy mayde visyons reuelacyons plentuously soo ferforth yt vnnethe myght founde two men homely conuersacion gyders oure lorde jhesu gyders whether prayed redde medytacions walked slepte wyse comforted many time whan spake wyth hadde reuelacions vysyons spake sowle lord whyles tongue spake outward myghte longe contynue sowle wonderly drawe vp spouse jhesu wythin lytyll whyle afterward rauysshed bodely felyng rauysshyng came many merueylous thynges foloweth afterward well grete abstynence merueylous doctryne also vpon myracles whiche oure lorde shewed lyffe lest somme wolde doubte whether holy mayde hadde suche reuelacions shalle telle confessour mayster reymound preued whether reoelacions vysyons trewe begynnyng whan mayster reymound herde hye couersacio liuyng bega waxe homely wyth comunycacion wyth coude fele verely yt suche reuelacyons myght trewe whiche mystruste better therfore enquyred diuers menes wayes knowe whether came god fende whether fals trewe thenne came mynde ypocritis whiche regnyd dayes founde many dyscetys namely amoges wymmen ye deuyll dysceyued wyth ye vyce aboue creaturs hyt came also mynde ye fyrst womman eue deceyued many suche therefor doubted holy mayde whyle stode long thus suche doubte came mynde yf myght hir prayer gete lord one grete contrycyon hys synnes aboue customable contrycyon yt wonte haue myght knowe hyr vysyons reuelacyons dedys come holy ghost ther may none gete suche contrycyon yefte holy ghost ther none lyuyng saye whether worthy god hate loue yet hertely contrycyon synnes grete token grace mayster reymond sone thought thys went thys holy mayde prayed hir hertely wold praye hym oure lord yt wouchesauf gyue hym synnes whyche done thys holy mayde answerd sayd wold full gladly sayde mayster reymond myght easyd desyre hyr prayer onely yf bull hys synnes gyuen thys holy mayde axed wyth smylynge chere bull desyred haue answerd token bull axed one grete contrycyon hys synnes whiche contrycyon thys holy mayde sayde shold haue redy thenne tyme hyt semed mayster reymond vnderstode clerely hys thoughtes went hyr morne happed mayster reymond seek laye bedde kepte one hys brethern deuoute man whyche called nycholas pyse place ther lay seek hows sustres moche caught hys sekenes sodeynle jorneyng waye whan holy mayde perceyued seke o vp hyr bedde wythstondyng seek hir self feuers dyuers passyons sayd hyr felawe goo see srere reymond dothe fare hyr felawe answerd sayd nede though nede yet seker neuerthelesse yet come hym axyd ferd anone whan sawe hyr meruaylled gretety sayd hyr fe illy myght speke aa lady come ye hyther ye agrete dele seker thanne began speke goodnesse lord wonte oure vnkyndnesse ayenst hym wyth mayster reymond hir confessour arose vp hys bedde gretely comforted hyr wordes sate bedde besyde hauyng mynde yet wordes holy mayde spake hym euen afore whyle contynued spekyng kyndenes lord oure grete vnkyndenes sodeynly tyme hyr deuoute comunycacyon came hys mynde clere consyderacyon hys synnes hym thought stode afore ryghtwys jugement condempned peyne wycked lyuyng ryght theef stood temporall juge hym thought also sawe hys soule grete benygnyte mekenes lorde gracyously delyuered hym fro peyne worthy haue onely also clothed hym wyth hys owne clothes ther naked hym hys holy hows fedde hym nourysshed hym accepted hym hys seruyce ther synguler grace hys ende loo goodnesse hys deth vnto lyf hys drede vnto hope hys sorow vnto ioye hys shame vnto worshyp thyse consyderacios clerely knowynges syghte hys soule wyckettes wyndowes harde herte broken vp opened wellys ryuers wepyng terys aperyd plenteuouly cause foundament grounde hys trespassys shewed clerely hym moche wayled aferde laste suche grete plente sorow hys herte brest wold haue barst whan thys holy mayde saw styll suffred hym whyle fedde wyth hys owne terys therefore came wythin whyle cessyd lytell lytell bethought meruayllously newe grace thynkyng also hys petycyon whiche axed holy mayde day wyth torned hyr sayd thys thy bull spak yesterdaye answerd sayd ye laynge hir hondes vpon hys sholdres seyeng thus haue mynde fader gracyous yeftes lord soo wente home hyr chambre abode stylle wyth hys felawe gretely edyfyed comforted another tyme mayster reymond another excellent token thys holy mayde wyth ony axyng afore hit happed tyme thys holy mayde vysyted dyuers sekenes laye seek hyr bedde sent hyr confessour desyryng comen wyth pryuely newe reuelacyons whyche lord shewed grete sekenesse beganne speke goodnes lord reuelacion shewed hyr day heryng grete reuelacyon wonderfull shewed hyr none euer herde hauyng mynde grace lord hadde gyue hym afore prayer holy mayde bethought hym somthynges rehersed sayd thus whether trewe seyth whanne thought thus loked sodeynly hyr face saw hyr vysage transformed mannes vysage berded whyche vysage behelde hym stedfastly made hym sore aferde hit syght semely longe vysage myddel age hauynge long berde resonable assise coloured whete shewyng syghte mageste mageste oure lord jhesu myght wyse tyme see none face onely face thys syght grete fere lyfte vp armes began crye sayd oo loketh vpon whome holy mayde answerd sayd seeth beholdeth wyth worde dredefull face vanysshed awaye maydens vysage appyred clerely thys feynyng thyng trewe recordeth bereth wytnes hys wrytynges recordeth also confyrmacyon myracle sensybly vysyon hadde soo clere knowyng wythin hymself im sowle ghostly illumynyng mater holy mayde spak hym whiche wyll pupplyche openly hym thought felt experyence thyng whyche lorde sayd hys dyscyples whan behote holy ghoost seyeng theim thus et que ventura sunt annunciabit vobis whan ye haue receyued holy ghost shall shewe thynges ben come loo mystrust hadde wordes oure lorde gracyous goodnesse wouchesauf teche hym clerely self afterward bere wyttenes hir reuelacions ben trewe pryntyng stedfastly mynde grete grace shewed saynt thomas inde wolde taught enfourmed open tokenes gracyous gyfte whyche receyued holy mayde taught enformed example suche disciple mystrowyng tyme receyued gracyous token conpunccyon lord fore merytes holy prayer holy mayde yet contynued mystrust hyr reuelacyons trewe wherefor lord shewed hym self openly outeward wyttys myght therby knowe open experyence spak hir may sayd shewed thenne mayster reymond whiche mystrowed dyd som tyme saynt thomas inde bodely felyng ryght cryed afterward sayd worde deus meus et dominus meus god lord may thys mystrowynge renuwed saye thise two vysyos holy mayde veray spouse veray discyple lord god ben rehersed maydens ye sholde doubte ne despyse reuelacions vysyons whiche ye shall helpe god afterward alle wytnes may founde recorde saue allone ye sholde hem rede hem vnderstonde hem reuerence also ye may lerne ther holy example doctrynes whiche lord hath shewed suche vessell kynde seke bryttell grace meruaylously made strong precyous thus make ende chapytre thoo thynges whiche mayster reymond taught enfourmed holy mayde hath declared openly chapytre outake one thyng charged hyr kepe pryuely certeyn reuelacion rehersed fore p noble doctryne whyche lord gaf hyr begynnyng doctrynes whyche founded hyr maner lyuyng capitulum x syth grounde foundament trust byleue touche reuelacyons holy mayde helpe god declared chapytre goth afore therfore shall procede forth shewe spyrytuall edyfycacyon mayde cause trewe sowles feythfull ben fedde edyfyed wordes lord therefor shall telle shewe notable doctryne ye whiche holy mayde taught lord self thys holy mayde tolde hyr confessours amonges mayster reymond one begynnyng hyr vysyons lord appyred hyr whan prayed sayde hyr wyse knowest thou doughter thou arte yf thou knowe well two wordes thou art shalt blessyd thou art art yf thou haue veray knoweleche two thynges thy soule thy ghostly enemye shall neuer dysceyue thou shalt escape gracyously snare ne thou shalte neuer consente ony thyng ayenst commaundementes preceptes alle grace alle treuthe alle charyte thou wylte wynne wythout ony hardenesse bryef worde grete maner infynyte endeles oo grete wysdome expressyd vnder fewe syllable whether leng brede heythe depthe whiche saynt poule desyred haue wyth sayntes trowe yes oo dere maydens consydereth beholdeth meruayllously incomparable tresoure whiche founde holy maydes breste lord jhesu vndeceyuable trouth seyth holy mayde thus yf thou knowe thyse two thynges thy sowle fende shall neuer deceyue semeth full good make thre tabernacle dwellyng place vnto worshyp god excellent doctou whiche ched vnderstondyng thyse fruytfull wordes another loue deuocyon holy mayde katheryne whiche receyued holsom doctryne fewe fruytfull wordes thyrde ghostly tresoure valour tho whiche fynden lyf fewe fruytfull wordes vnderstondyng thoo fruytfull wordes founden ghostly rychesse plenteuously shall nede alle tho haue soo founde ghostly rychesse begge whether bryef fruytfull sentence trewe sayde art thou troweyes euery creature made maker jhesu cryst nought ferforth yf lord jhesu cryst oure maker wolde cesse tyme neuer lytell fro conseruacyon hys creature hath made anone creature shold torne nought whan soo euer creature doth synne whyche synne hym self nought ne hym self may noo thynge thynke ought saynt poule seyth meruaylle may ne haue beyng self ne yet conserued self beyng therfore apos le sayd qui se existimat ali uid esse cu nichil fit ipse se seduci wenyth ought nought decey ueth hym selfe se st thou mayde noughty creature creature made nought euer self owyng nought synne maketh self noughte saynt austyn sayd may noo thyng ought hym self rather nought oure lorde sayd sine nichil po stis sacere wythout ye may ryght nought whyche nought synne therfore ye may wel clerely know creature hym self nought knewe well saynt afore thys tyme whiche knoweleche veray wysdom excluded vera ly theyr sowles alle manere synne manere inflacyon synne may entree suche sowle whiche knoweth hir self nought may ioyfull vayne glorye ony good werke euer dyd whiche knoweth wel nough suche good dedys come neuer hir fro god may suche sowle enhaunce hir selfe pryde aboue holdeth hyr self nought may sowle thus sett th hir self nought inwardely despyse haue enuye may ony creature haue vaynioye outwarde rychesse hath dyspysed owne ioye hym self trowe suche creature taught wordes lord endeles wysdom sayd siego quero gloriam meam gloria mea nichil est yf seek myn owne ioye ioye nought also may suche creature knowed hym self wyse owne onely made hym see alle outwarde thynges myne syth hym self myght make suche creature haue delectacyon flesshely synnes euery day restreyneth hym self suche manere consyderacion nought loo maydens bryef fruytfull wordes thou art nought ye may consydere maner synne may excludeth bryef fruytful worde oure lorde sayde holy mayde whether bryef fruytful worde newe worde ye forsothe bothe newe olde olde worde lorde sayde moyses sussh whiche semyd brennyng whan sayde qui est misit say chyldren israel sente hit also newe worde cause newe reherfed holy mayden lyke wordes whiche fyrst bryef fruytfull sentence taught knowe hir self nough sholde lerne nexte fruytfull senten e aske lorde ought whiche endeles welle essencyall beyng thyse bryef fruytfull sentencys may ye knowe creature nought hym self hath vertue beynge cometh god maker creature almyghty god maker al creature hath onely hym self none endeles perfeccyon essencyall beynge myght neuer forme make thyng nought yf infynyte vertue essencyall beyng hym self wherfore alle euer oure lorde jhesu souerayne mayster taught spouse tho two bryef sentence rehersed afore thyng ellys sholde knowe hir self lord verayly hir maker depnes hir herte thenne sholde blessyd wyse fynde wryten sayd saynt k theryne virgyn marter whan vysytre hir prysone doughter knowe thy maker suche manere knoweleche cometh maner perfeccyon ordynate settyng sowle may loue large free gyuer wyth herte sowle styred euery day loue suche lorde fyrst er thanne made creature loued hem theyr deserue meryte onely infynte goodnes p ferth dredeth contynually offende ony maner wyse soo grete soo dredefull maker soo myghty soo large gyuer soo gladsom soo free louer may gladdely suffre manere dyseases suche lorde hath receyued receyuyth day day hopeth receyue wythoute ony deubte soo manyfolde goodnesse sholde wery tormented sekenes please amyable lorde endeyneth kepe reuerently louyngly hys mynde blessyd wordes suche lorde wouchesaue hys creature p wyll gladdely obeye commaundementes pretho thynges sowle loueth ye whiche desyre may hadde wiwout werke soo ferforth moche loueth soo moche werketh yet neuertheles trusteth nought owne werke owne self lorde worched cause louely desyre noothynge ellys knoleche god aulterd therfore amonge merueylaus thynges holy mayde helde doctryne whiche lord taught syngulerly bee worshy p ed whiche wurshypfull doctryne yet shall adde yf gretly dysceyued come fyrst notable doctryne ofte tymes holy mayde wout comyn speke tor confessoure mayster reymound worthynes condycions lord loued sowle sayde suche sowle perceyued ne seeth ne loued self ne none sowle ne hadde none mynde none creature full hard word mayster reymound vnderstonde therfore prayed hooly mayde declare thenne sayde sowle seeth selfe verely nought self knoweth perfyghtly goodnes wyth alle myghtes sowle maker p forsaked vite ly self alle creature hedeth self fully maker lord jhesu soo moche yt sendeth fully pryncypaly ghostely bodely werkynges hym perceyued maye fynde goodnes perfection blessydnes therfore shalle haue none wyll goo suche inwarde knowleche hym nothynge vinte loue encresed euery daye suche sowle transfourmyd maner oure lord may neyther thynke ne vnder stonde ne loue ne haue mynde god ellys god maye see self ne none creature onely god ne may loue self ne none god ne maye hane mynde self ne none god ne maye haue mynde maker ryght man vnder water swymmeth vnder water nether seeth ne touched nothyng water vnder water thynge yt aboue ye water neyther toucheth ne seeth yt aboue ye water shy neth vnder water may perceyue yet none wyse water maye byshewed water longe voder water ryght fareth sowle hyd loue god p lerned lorde dyuyne loue whiche neuer teched errour meke dyscyples ne gyueth theym cause coueyte ony thynge wyth hym euer ghostely excersyse hym p another tyme holy mayde reher syd presence confessour maister reymound many wer called clennes lyuyng full notable doctryne vertuous whiche good pure maydens knowe who chast lyuyng full spe yally god ye ben met ner god swete meke maydenhede sonner ye maye vnderstonde vertuous doctryne sowle whiche vertuously mette god rehersed afore moche hath loue god soo moche hath hate owne sensualyte loue god naturally cometh hate synne whiche ne agaynst god sowle fore consyderyng rote begynnynge synne regneth sensualyte pryncypally roted meued storyd hyghely holyly wyth alle merytes agaynst owne sensualyte vtterly destroye rote mayr longe sowle dwelleth body lyuyng lyffe euer shall lefte rote namely smale venyall synnes wherto accordeth ryght well saynt johan whan sayth thus si diximus quia peccatu non habemus ipsi no seducimus c yf saye haue noo maner synne sensualytes namely venyall synes desceyue oure self cause maye vtterly destroye rote synne thus sensualyte sayde afore conceyued grete displesaunce agaynst sen sualyte sesu lyte whiche dyplesaunce spyngin vp hooly hate dysplrsyng sensualyte whiche sowle euer wel kepte fro ghostely ennemyes p noo thynge kepeth sowle soo stronge soo syker doth suche holy ha e felt well appostle whan sayde cum infirmot tunc forcior sum et potens p whan feble syke myn sensualyte hate synne thenne stronger myghty er myn sowle loo fader suche hate cometh vertu swete febylnesse sykenesse cometh strengthe suche displesaunce cometh plesaunce p suche holy hate fader haue euer shall make meke euer fele meke thynges self shall make pacient aduersyt temperate prosperyte sette namely honeste vertue shall also make loued oi e god man p paynfull sowle full woo hath blysse suche holy hate ther moche vnordynate loue whyche stynkyng thorroke canell synne cause rote euill concupyscence al suche lyke wordes hooly mayde comyned daye daye wyth suche drede commendyng holy hate synne despysyng vnordynate loue p whan euer perceyued ony defaute synne synne many creature comyned ony anon wolde styred compassyon sayde loo brethern loo susteren cause tr spaas synne nothyng ellys vnordynate loue self whiche vnordynate loue norysshed pride vice p doth besynes loue god put e awaye suche vnordynate loue owne self oute owne hertes planteth therin holy hate synne certeyn ryght waye perfection amendement synne p loo maydens well thys hooly maydes doctryne accordeth wordes saynt poule sayd thus quod virtu infirmitate perficitur vertu made parfyghtly sekenes febylnes wha prayed lord remeue awaye temptacions whome oure lorde answerd sayde thus p sufficit tibi paule gracia mea inow paule myn grace hate synne wythstonde thenne brake saynt paule saide p libenter gloriabor infirmitatibus mei vt inhabitet virtu cristi shal gladly joyefull minsekenes febylnes laborynge hatyng vnderstondyng synne vertu grace therof maye inhabyted myn sowle see ye thyse holsom doctrynes holi mayde ben grounded vpon stedfast stone trouthe whiche stone cryst moche acorden wyth holy wrytynges doctours thus endeth chapytre praye al shall rede mekely consydere meryte deserte holy mayde whan oure lorde vou chesaf enforme vertu owne proper persone also wolde gyue credence wythouten ony othe wordes faythfull doctour taught thus make ende chapytre p merueylous victorye temptacions another maner doctryne gyue vnto lord famylyaryte holynes whiche hadde wyth oure lorde whiche hath herde fore capitulum xi ifynde wryten whan kynge salamon hadde doon make reysed vp toure kepe cyte jherusalem fro enemyes kynge babylone wood wyth reysed vp host destroye toure yf myght assone kinge salamon perceyued wold come wyth hoste destroye toure ordeyned made merueyllous stronge wally rounde aboute toure myghtely soo myghty walles whan euer came assayle wyth ony maner shotte dartes sholde merueylously turne agayn wounde slee hoste p ryght soo kynge babylone kynge pryde enemye pea fende ghostely enemye consyderyng kynge salamon auctor conseruatour keper pea hadde reysed vp hyghe vertuous toure whiche holy mayde katheryn defens jherusalem holy chyrche dredyng therby feste sholde cause many creature helthe dede good ensamples lyuyng also holy doctryne waxed wood wyth tourned wyth spyryte hys malyce destroye wyth many thousande whyles almyghty god mercyable peasyble lord suffred done encrece victoryous blessed endeles crowne spouse therto strengthed ouer wyth myghty ghostely armour ouercome hym wan vertue tyme batayle ouercomynge temptacyons thenne dyde tyme pea whylys wythout temptacions soo fende whyles tourned agayn shamefully hym self oure lord enspyred aske bi prayer haue vertu ghostely strengthe wherfore prayed many dayes longe tyme laste suche longe deuoute prayer lorde vocheusaufe gracyously taught wyse sey ng thus doughter yf thou wilt gete vertu ghostely strengthe thou muste folowe myght myn goodly vertu ouercome power fendes many maner wayes ouercomyng p yet gyue ensample manhede wolde ouercome hym takyng dethe vppon crosse ye myght taught therby yf ye wolde ouercome ghostely enemyes take crosse dide whiche crosse shall grete refresshyng temptacyons yf ye haue mynde paynes suffred vpon temptacyons certeyne paynes crosse may well called refresshyng temptacion payne ye suffre myn loue lyke ye bee passyon nedes ye muste lyke joye p therfore myn loue doughter suffre pacyetly bytter thynges none swete thynges doughter none wise thou shalt stronge enough suffre alle thynges pacyently p whan holy mayde hadde herde holy lesson foryate nought bare euer quykly mynd euer afterward hadde joye delyte trybulacions soo ferforthe noo thynge erthe soo grete refresshyng passios trybulacyons swete sufferaunces trybulacions wyste well crowne encresyd blesse heuen p tyme kynge salamon oure lorde jhesu cryste kynge heuen ande erthe hadde armed hys blessyd toure maydes sowle swete myghty holsom doctrynes suffred enemyes come preue toure yf myght ony waye wyse destroye p kynge babylone oure ghostely enmye fende wyth alle hys cursyd companye come byseged thys blessyd toure thorugh sufferaunce god rounde aboute wyth many wretchid temptacions p fyrst began assayle mayde flesshely temptacions oonly tempted thoughtes withinforthe ne yllusyons fantasyes slepe opyn vysyons wakynge bothe seyeng herynge seyng p tempted many maner wyse takyng vppon hym body eyre shame foule flesshely synne tempted therfore shall reherse theym clene sowles delectable p holy mayde ouercame suche foule delusyons therfore shall reherce whan holy may de perceyned besy fende brynge synne arose agaynste self myghtely punysshed body weryng cheyne soo moche blode folowed therto walked thenne wonte doo chirche almoost vse whiche slepe taken awaye yet wolde fende sece fro bata e hadde begonne toke vppon hym body eyre haue rehersed fore wyth greate nombre horryble companye wyth hym came stode byfore holy mayde thought hadde compassyon cou seylled sayd wretche tourmentest thou thy body soo ydell shalt thou wynne suche tourment peyne wenest thou thou mayst contynue therin thyn laste ende thenne mayst thou neuer contynue therin warne well yf thou wylt slee thy self soo better sese grete folye thenne soo slee thyn owne body yet hast thou tyme haue ioye worlde thou arte yonge therfore thou mayst sonner recouere thyne strengthe thy body agayn p notwythstondyng thyn grete penau ce thou hast doo lyue wymmen doo take husbond brynge forthe chyldren encrece mankynde yf thy desyre plese god trowest yu holy wymmen haue weddyd thynke sara rebecca lya rachell weddyd brought forth chyldren yet hooly wymmen wherto hast thou tabe vppon synguler lyf thou mayst noo wyse contynue whyles suche wordes many lyke fende wyth cursyd companye multeplyed agaynst prayed euer deuoutlye comaunded lyuyng spouse jhesu kepte herte keyes whyles fendes stood afore answerde none worde theym thus truste myn lorde jhesu cryste myn self worde myght neuer haue alwaye contynued stedfastly deuoute prayer afterward tolde confessour mayster reymound thaughte many conuersaunt lesson generall rule whan temptacions arysen v sholde neuer dyspyse ne make question sayd fende seketh v falle questyons wyth hym trusted soo hyely grete sotelte malyce sholde ouercome v wyth sofystycall resons whiche sholde make questyons wyth hym ne answere questyons shall tel ensample ryght chast woma hir husbonde sholde answere sotelte maundes wonteth make rather bowe awaye hym yf wolde escape synne ryght sowle whiche coniuncte oure lorde chaste loue sholde neuer make questyons ne answere questyons fende cursed auout er enemye rather tourne deuoute prayer commaunde lorde consente sotell demau de vertu deuoute prayer stedfaste faythe maye ouercome alle sotell temptacions fend thus wyse holy mayde crystis spouse ouercome enemye soo cesyd kynde temptacions agaynst tourned hym another abhomynable kynde temptacions brought afore likenesse wymmen medlyng togyders fowlest wy myght deuysed spekyng gyders foule dyshonest wordes soo moche cursyd company ranne abonte wyth yellyng cryeng stere suche abhomynable synnes p lorde god traueyle hadde sowle soo constreyned see thynge hadde moost abhomynacion al closed hir eyen stopped hir eren ther yet hadde another torment hir spouse lorde jhesu wonte vysyte hir comforte gracyously semed tyme ferre hyr nother vysybly ne vnuysybly shewed hyr helpe semed whyche hadde full grete sorowe hyr sowle cessyd hyr grete penaunce euer contynued ther inne deuoute prayer last bethought inspyracyon holy ghoost certeyne fleyte whyche tolde afterward hir confessour many eshe ther sotell temptacion fende happed sayde whyle deuoute feruour sowle leuyng oure lorde jhesu somme certeyne synne ellys newe sotyll temptacyons fende wexyth dull slowe whyle brought veray coldenesse moche somme vnwytty folke consyderyng ben destytute fro ghostly comfortes whiche wonte haue leue therfore theyr ghoostly excercyse wonte vse prayer medytacyons redyng holy comynycacyons penaunce doyng wheby made redy ouercome fende desyred thyng ellys crystys knyght sholde putte waye hys armour whiche wonte ouercome hys enemye wyse knyght lord jhesu cryste shold thus seeth hym self dull slouth colde deuocyon rather sholde contynue hys ghoostly exercyse nought make lesse rather encrece another thynge also thys mayde ferned lorde jhesu vsed saye hyr self edyfycacyon thou vyle wretchyd creature art thou worthy ony maner comfort lyffe host thou mynde thy synnes supposest thou thy self wretchyd syner nough trowest thou thou art escaped mercy lord fro euer lastyng dampnacyon therfore thou sholdest well apayed yu wretche though thou suffreddest peynes derkenes soule dayes thy f art thou thanne heuy sorowfull suffre suche peynes sythe goddes grace thou shalte escape endeles peynes wyth cryst jhesu wythout ony doubte thon shalt comforted endelesly yf thou suffre peynes pacyentely whether thou hast chosen serue lorde onely comforte thou mayst haue hym thys fyf nay conforte thou shalte haue hym blysse heuen therfore aryse vp cesse thy ghostly excercyse yu hast vsed rather encrece ther wyth thyse dartes mekenes holy mayde wounded provide kynge babylonye hyr enemy fende strengthed hyr self gretely wyth suche wyse wordes knoweleched hir confessour mayster reymond ther suche multytude fendes hyr chambre hyr semed sawe hyr eyen aboute styre hyr foule thoughtes synne fledde hir chambre tyme kepte hyr self chyrche thanne wonte alle pursued thyder theyr sotyll temptacyons yet neuerthelesse thought wolde folowe steppe saynt jerome fleenge hydyng hir self dale hylles eshewyng suche abhomynable temptacyons euer whan came home fro chyrche hyr chambre founde many multytude fendes inne seyenge vnhonest wordes doyng abhomynable dedys lecherye hir semed rennyng aboute hyder thyder ben passyng swarme flyes thanne took hir prayer longe prayed lorde vnto tyme heuysom compayne swaged somwhat fro theyre abhomynable temptacyons whan thyse wretched temptacyons contynued many dayes gydres tyme whan come fro chyrche hyr chambre fyll doune prayer sone ther appyred gladsome beme holy ghoost opened hyr sowle sholde haue mynde many dayes fore hadde asked lord vertue gyfte strengthe doctryne lord gyue hyr gete gyfte vertue strengthe anone vnderstode meuynge foule temptacyons fende conceyued ther grete gladnesse lord gyue hir suche strengthe ouercome purposed euer afterwarde suffre mekely gladdely suche heuysom temptacion maner dyseases loue hyr spouse one fendes bolder thanne ony wycked spake holy mayde thys wyse thynkest thou wretche thynkest thou euer kepe caytyf lyf knowe well shall neuer cesse payne heuy thy deth vnto tyme thou consente v holy mayde answerd hauyng minde doctryne whiche oure lorde taught seyeng thus haue chose payne refresshyng therfore harde suffre theym rather dylectable loue sauyour longe pleseth mageste shall suffre theym assone hadde sayde worde anone sodenlye abhomynable companye fendes vanysshed awaye confused grete vnspekable lyht heuen appieryd shynned alle chambre lyght apperyd lord jhesu cryste hynge vpon crosse whan shedde precious blode called holy mayde hym sayde myn owne doughter katheryn seest thou suffred heuy therfore suffre came nerre hyr another maner lyknesse comforte hyr thanke hyr gloryo victorye wonne thenne thyse wordes saint anthonye seyde hym thus lord jhesu thou whan sowle soo vexyd wyth suche fowle fylthy temptacions lord sayde agayne thy sowle thy herte thenne sayde agayn lorde sauyng alway thy trouthe reuerence thy mageste maye thou sholdest dwelle foule herte replete wyth soo many fylthy thoughtis vnclennes oure lorde sayde eftsones whether caused tho temptacions tho thoughtes thyn herte gladnesse sorowe delectacion weylynge answerde naye lorde grete soro weylynge lord sayde ne cause sorowe weylyng dwellyd thyn herte yf hadde thylke foule thoughte sholde hadde partyd thyne herte thou sholdest hadde dylectacion theym presence cause theymyslyked whan thou woldest hadde putte theym fro wyth dyplesaunce myghtest thou woldest thou weptyst sory thys made presente wythinforth wyth thyn herte defended thyn enemyes suffre wythout forthe troubled moche nedeful spedefull thyn helthe whan tyme bataylle fulfylled ended sente wyth forthe bemys lyght anone derkenes fendes fledde might abyde lyght whiche enfourmed last tho peyne full holsom wynne ghostely strengthe thou sholdest suffre theym paciently longe lykynge shyneth beme cause thou offredes thy selfe hertely suffre tho peynes paciently sowle therfore frely wyth drawe fro shewyng preserce therfore doughter hast soo trewely ouercome vertue thyne thou hast deserued grace thenne thou wenest wherfore fro tyme fortherward shall shewe famulyerly homely haue doo tyme vysyon ended belefte moche plente swetenesse noo penne may wryte ye full belefte herte syngulerly amerueylous swetenesse worde lord callyd doughter whan called myn owne doughter katheryne soo prayed confessour mayster reymoud wha euer wold calle wold vouche sauf calle wyse euyr swetenesse myght therby renewed sowle fro tyme fortherward oure lorde jhesu spouse wyth ryght homely apperyd ofte tymes whyle hym self allone whyle brought oure ladye blessyd moder wyth hym p whyle saynt domynyk ther whyle gyders p also somtyme brought wyth hym marie magdalene saynt johan euaungelyste saynt poule appostle moo suche lyked party came hym self allone spake wyth homely frende wolde speke wyth moste homely frende soo moche bothe gyders wolde walke vp doune chamber two relygyous men two clerkys seyng psalmes howres gydres knewe ofte tyme afterward mayster reymound confessour full ferefully merueylous thynge merueylous shewyng homely neuer hath herde afore neuertheles maydens ye nede doubte therof yf ye mekely inwardely consydere depthe goodnes lorde eueryche chosen soules gyueth somme synguier gyfte grace wherof maye haue excellent joye aboue heythe souereygne magnyfycence apperyd sayntes onys eueryche hym selfe somme synguler grace ryght sene daye yt one man lyke another hathe somme maner dyfference ryght soo eueri saynte heuen hath somme dyffere ce synguler grace gyuen god fro therfore merueylle gretely though somme speciall grace bee seyde one founde therof cause haue rehersyd seynge ther psalmes shall tell maydens holy maide lerned rede techyng man woman lerned neuer tolde one hir cofessoure mayster reymond hadde desired kunne hyr mattyns therefore tyme prayed one hyr susters gete b c teche knowe lettres hadde traueylled sore many wekes gydres dyde spende tyme aboutes knowe lettres myght come therto bethought complayne oure lorde heuely mayster myspendyng tyme prayeng hym wolde vouchesauf teche yf lykynge hym spendefull soo kunne rede ellys lorde thy wylle done inow yf lykyng ye symple lyuyng spende tyme holy medytacions merueylous thynge hadde soo soone endeth prayer coude rede lyuelye psalmes redely hadde ben ony kunnyng clerke whan confessour perceyued gretely astonyed moche coude spelle ne knowe vnnethe noo lettre whiche ordeyned god supposed merueyllous token mayde gate bokes goddes seruyse saye ther matyns howrys theri amonge verse sayde marked verse euery houre begynneth wyth deus adiutorium meum intende ne adadiuuandum festina kept verse specially mynde lyues ende ofte tymes wolde reherce yt soone encresyd soule merueylously perfeccion contemplacion thenne cessyd lytyll vocall prayer bycause soo ofte tymes rauysshed heythe contemplacion soo ferforth cause suche ofte rauysshyng myght ofte tymes perfourme ne make ende pater noster sowle rauysshed fro outward wyttes shall declare afterward helpe god thus shall make ende chapytre conteyned therin confessur knowleche pryuely somme relacion tolde hadde tolde another self edyfycacio p merueylous disponsacyon wyth whiche weddyd faythe lorde wyth rynge capitulum duodecium holy mayde encrecyd profyted day daye grace vertu came holy desyre sowle praye lord gyue perfyte degre feyth whiche fayth myght able hym oythouten ony chaungynge thenne fore anone forthe prayed lord wolde vouchesauf encrece fayth make perfyte shold neuer hurte ne throwe doune violence ony maner aduersarye ouce lorde answerd wyse shall dyspouse faythe yet prayed often tymes aftyrward euer hadde answere lorde agayn laste happened lytyll fore begynnyng lente dayes ye peple made ende eting offlesshe manere made veyne ydil festys seruyng wombe thys holy mayde closid hyr vp hyr chambre sekyng fastyng prayen ge gloryus gracious face hyr spouse hu axyng specyaly feruent prayer vncessablythe axid afore vertu fayth wolde vouchesauf encrece make perfyggt lord apperid sayde cause thou hast putt awaye flelde maner nf vanytes etyng slesshe thyse dayes loue sette dylectacion thyn herte fully tyme aboute namely hous thou dwellest maken festys ioyen therin shall therfore make solempne feste dispousacion betwene sowle behyte shal dispouse faith lord soo soone sayde wordes lady gloryous moder hys blessyd euangelyste saynt johan gloryous appostle saynt poule saynt domynyke fader relygion apperyd wyth theym dauyd prophete brengyng honde sauter musyke p fyrst blessyd lady goddes moder came holy mayde toke honde holi honde stret chyng fyngers sone prayleng hym wolde vonchesuf wedde mayde hym feythe whiche deuoute axynge oure lorde graunted brought forth rynge arayed rounde aboute wyth foure precious margarete stone ouer parte rynge enclosyd ryght fayre dyamant stone rynge put holy honde vppon fyngre maydens ryght honde seyeng thus loo dyspouse thy maker thy sauyour faith whiche disposycion shall confermed kept vndefouled vnto tyme yu shalt halowe euerlastynge weddyng wyth blesse heuen therefore douhter fro tyme fortherwarde worke myghtely put awaye maner doubte thou arte armed strengthe feith ouercome therby thyn aduersaryes thus gracio visio cessyd euer afterward rynge bylefte vp holi maydes fynger folkes syht owne syght knewe many tymes ofte confessour maister reymound wyth grete drede fere sawe euer rynge vppon fyngre neuer tyme sawe loo maydens ryht saynt katheryn martyr virgyn quene baptym dyspoused lorde ye legende maketh cion ryght ye maye consydre holy mayde katheryn many victoryes temptacions flesshe solemply dyspoused lorde ye consydre coudycyons rynge ye shall welle see tokene acordeth betokeneth axed stedfaste feythe strenger dyamaunt stone wythston dyth maner hardenesse persyth hardest thynge stone self broke onely blode goote ryght soo stronge feythfull herte wythstondeth ouercometh wyth strenthe alle maner aduersyte mynde crystys precious blood whiche called holy wryte goote whiche precious blode shadde vpon crosse mankynde stroge herte lentyd al broste four precious margarete stonys rynge betokenyth noo thynge elli foure purytres clenes yt whiche holy mayde clennes hyr entente clennes hyr thouyt clennes hyr speche clennes hir workynge alle thyse shall declared grace god largely aftyrwarde supposo thys dyspousacion thynge ellys confirmaciou godis grace token thys gracyous confyrmacion ye rynge whiche apperid none cause shold fere ne drede delyuer owte wretched worlde prayer helpe special grace god hadde endowed wyth one ye princypall cause holy doctours ye almyghty god vouchesauf synguler preuylege shewe ben plesaunt hym estate grace wycked world worshyppe entent sende fyght wyth wycked world worshyppe holy name helthe soules dyde appostlis wytsondaye whiche token specyal tokenes grace ryght soo hooly mayde aboue condycion alle wymmen tyme thus confermed grace sente openli wourshyppe god procure helthe sowles shall bee declared helpe god afterward openly therfore trowe toke lorde token confyrmacio grace sholde boldely myghtely doo execucion lorde commaunded thus shall make ende chapytre fyrst parte legende hooly mayde saynt katheryn scene worship holy trynyte helthe sowles regnaute semper oi scis domino nostro ihesu cristo qui cum patre almo que spuisco viuit et regnat deus per oia secula seculorum amen p begynneth second partye whiche shewed conuersacion holy mayde men gyftes whiche hadde receyued oure lorde pryuyly enclosed wythin openly shewed worlde fyrst oure lorde bad sholde conuersaunt amonges men capitulum prymum tyme holy mayde despoused rehersed afore lorde began drawe litill lytyll conuersacion men full mennerly mesurably wythdrawe vtterly fro dyuyne presence rather moche longeth mesure perfection encrese shall declared openly afterward therfore tyme whan appyred hadde taughte kyngdom heuen shewed many mysteryes also seye psalmes houres dyuyne serui ce rehersed afore forthwith bad sholde go doune mete moders housholde afterward sholde come agayn whan holy mayde herde sobbyd wepte fyll doune feete sorowe fayde hym thyse wordes swete ihesu lorde puttest yu awaye fro yf haue offendyd displesyd mayster loo lord myn body thyn foot punysshe shal gladly helpe therto suffre good lord punysshed wyth sharpe soo hard payne departed ony maner wise fro thin blissed presence haue doo wyth mete haue mete knewe whether receyueth anone lyf bodely mete ghostely mete lorde thou knowest well haue fledde conuersacion men myght sonner fynde sythe haue founde mercy graciously thou haste shewed though vnworthy sholde nowe forsake precious tresour put conuersacion men eftsones soo ben founde reprobable faythe nay lord suffer soo thyne infynyte goodnes wha thus longe wepte weyled wyth swete sobbyng wordes oure lorde sayde suffre dere doughter full semely thou shodeste fulfylle maner vertu fruytfull thyn self also myn specyall grace myn entent dysceuere departe ony maner wyse rather shall haue strenger medytacions neyghbours charyte knewest thou well thise two thynges scondeth perfection myn commaundementys loue god loue thyn neyghbour wil therfore thou wyll fulfylle verof thyse two preceptis thou may go heuen wyth one wynge wyth tweyne haue doughter thin yonge age thou hast hyther yele loue helthe sowles hathe encresyd moche thyn yonge age thou purposed feyne aman cause thou myghtest sonner receyued amonge order fryer prechours straunge contrees yu sholdest knowen soo prouffyte helthe mennys soules yt synguler loue thou haddest myn seruaunt domynyk thou desyrest wyth grete honour habyte thou hast receyued whiche domynyk pryncypally helthe soules ordeyned order merueylest thou wey lest thou soo yf brynge thou hast soo longe desyred wyth thyse wordes lord holi maide gretely comforted sayde vnto hym lyke gloryous lady gloryous vyrgyn marie sayde gabriel suche wordes qno fit istud good lord wyse maner may done lord sayde agayn myn goodnes shal dyspose ordeyne thene good dyscyple trewe folower mayster cryste ihesu sayde lord thyn wyl done thynges derkenes thou art lyght nought thou art ought vnwis thou art endeles wysdom ye fader yet praye lord maner wyse may yu seyste wretche soo freell shold soo profytable mannys soule thou knowest well lord men setten lytyll store woman wordes speke ye neuer vertuously semely ne lyuest thou wymmen sholde conuersaunt amonges men lorde answerd maner gabryell answerd oure gloryous lady gloryous vyrgyn mary sayd none word cometh fro goddes mouthe vnpossyble hym done whiche hathe made mankynde bothe man woman shappe euery eyther wyl enspyre myn grace al one man woman necke agayn kynde cryeng one maydes susters sholde cese lefte tyme spyryte restoryd agayne bodely wyttys felte necke soo sore thought smyten wyth many grete strokys hooly mayde tolde afterward confessour maister reymou de yf moder hadde put neuer lytyll strengthe dyde ryghting necke aboute shold haue broken necke suche maner passyng body sowle holy mayde ofte tymes rauysshyng whyle vyolens spyryte body lefte vp fro erthe marie magdalene tyme rauysshyng shall declared afterward openly p shall tell myracle befyll begynnynge rauysshyng befyl tyme whan hooly mayde tournyd spete broche wyth flesshe fyre hote brenning cole sowle enflamed brente mene whyle wyth fyre holy ghoste anone rauysshed fro bodely wyttes seasyng ye tyme tournyng spytte wha brother wyf whiche callyd lysa perceyued knowyng condycions holy mayde toke spytte honde lete alone whan mete ynow also folke suppyd yet bylefte sarauysshyng thenne lysa bethought abyde vpon vnto tyme hadde doo brought husbond bedde chyldren came agayn aspye dyde founde falle doun hote brennyng cole wyth lysa weyled cryed sayde ala ala katheryn alle brennyd ran anone pullyd fyre founde clothes nothyng hurt ne brente ne hauynge noo maner tastyng fyre ne yet ouer bylefte nomaner asshes vpon clothes loo perceyue ye maydens vertu gostely fyre wythin maydes sowle who myght strengthe outward naturall fyre vtterly wytdrawe see ye myracle chyldren whiche caste ouen brent thenne renewed holy mayde myracle onys shewed ofte tymes p onys befyll chyrche fryer whan soo rauysshed bowed hede doune pyler mene whyle whiche pyller certeyne ymages dyuerse sayntes reuerens whiche sayntes man styked vp waxe candell brennyng whiche candell fyll doune vppon thys holy maydes hede tyme rauysshyng soo brennyd vppon hede tyme candell wasted soo harme merueylous thynge wounderfull ye candell brennyd vpon hede till wasted hurte nothynge kerchies p whan candell brente quenchyd vpon hede though hadde quenchyd vpon stone vppon erthe p myracle bare wytnesse many susters sawe tolde afterward confessour mayster reymound one susters whiche sawe called lysa another alyxa thyrde francisca yet besyde befyll lyke vnto dyuerse place worlde came namely whan aboute edefye menys sowles vertu fend malyce gretely stered agaynst sufferauce god soo ferforth presence many goddes seruauntes kast fyre whyles aboute drawe wyth wepyng weylyng smyled vpon theym come fyre selfe nothynge hurte neyther body ne clothes thenne sayde theym stode aboute beeth thynge aferde myn ghostely enemye fende hath doo myracle recordeth dyuerse sawe mayster reymound confessour p another tyme also chambre bi beddes syde erthen panne wyth brennynge cole whiche brennyng cole enuyous fend caste wyth suche strengthe hede fyrst fyll fyre panne braste vyolence stroke yet hed noo wyse hurte arose vp sayde wyth smilyng deuoute woman whiche callyd gabryell loo malycions enemye werketh lyke ride vitas patrum woman callyd infracia therfore none merueyle though lord suffer fende werke suche thynges derlynges chosen chyldren sythen suffred hym werke harde thinges persone wha suffred hym sette hym vpon pynacle temple vppon hye hylle p tus suche merueylous thynges lord wrought merueylously hys mayden katheryn soo encresyd grace euery daye perfection moche loue bothe rote cause werkys charytable werkisof neybours passed werkys charytable werkys double wyse bothe body soule p fyrst shall telle dedis charyte mercy dyde neyghbours syke body afterward dedes charyte mercy dyde theym seke sowle nexte chapytre shal declare openly dyuerse merueylys lorde shewed helyng poure folke also merueylous charyte shewed nemptis hem seke body wytnesse chapytre rehersed wythin chapyter p woundres whiche dyde helthe comforte necessyte theym poure nedy capytulum iij whan holy mayde katherin perceyued yt mylder neyghbours gracyous syghte spouse ihesu applyed euer afterward socour helpe theym nede wyth herte largely p cause wolde nothynge haue owne owne owne possession ryght relygyous woman hadde ordeyned owne herte kepe iij pryncipall vowes relygyon rehersed afore fyrst party lest sholde founde gylty withdrawynge mennys good ye hauer wente fader besoughte hym mekely lowely wolde gyue leue gyue almesse conscyence ore folke goodis god gyue hym housholde whiche fader graunted frely moche knowe well folowynge perfyghtly steppe graunted oonly thus pryuyte bytwene theym bothe also afterward housholde gaue commaundemente noo body sholde lette dere doughter gyue almesse suche goodes lord hadde gyue hym housholde though wolde gyue poure folke euer hadde hys housholde assone hadde lycence began departe goodes fader poure folke neuerthelesse moche lyued wyth gyfte dyscrecion departed good alle wolde aske theym knewe nede folke alle though asked amonge nedy folke came two knowleched many poure nedy housholders lytyll besyde cyte gene grete nede sore ashamed aske tyme knewe forgate arose vp erly ye morowe saynt nycholas dyde bare sholders home house bothe wyne oyle thynges nedefull god wolde whan came founde dory ope put wythin dores brought drewe dore fledpreuyly waye p befyll tyme seke body soo fro sole fote toppe hede body swollen myght aryse vp bedde ne stonde fete herde saye poure wydowe lytyll besyde whiche grete hunger greate nede wyth sone doughters compassyon hadde poure woman chyldren nexte nyght prayed oure lorde wolde vochesauf gyue soo moche strengthe tyme yt myght goo oour poure woman anone aroos vp erly vpon morowe fylled sacke faders grete vessell flacat wyne another vessell wyth oyle myght euer fynde besyde forth whiche myght bee necessarye mannys lyuelood thyse kept chabre eueryche thyse berdem ynow alone yet bare onys wedowes hous somme therof trussed vpon sholders somme vp ryght arme somme vp lift arme somme therof bonnden onder gyrdell myracle heuy ynouht bere eueryche hym self bare alle onys esely without ony peyne greuau ec knowleche ward bothe confessour mayster reymoud fryer berdom wayde nomore thought hadde lifte vp lytyll wase strawe yet trouthe yf hadde trewely wayed sholde haue wayed hondred pound weyte aboute er comyn bell cyte roungen erly morowe lefull neuer one walke cyte aft tyme ronge holy mayde waited well tyme toke journeye wyth burthen yonge forbolnyd bysekenes yet ranne poure wydowed hous faste though hadde felt nothynge paynes ne burthen wha came nyghe poure wydowes hous byrthen waxit heuy greuo bere soo semed myght bere paas whan perceyued vnderstoode anone yt oure lordes wyll prayed deuoutly wyth truste wolde vouchesaufe ese anone esyd byrthen came poure wydowes hous founde dore half open preuyly coude drewe byrthen wythin dore yet made suche noyse woke wydowe fledde myght sekenes full ferre sekenes encresyd ordeynaunce god vnnethes myghte remeue waye wherfore spak lord wyth wei lyng chere maner smylyng chere sayde good lord hast thou dysceyued good shame thy wyll myn foly bee pupplysshed folke aboute hast thou forgete thy mercy yu haste shewed thyn vnwourthy praye lord yelde myn strengthe maye come home myn chambre tyme spake thus thyse wordes lyke thyse enforced strengthed self myght go forthe seyeng owne body thus thou moost nedes forthe though thou sholdeste deye waye therfore goo forth wyth goynge wyth crepyng forth wet lytyll soo fer poure wedowe arose vp aspyed habyte dyd benefet p oure lord thenne consydered gretely tourmentyd goyng restoryd agayne strengthe hadde afore soo perfyghtely wyth grete hardynes came home er thenne lyght daye laye doune bedde ryght feble dyde thus oure lorde touched touched sekenesse hym lyked loo maydens ye maye see myracles saint nycholas renewed holy mayde myracle many myracles shall procede forth shewe vertuous lyuyng saynt martyn lord shewed hym p befyll tyme whan holy mayde chyrche freyers came poure man asked somme helpe loue god holy mayde perceyued wel hadde nothynge myght gyue hi wonte neyther golde ne syluer prayed hym wolde abyde whyle tyll came home gladly wolde plenteuously gyue almes suche thynges yt hadde home houshold thenne ye poure man sade yf thou haue ony thyng gyue praye gyue may abyde long suppose another yt apperyd poure man lykenes semed holy mayde sholde goo fro somwhat bethought myght gyue hym fulfylle nede anone came mynde lytyll syluer crose hynghe bodyes yt whiche tyme honde pulled away lytyll crosse gaue gladly poure man whan poure man crosse wente awaye fro gladly asked nomore almes ye day none though come crosse alone nexte nyght folowyng whan holy mayde prayed wounte almyghty god oure sauyour apperyd hauyng lytyll crosse blessyd honde arayed wyth mani precious stone sayde doughter knowest thou crosse mayde answerde hym sayde knewe well sayde soo fayre araied wha lord sayde yesterday thou gauest gladly wyth grete charyte loue whiche loue charyte betokeneth thyse precious stone therfore behote daye dome afore alle ye companye angel men shall shewe encrece thy ioye shall hede ne suffre hyd dedes mercy ben doo wyth lorde cesyd aperycion thanked ourlord euer steryd doo suche almesse well proued afterward another daye also befyll whan deuyn seruice doo fryer tyme peple goo chyrche bylefte behynde alone wyth one susters praye came dounward fro chapell whiche ordeyned susters penaunce oure lord apperyd lykenesse poure pylgrym age semed ij iij thyrty yere half naked asked wolde gyue hym clothes loue god theene tyme steryd doo dedes mercy euer prayed poure man wolde abyde whyle vnto tyme came doune agayn fro chapell thenne wolde helpe hym somme clothes wente vp agayn chapell dyde herk ertyll vnder whiche kertell wered nexte body cote wythout sleues gaue wyth greate gladnes poure man tyme poure receyued asked sayde good lady praye sythe ye haue gyue wollen clothe gyue lynen clothes nexte myn body thenne sayde hym come thou shalt houe gladly went fore hir spouse thesu vnknowyng pylgryme lykenes folowed whan came home went thyder lynen clothes fader brother layen brought bothe sherte lynen clothes toke gladly poure pylgrym yet whan poure man hadde receyued asked prayed wolde gyue hym sleues kertyll couer armes p wyth wente nothynge heuy crawyng gladly sought aboute sleues laste founde newe cote mayden seruaut hous hauyng hangyng vpon perche whiche neuer werid ther toke awaye sleues toke gladly poure man yet asked sayde lady thou hast clothed thanke who loue yu hast doo yet haue felawe lyeng hospytall besyde whiche nedeth gretely clothes ye wyll sende hym ony clothes shall bere hym byhalue full gladly yet hooly mayde multyplyeng askynge neuer weryer rather feruent almes largely thought hyr mygth haue clothe clothe wyth nedy man yt lyeth hoospytall thenne fyll hyr mynde meyne hou solde ryght lothe geuen almes take hyr fadre allone therfor ye shytte vp alle clothes vnder lok keye lest sholde fynde gyue almes ouermore consydered dyscretely take nogh awaye mayden seruaut housholde therfore wolde take awaye nomore hyres cause nedy hyr selfe thanne dysputed wyth hyr self whrther sholde gyue hym hyr owne cote cause hadde noo moo one charyte sayde yes hone ste sayd nay atte last charyte oueroo honeste say charyte longeth sowle ouercome honeste whiche hadde compassyon vpon body thought yf pour man shold go awaye wythout somme clothe shold slaunderous yf gyuen hyr owne coote goo naked sholde hadde slandred sowles who soules ought loue body therfore hir semed sowles shold slaundred wyse temporall almes thanne answered poure man thus trewely dere frende yf honest lefull gyue cote thou sholdest haue gladdely cause haue moo semely sholde gyue awaye thys therfore praye holde excused gladdely wolde gyue yf hadde ony moo thenne poure man smyled vpon hyr sayd well lady see well yf thou haddest moo thou woldest gladdely gyue therfore thanke fare well whanne borned fro hir holy mayde perceyued certeyn sygnes sholde whiche wonte appere hir often tymes conuersaunt wyth hyr manere doubte hyr herte brenned loue neuerthelesse moche helde hir self comyne occupacyon housholde wonte next nyght suyng lord jhesu cryste appered hyr prayed lykenes poure man holdyng hys honde cote holy mayde gaf hym arayed wyth clere shynyng precyous stone sayd hyr thus dere doughter knowest thou dote answered sayd yes gaf arrayed whome lord sayd ageyne thou gauest yester daye cote frely charytable voyded awaye fro peyne colde therfore shall gyue cote whiche shall inuysyble men shall sensyble myn holy body shall take hyue whiche bothe thy body thy sowle may keuered kepte noyous colde vnto tyme yt shall arayed ioye wythout ende fore sayntes angel anone forth wyth toke clothe sangueyne colour wyth hys holy hondes wounde syde shynyng alle aboute quantyte mesure maydens bodye wyth arayed hyr wyth hys owne holy hondes sayd thys clothe gyue whyle thou dwellest erthe token thy clothe ioye thou shalt arayed wythin heuen thus vysyon cessyd holy mayde hadde soo grete grace receyuyng ghostly gyfte onely hir sowle also hir body fro houre hyr endyng daye neded neuer moo clothes wynter thanne somer wedder neuer colde vsed mo clothes cote kertell euer afterward semed felte ghostly cote vpon hyr whiche lord gaf hir cause felte colde see ye maydens worthynes holy mayde folowed saynt nycholas gyuyng atmespryuely folowed saynt martyn gyuyng hyr owne clothes whiche lord allowed hys holy apperyng thys blessyd mayde gaf hyr sensyble euerlastyng token fele erthe plesaut almes dedes ben hym semeth whan lorde sayd thys holy mayde wolde hyr lytell crosse daye dome whiche gaue almes also wolde araye hyr wyth clothe ioye heuen thyng ellys sikernes endeles helthe therto excellent ioye blysse hir mede therfore maydens sett lytell suche reuelacyons suche tokenes sykernesse endeles helthe onely causeth grete ioye grete comforte sowle impossyble tongue tell penne wryte foloweth suche sykernesse ioye trowe ye sowle trewely encrece vertue pacyence strengthe temperaunce besynesse delygence kepyng hyr self holy werkes feyth hope charytr suche vertues harde suche soule fore ben made suche comfort ryght esye loo grace suche predestynacyon notefyed clene sowle wercheth another tyme also befyll thys holy mayde fulfylled wyth compassyon perceyued ther man whiche made pore wylfully goddes loue lacked mete wherfore toke preuely lynnen bagge fylled wyth egges bare wyth hyr preuely vnder hyr oote refresshe wyth poure man whan mette wyth came place poure dwellyd entred fyrst chyrche besyde praye whan entred bethought lord inwardly anoue spiryte rauysshed soo fully tyme wythdrawe hyr outwarde wyttys rehersed afore whanne thus rauysshed happed sodeynly body bowed pyler casuelly syde egges lened fully vpon bagge wyth egges thanne ther bagge goten fore thymbyll tayllours sowen wyth whiche thymbyll broken thre partyes burthon hir body eyren charyte hyd hole noo partye broken thys meruayllous thyng eyren hole thymbyll coper broke lorde shewed hys myracle charytable eyren lord shewed helpe holy mayde nedy folke also shewed hys myracle hyr werkes godhede declare openly shall tell meruaylles thyng whiche meruayll wytnes bothe men woman aboute nombre xx maydens faders housholde moder lapa tolde mayster reymond hir doughters confessour tyme hir doughter thys holy mayde leue hyr fad gyue almes befylle meyne housholde dronke amonges certeyn vessell wyne remenaut whiche lefte fresshe gyue poure men asmoche custome gyue beste goddes loue went hyr next vessell wyne besyde hyr faders seller tamed poure folke gaf largely ther euery day neded many dayes gyder aspyed meyne last whan fyrst vessell done boteler mynystred drynke meyne vessell whyche holy mayde tamed yet holy mayde left therfore alwaye gaue ther poure folke ye meyne dronke largely gaue poure folke aspyed ne wyne neuer vnfressher ne neuer lasse vessell allewaye kepte estate bothe fulnesse fresshenesse alle meyne housholde gretely meruaylled ther vessell contynued long wyne good fresshe well knowe fore suche vessell wyne myght laste ouer xv dayes xx dayes ferthest neuerthelesse contynued onely xx dayes full moneth complete yet semyd vessell noo wyse lessened meyne meruayll ther yt wyne good fresshe lastyd long better wyne semed tastyd neuer vnknowe myght holy mayde knewe well nogh yt myracle lord cause almes gaue ther largely poure folke therfore gaue ther largely pour folke openly meyne myght see yet semed neuer lesse vessell moneth passyd began entre yet wyne contynued euer lyke fresshe lyke full dyd fyrste tyme grape rype make newe wyne whenne g ape rype vessellys ordeyned fylled wyth newe wyne mayster wyne bad commauded vessell whiche cotynued long wyth olde wyne sholde emptyed fyllyd newe wyne one seruautes made ordynauce empte vessell fyllyng botellys yet semed neuer lesse atte laste vessell vndone gawgid knowe ther lefte vessell founde drye though ther wyne ther inne many monthes afore thenne housholde amexuaylled ye myracle thenne habundaunce wyne afore loo maydens myracle lord shewed gyuyng almes dede holy mayde katheryne whiche myracle openly afterward knowen cyte sene thus endeth chapytre wyttenesse thys mater conteyned thys chapytre ben rehersed thys chapytre p meruayllous dedys whiche dyd lowely besy seruyse syke capitulum iiij thys holy mayde meruayllous compassyon hyr soule poure folke nedy yet hadde excellent meruayllous pyte seke folk whiche pyte hadde wroughte many wonder thynges shall rerce grace god edyfycacyon theym whiche shall rede thys holy legende though seme somme incredyble yet shall leue therfore cyte sene ther full poure womman syke nede wantyng temporall gooddes constreyned lygge hospytak cyte supposed haue fynde remedye hyr syknes myght haue hyr self happed thanne receyued poure hospytall cyte whiche hospytall vnnethe myght haue nedyd hyr sykenesse encrecyd hyghely lepre tho ugh hyr body thenne euer wyth inne hospytall eshewed hir te dysposed sholde sente spytellhous wythout toune whyche ordeyned lazaros abyde amonges whanne thys holy mayde perceyued thys wente full charyte hospytall vysyted poure leprous womman mynystred hyr onely substaunce temporall gooddes also helpe hyr owne mynystracyon euery day morowe euery nyght euen vysyted seek womman hyr owne persone consyderyng leprous womman hir spoust jhesu hyr ghoostly eye therfore serued besely dylygentely mekely thys holy mayde serued hyr prude vnkynde seek womman ageynst hyr ofte tymes happeth ben meke mekenes ther shewed proude sholde thanke lord kyndnes whiche shewed shewe rather iniuryes wronges ryght dyd thys seke womman holy mayde whan saw serued soo customably euery day thys holy mayde began chyde hir whanne serued hyr plesaunce befyll whyle thys holy mayde longe chyrche contynued somtyme longer thenne somtyme cause ofte tyme taryed fro seek woman whan came late seek woman wolde chyde hyr shappely sayde hyr soornfully many suche heuy wordes lady quene welcome haue ye ben longe lady quene ye grete lady long haue ben frerys haue ye talkyd nough wyth freres lady wyth suche lyke wordes many lyke dyd coude styre thys holy mayde wrath yet styred hyr wordes rather serued hyr wolde hyr owne moder comforted hyr lowely mekely wolde hyr owne moder seynge hyr ryght thus good moder goddes loue dyspleased wyth though haue longe shall mende thyng anone hyd hyr fast made fyre ordeyned besyly hyr mete necessaryes wolde hyr owne moder soo seke womman hyr vnpacyence meruaylled hir pacyence thys rebukynge contynued longe tyme yet holy mayde neuer wery hyr seruyse rather contynued many folk meruayll therof hyr owne mod lapa gretely troubled wyth al cryed vpon hyr sholde leue minystracion lest lepre ye seke woma oftymes sayd hir doughter wote well thou shalt leper yf thou contynue seruyce seke woman may suffer therfore leue charge holy mayde excused honestely sayde hadde oure lord sholde leue minystracion poure woman soo e ed moder contynued forthe hooly mynystracion thenne fende perceyued myght bee ouercome swete reuelyng tourned hym another whyle suffraunce oure lorde made hondes leper whiche touched leper body seke woman soo ferforth euery body yt sawe sayd leper yet wold sece thefor rather desireth leper se e holy ministracio despysed owne body rought neuer befyll mightserue lord leper sekenes contynued vppon many dayes semed full fewe daye comparyson grete loue hadde lord blessyd lord whiche tournyd thynge god louers tyme consyderyd ghostely strengthe spouse holy mayde wolde suffer leper sykenes sholde longe endure wythin lytyll tyme afterward happed dysposycyon lord leper woman sholde passe worlde soo tyme passynge holy mayde wyth comforted besely blessydly p whan passed wasshed deuotly lepres body arayed berynge whan dyryge masse done beryed wyth owne hondes assone buryed leper passed awaye fro hondes though hadde neuer ne sykenesse therof rather hondes fayrer afterward thenne ony place body though hadde neuer touched wyth ony spyce lepre see ye maydens encrece vertue hooly mayde wan dede mercy charyte moder vertu stererd doo charytable dede mercy mekenesse conpeled charyte whiche made bee subiecte seruaunt seke also pacyence conpeled wyth charyte whiche made suffre pacyently gladly seke wommans rebukynge p yet ferthermore dede charyte knytte wythouten ony doughte sekernesse clere faythe whiche faythe behelde euer spouse jhesu sowle ofte mynystred woman p yet neuertheles failed none hope whiche contynued laste ende holy mynystracyon alle thyse hooly company vertues folowed open myracle clensyng lepre dethe poure woman whiche toke mynystracyon gracious myracle merueylous yet sholde ye see merueylous thinge folowed yf ye lysten besely cyte gene susters penaunce saynt domynyk seke yt whiche called maner speche ye coutre palmaria ye suster palmaria gretely styred hate excytacion ye fende agaynst holy mayde katheryn yt ofte euer sawe herd herd speke herd speke hyghely troubylyd sowle soo ferforth shewed alle tokenes malyce agaynste bothe ba bytyng pryuyly openly also cursyng assone holy maide perceyued shewed alle maner myldenes mekenes pee coude alway seke suster despysed mekenesse vtterest sette none pryce bi thenne holy mayde ranne prayer wyth feruent deuote herte lorde ihesu spouse prayeng hym specyally seke suster wold vouchesauf gyue grace forgyuenes prayer brennyng fyre ascendynge vp lorde askyng bothe mercy dome bee entent holy mayde nothyng ellys aske mercy ne dome yet lykyng lorde tyme gyue hys mercy wythout dome shewed oure lorde hys grete dome yf byrrayers holy mayde shewed gretter mercy smote mercyably suster palmarya body soule shol made hole hardynes obstinacion seke suster swetenes charyte agaynst spouse katheryne clerely shewed afterward ryghtwysdom euermore encresyng holy mayde katheryn loue sowles shewyng wonderfull fayrnes susters soule whiche fyrst ye ryght wysdome hym demed bee dampned ob ynacie merytes prayer hooly mayde afterward saued whan lorde hadde smyte suster palmarya body bodely sekenes entent onely soule shold hole yet wolde sece malycyous hate shewed wythout cause holy mayde rather greuo sekenes thenne hele froward holy mayde mekenes wed agayn wold ofte tymes full charytably wyth seruyce wyth louyng wordes dedes p yet seke suster harder thenne ony stone agaynste neyther charytable wordes ne dedes ne seruyces wolde pesed euer grutchyng vpon soo ferforth bad goo hous inne wyth wood violent spyryt consyderyd lord rightwis iuge leyde honde ryghtwysnes vpon enmye charyte touched soo soo sodenly bothe wythout shryfte housell drewe faste deth body sowle whan holy may herd anone went chamber bysoughte lord deuout prayer soule lest sholde peryche occasyon suche wordes seyde oure lorde sowle tyme prayer afterward knowe confessour lord whyder wretche bore ende occasyon soules made lyke yt shold put endeles peynel wylt yu suffer lord yt occasyon endeles dapnacion myn suster sholde instrument euerlastynge helthe myn good lord put awaye suche orybyll dome sor multytude thyn grete mercy better neuer borne soulis bought precyous blod shold dampned lorde thyse thyne byhestes whiche thou behotest thy large mercy sholde profytable sowle hele myn neyghbours thyse fruytes helthe sholde brynge forth myn suster sholde dampned none douwte mynsynne cause therof payne fruyte brynge forth synne alone yet shall cese aske mercy vnto tyme haue somme comforte myn susters sauacion wyse hooly mayde prayed sowle thenne worde outward shold haue compassyo susters sowle lord shewed mischefs perile susters sowle inne comered wythinne syght oure lorde answerd sayde myght suffer ryghtwysnes suche malycious hate obstynate must nedes punysshed thenne holy maide fell doune fore oure lord prayer sayde lord shall go neuer place tyme thou hast shewed methy mercy suster punisshe lorde synne cause trespaas shold bee punisshed therfore merciable lord beseche thy grete mercy thyn endeles godenes yu suffer myn susters sowle goo body tyme haue receyued grace thy merci p loo maydens prayer grete strengthe suster soule myghte passe body vnto tyme oure lorde shewed plentuous mercy notwythstondynge seke woman lay adrawyng thre dayes thre nyghtes soo many folke knewe merueylled sorowed suffred soo longe peyne yet tyme holy mayde continued deuout prayer neuer cesing vnto tyme hadde ouercome maner lord meke teres e lorde deuout prayer graciously sent mercy vnto sowle gaue clere knowyng knowe trespas also gaue suffycient contrycion helthe sowle assone holy mayde perceyued reuelacion hadde suche grace wente ye seke susters chamber comforte whan seke suster sawe hooly mayde dyde reuerence wyth grete ioye myght whome first grete repreue soo accused self wyth spekynge token makyng asked mercy forgyuenesse trespaas myght speke soo shryue hoselyd passyd worlde wyth grete contrycion whan passed world thenne lorde shewed holy mayde sowle soo grete bryghtnesse fayrnes yt knowleched afterward confessour myght tolde ne spoken wyth mannys tongue yet fayrenesse sholde haue blysse endelesly oonly fayrenes hadde first creacion receyuyng baptysme thenne sayde lord hooly mayde loo dere doughter haue receyned soule yt loste thys fayre soule semely loo wyll doo besines wynnyng suche fayre sowle yf ye souerayn fayrnes cometh alle maner vertues fayrnesse oucome thrugh loue fairnesse manys soule yt wold come doun froheue erthe shedde blode rau som moche ye thenne shold laboure eyther ye fayr creature lost cause haue shewed soule yt yu may ye afterward erid wynne soules also thou may stere grace holy mayde thenne thanked lord blessyd reuelacion prayng hym mekely wyth alle affeccion sowle wolde vouchesaf gyue grace euer afterward myght see fayrnesse euery soule tho whiche conuersaunt wyth steryd winne helthe whiche grace oure lorde graunted sayde cause thou haste despised myn sake maner flesshely conuersacion art knytte spyryte whiche moost souerayn spyryte also haste prayed soo besely soo deuotily fore sowle therfore gyue thy soule clere syght whiche thou mayste perceyue beholde bothe fayrenes fylthes euery soule present afore thy bodely wittes afore tyme haue perceyued condycions bodyes ryght tyme forward thyn ghostely wyttes sholde perceyue consydere condition spyrytes tho whilche ben presented also who helpe thou shalt praye though neuer presented thy bodely syght p grace gyfte euer ward soo spedefull holy mayde fro tyme forward perceiued clerly qualytes dedes ye sowles theym whiche aperyd afore bodyes ferforth tyme mayster reymound confessour complayned grutched vppon cause suffred many dyuerse persones knele afore wolde byd theym stonde vp au terd wyse god knoweth fader occupyed aboute consyderacion sowles perceyued nothyng maner outward dedes thenne asked confessour sayde wheder ye see sowles answerd thus fader vnder confessyon shewe tyme sauyour hadde gyue suche grace sawe fayrnesse myn sufters soule whiche ordeyned dampned trespaas right wysdom delyuerd mercyable mym prayer shewed afterward fayrenes ther apperyd afterwar vnnethe afore sawe condycions theyr sowles therfore fader syker ye hadde onys seen fayrenesse resonable sowle ye wold suffre hondred tymes bodely deth possyble wynnyge soule nothyng wi worlde maye lykened fayrnesse wha ofessour herd prayed yt wolde vouchesaf tell hym processe come suche reuclacion thenne holy mayde tolde al processe reherced afore bee though tolde shortly kely trespas seke suster done agaynst confessour afterward enquyred sothe odyous cryme susters ye whiche knewe well ynow ferthermore cofyrmacion thyse thynges benrehersed fore maister reymound co fessour recordeth yt ofte tymes speker bytwene pope gregori xj ytaly coude vnd stonde none latyn pope gregorye coude vnderstonde none ytaly therfore mayster reymound confessour coude bothe speker bytwene amonges alle communycacions holy mayde communyd wyth pope gregory complayned court rome sayde paradyse sholde vertu ther founde stynche cursed vice thenne pope asked confessour longe hadde courte answerd sodenly wyth meke boldenes pope wyse worshyppe almyghty god dare well say perceyued moche stynche synne whiche vsed court rome home myn owne cyte borne thenne hath sinned synne euery daye thenne pope answere helde pea merueylously astonyed confessour maister reymound merueylously marked wordes wyth auctoryte spoken suche wourthy prelate also ofte tymes befyll bothe mayster reymound confessour folowed holy mayde dyuerse countrees neyther ne came afore yt ther come hym many vnknowen person semely arayed comin theym vertu semyng though hadde vertuous folke trouthe encombred wyth wretched synnes who synnes perceyued anone wherfore wolde neyther speke theym netourne face theym whan sawe abode lo ge thenne brake lytyll voyce wonte doo sayde theym suche wordes fyrst shold amende lyf fro synne goo deuyles seruyce thenne speke lord wha said suche wordes wente fro theym assone myght goodly afterward confessour felawes founde sothe e ncombred wyth wretched synnes whiche synnes co tynued wythouten repentaunce another tyme also spake wyth woman ye whiche woman semed honest woma soth concubyne man holi chirche grete pyte spake togyders wymmen myght loke vpon maiden face cause euer hooly mayde tourned awaye face fro thynge confessour hadde grete merueyle tyme asked dyde soo p whome answerd sayde fader syker ye hadde felt stynche synne felte ye wolde haue caste oute alle body sqweymusnes loo maydens thyse ensamples haue sett ye sholde knowe excellent gyftes grace lord gaue hooly mayde cause meke lyuyng p ouermore ghoostely enemye fend perceyuyng hooly mayde wan grete vertues seruyce dede seke folke thought somme maner wylle wythdrawe fro holy besynes yet myght aboute lette encresyd vertuously occupacion p befyl tyme one susters penaunce whyche called maner countree andred andred touched bi suffrau ce oure lorde wyth greuous infyrmyte thyse hadde vppon brest sore whiche called cancer fretid flesshe rounde aboute soo corrupte myght none come nyghe stynche yf hylde nose soo fewe none myghte suffre come nyghe p whanne hooly mayde perceyued vnderstoode oure lord receyued seke suster kepyng thenne anone came wyth glad comforted serued gladly laste ende sekenes seke suster toke seruyce freely moche consydered forsoke holy mayde lefte thynge vndo yt longyng seke suster encresyd neuer abhomynable stynche neuer moche stode opened wounde wasshed wepte coueryd yet neuer hyldeth nose noo stynche ne shewed none token lothsomnes ne neuer heuy ne wroth seruyce ne wery gladli dyd dilyget seruyce soo seke suster merueyle grete stedfastenes grete sufferaunce grete fulnes loue charyte yonge mayde grete loue charyte shewed seke suster ye fende grete enuye aboute lette dede mercy charyte power p fyrst vpon daye holy mayde aboute vnoouere wounde wasshe wype refreissh agayn came suche odoure stynche vnnethe stomake myght suffer almost brought vomyte assone perceyued arose agaynst self wyth hyghe wrathe sayde skeymons flesshe wyse whether ye wretched flesshe haste abhomynacion thyn suster whiche oure lorde boughte wyth precious blode yu mayste falle euery daye ye sykenesse verse trewely thou shalt punysshed therfore anone bowed done sore hyld nose mouthe open agaynst wounde soo longe vnto tyme felt selfe skeymousnes goo soo ouer came flesshe contrary spyryte seke suster behelde cryed merueylyng sayde cecedere doughter corrupte thy selfe wyth foule stynkyng sore p holy mayde alle cryenge wolde aryse vp vnto tyme felt enemye ouercome arose vp auoyded awaye fro tyme consyderyng myght haue maystry wrought wylyly agaynst seke suster put herte suche heuenes agaynst holy mayde lotheth seruyce lytyll lytyll malyce soo encresyd lothenes tourned hate though knewe well ynow none wolde serue yet cyd pryuy hate brake agaynst suspycious g losye condycion theym yt lyuen hate euer lyghtely leue suspycious thought hate laste began ymage ne bere honde whan present wyth aboute somme actuell synne flesshely somme preuy place p yet wold holy mayde neuer ce holy seruise aboute notwithstondyng suspycious ymagynacions put agaynst wel wylecome deuyll besy aboute wrathfull seke suster agaynst exortacion excitacion fende euer hated dedes charite moche steryd seke suster slander thys holi mayde openly ye filthe vnclene scland open last whanne came hir susters ryng somme oldest sted fastest cam thys seke suster knowe trouthe thanne seek suster sdaudred hyr fore ryght soo contynued sclaund hir susters accusyng hir full foule actuell vnclennesse whiche foule accusacy thyse sustres gretely meruaylled styred ageynst thys holy mayde called forthe fore sharpely rebuked wyth many repreuable wordes axyng hir wold suffre hyr self deceyued lese hyr maydenhode whome thys holy mayde answerd full pacyently softely seynge thus trewely ladyes sustres grace lord jhesu
