cryste mayde neuer wold say worde blamyng hyr accused hyr onely thus trewely mayde trewely mayde yet thys cessyd neuer hyr seruyse full heuysom hir suche wordes sclaundre yet fyrst serued hyr seek suster afterward went hir chab e praye hyr comforte suche dyseases prayed soule thenne wordes mouthe yt thys wyse almyghty god dere beloued spouse thou knowest well name maydes tender lyghtly catche sclaundre namely suche maydens haue chosen spouse ye cause thou woldest thy gloryous moder lady saynt mary commytted joseph called spoused hyr husbond kepe hyr name virgynyte wythout sclaunder thou knowest lord alle thys sclaundre whiche putte vpon come fende fader esynges cause sholde cesse besynes whiche haue begonne thy loue therfore lord praye helpe knowest well gylteles suffre thys wycked enemye whiche ouert rowe thy passyon haue maystrye whanne hadde prayed thus longe lord wepyng plenteuously oure lorde appyred hyr knowelechyd afterward confessyon hyr confessour mayster reymond holdyng ryght honde golden crowne arayed precyous margaryte stonys hys lyfte honde garlonde sharpe thornes seyng hyr thys wyse dere doughter nedefull yt thou crowned wyth owne thyse two crownes therfore chese whether thou hast leuer haue thys two ch se whether thou haddest leuer crowned wyth sha pe crowne thorne thys ly reserued euer lastyng lyf ellys haue precyous crowne haue ye thys lyfe thenne thys holy mayde sayde lord thou knowest well haue forsake myn owne wylle chosen thy blyssed wyll therfore dare chese maner thyng wythout thy plesaunt wyll neuerthelesse cause thou wylte shall answer say thus chese rather thys lyf euer co fourmed thy blessyd passyon soo suffre peynes thy loue thyse wordes anone toke lordes hondes garland thornes feruently put myghtely vpon hyr hede wyth maner ef vyolence thornys percyd hir hede rounde hir thought moche peyne long afterward hyr hede prykynge thornys recorded hir self openly mayster reymond hyr confessour sayd ford hyr thus poure al thyng haue suffred sclau der areysed ryght power cesse therfore thou shalt contynue holy seruyse thou hast gonne gyue stede sende wold let shall gyue full vntorye thyne enemye euer hath imagyned ageynst shall torne hys owne hede thy ioye hys peyne thus thys holy mayde comforted soo bode stylle holy seruyse whanne thys sclaundre cam hyr moder lapa yt seker ynough hyr doughter gretely styred thys sclaunder sayd hyr wyth myghty spyryte thys wyse doughter haue oft sayd thou sholdest nomore serue stynkyng woman loo reward hath gyue thy besye seruyse hath sclaundred full foule thy sustres yf thou euer serue hyr come hyr neuer shall calle ne name doughter afterward ne thou thy moder soty lest wyll ther fende myght haue maystrye hir sclaunde ryng hyr seek suster beganne wyth maner pyte lette hyr hyr holy seruyse hyr moders mouthe thenne thys holy mayde astonyed somwhat hir moders wordes last wente hyr knelyd afore hyr seynge hyr thus swete moder whether lorde wolde pleased yf leue vndone dedys mercy negyhbours theyr vnkyndenes whether sauyour lefte raunsom v suffryng deth crosse reprouyng wordes obloquye men god knoweth moder charyte also yf lefte thys seek suster wolde hir seruyse wolde none hir seruyse shold deye defau sholde cause occasyon hyr deth lytell deceyued ye fende perauenture afterward lorde wyll gyue hyr grace knowe hyr trespas suche wordes lyke thise laste wan hyr moders blessyng wente seek suster ageyn serued hir gladly though neuer sayd euyll hyr ke suster astonyed perceyued thenne amysse beganne haue sorowe contrycyon hyr herte hir sclaunder put vpon hir thenne lord shewed mercy hyr make good fame hys mayde shewed seek suster tyme laye hyr bedde gracious vysyon wouchesauf shewe thys holy mayde vpon daye whanne thys holy mayde wente hyr chambre hyr seruyse seek suster seek suster sawe laye hyr bedde aboute holy mayde grete lyght comyng heuen grete mirthe swetenes made hyr forgete vtterly hyr dyseases thys myght mene clerely wyst neuer loked aboute behelde maydes face transformed trasfygured hyr semed thenne katheryn lapais doughter rather lyke heuenly creature gloryfyed lyghte beclypped hyr rounde aboute behelde hyr yelde hir self gylty hyr sowle lorde sclaunder putt vpon holy mayde whanne thys vysyon hadde tary whyle whiche appyred bodely eyen seek suster came passyd awaye whiche passyng seek suster long comforted also sorowfull trespas anone axed mercy holy mayde wyth sobbyng terys wyckedly trespassyd ageynst hyr sclaundred hyr full falsely loo maydens outward lyght lorde gaf hyr inward lyght knowe falsely deceyued fende anone forthwyth whanne holy mayde herde mekely axed forgyuenes wente hyr mekely took hyr armes kyssed hyr seyng hyr thus full comfortably dere moder dysplesed wyth wyse wote well fendes malyce youres thanke yon wyth herte ye loue ye wolde kept clene therfore wyte thyng thys fende hath wrought malyciously ageynst wyth suche wordes lyke thyse thys holy mayde comforted hyr seek suster dyd hyr seruyse wonte whan leste shold haue spende hyr tyme vayne wente hyr chambre occupyed hyr prayer mene tyme seek su ste knowleched hir gylty wepyng waylyng afore thoo came hyr sayd openly afore theym alle dysceyte fende sclaundred ye holy mayde wrongfully axed forgyuenes hem alle sayde knewe well ynough yt mayde onely pure clene flesshely synnes also holy fulfylled wyth holy ghoost knewe well thenne somme saddest hyr susters axyd hyr pryuely wysely knewe mayde holy token hadde therof answerd stedfastly wyth feruent spyryt knewe neuer afore swetnesse soule ghoostly comfort vnto tyme sawe thys holy mayde afore hyr transfygured transformed ouercouered vnspekable lyght eftesones thenne hyr susters axyd hyr whether saw syght wyth hyr bodely eyen coude telle wyth noo thyng fayrenes lyght swetnesse felte hyr sowle tyme thenne ye holy maydens name began encreace vertuously ouer fende aboute dysceyue hynder hyr name holy ghoost enhauncyd hyr name vertuously thys ryght neuer sonner throwe doun euyll fame ryght neuer enhauncyd hir self elacyon suche good name contynued euer forthe hyr holy seruyse dyd hyr besynesse euer knowe hyr self nought yet hyr ghoostly enemy fende cessyd neuer lette hyr eftesones tempted hir hir holy minystracion squey mousnes stomake tyme whanne thys holy mayde wesshyd hyr seek susters horryble wounde cam suche sauour therof poynte caste hyr body thenne rose ageynst hyr self moche vyolently vyctorye another temptacyon grace holy ghoost sayde hir self thus trewly wretche thou hast moche abhomynacyon thou shalte receyue wythin anone toke wesshyng wounde matter fylthe went asyde dra ke preuely whanne hadde hir teptacyon abhominacion cessyd tolde afterward mayster reymond hyr confessour hir presence whome addyd sayd pryuely srth n borne thys worlde etc neuer ne dranke swete ne good sauour noo maner mete ne drynke thys gloryous vyctorye nyght suyng lord jhesu cryst appyred holy mayde shewyng hir hys fyue blessyd woundes whiche suffred helthe sayd thus de doughter many bateylles thou hast ouerpassyd helpe thou hast oue coome yet hyther whiche vyctoryes thou art ryght welcome specyally yester day thou plesyst gretely yu dyspysedest thyne owne nature kinde loue thou receyuest drynke whiche abhomynable dedely therfore ryght thou pas st thy kynde thy nature ryght shall gyue yu drynke passyth custome kynde man wyth helde hys arme necke brought hyr mouth hys blessyd wounde hys syde sayd hi thus drynke doughter drynke helthe ye whiche thy soule shall fulfylled wyth moche swetenesse shall boude thy body whiche thou hast meruayllously despysed loue thenne thys holy mayde sowked pype lyf comyng hys blessyd wounde wyth hyr mouth hyr bodye moche wyth mouth hyr sowle longe tyme gyder full plentuou ly vnspekable drynke euer lastyng helthe lost ordynaunce lord cessyd yet thursty withstondyng ynough maydens praye consydereth mekely thys vertues acte thys blessyd mayde beholdeth beseche rote hir charyte moeued take vpon hit folowely seruyse serue seek folke also beholdeth long contynued seruyse wythseondyng grete lettyng abhomynacyon nature behelde also grete stedfastenes hadde abydyng wythstondyng foule sclandres whiche put vpon hyr last beholde notable coclusyon tyme hadde receyued holsom drynke lordes syde fulfylled wyth moche habundaunce grace etc neuer ne myght etc afterward suche wyse dyd afore shall declared clerely wythin forthe touchyng chapytre shall make ende thyn ge wryten ne reherced thys chapytre suche mayster reymond thys holy maydes confessour knewe hyr confessyon hyr founde wrytyng hyr confessour afore certeyn hir sustres whiche trewe sadde leuyng p hyr synguler maner lyuyng dysceyued grutched wyth hyr meruayllous fastyng ca v tyme lord jhesu endeles spouse thys holy mayde proued hir ouen manyfolde trybulacyons also taught hyr ouercome hyr ghostly enemy ye fende dyuers bateyll ryght semely yt shold reward hyr thys lyf wyth somme specyall gyfte grace cause soules longe ben body may fully receyue fruyte vertue blysse endelesly therfore full nedefull fulfyllyng dyuyne prouydence lord euery chosen spouse hys erthe shold yet dwelle erthe neuerthelesse yet shall endowed som specyal reward mede cause sauyour wouchesauf begynne spouse handemayde katheryne wretched lyf maner heuenly lyuyng wyth maner lyuyng wolde assocye hyr erthely folke therfore whiche suche maner reuelacyon enfourmed hyr fyll tyme holy mayde prayed hyr chambre lord apperyd hyr sayd wyse wete ryght well dere beloued doughter thyne abydynge erthe shalbe fulfylled many meruayllous gyftes grace shall cause studieng incredulyte many mannes hertes specyally flesshely menys hertes knowen maner gracyous gyftes also many louen shall thought suppose passyng loue whiche werche yt shold dysceyte shall gyue grete habundau ce grace thyn sowle shall meruayllously rebounde thy body whiche thy body shall receyue haue meruayllous maner lyuyng whiche hath selde herde afore ferthermore thyn herte shall soo gretely kyndelyd helthe soules thou shalt forgete maner thyn owne kynde chaunge althy fyrst conuersacyon thou shalt eshewe shun company men wommen thou wonte rather theyr soule helthe thou shalt put maner laboure thy power myght thys maner lyuyng many one shold sclaundred many thou shalt ageyn sayd thoughtes ef theyr hertys may knowen theyr wordes loke thou wyse aferde ne troubled shall euer wyth delyuer thy sowle treucherons tonges lyers therfore werke myghtely holy ghoost shall teche ye yt shall delyuere ne sowle fendes power mediacion specyall grace shallede heuen whanne lorde sayd thyse wordes often tymes rehersed hyr comfortably touchyng poynte lord sayd hyr sholde ferdene troubled answerd beknewe afterward contessyon thou lord god thy wretched seruaunt euer thy wyll done haue mynde good lorde god thy grete mercy helpe thus vanysshed cessyd vysyon thys holy mayde bethought hyr kepte well hyr herte wha gracyous chaugyng sholde tyme comyng fro tyme afterward fro day day grace oure lord jhesu encreced hyr herte holy ghost habounded hyr moche hyr self astoned therof wext feble body sayd propheet sayd thyse wordes deficit caro mea et corpus um deus cordis mei et mea deus inete nu body flesshe sebled de ailleth good lord ye gouernour myn herte parte wythoutenende eftesones sayd pheet sayd another place memor fui dei et drlectata sum exercitata sum et deficit spiritus meus haue mynde lord god haue therin grete delyte hauce ye ghostly delyte therfore spyrytes strengthes body wexen feble defayllen mayde wext seek body loue lord hir sekenes remedy weping waylyng therfore wept wayled euery day yet suche wepyng waylyng myght cour hyr sekenes lord put hyr herte sholde good hyr souereyn cemedye hir sekenes oft tymes housled myght receyue lord yt loued sacrement autre myght yet fulfylled fully thys lyf shold heuen blysse netheles yt cause loue encrece gretter sekenes yet tyme made satys faccyon vertue feyth ye ser yse hyr charyte brenned contynuelly hyr herte sufflacyon holy ghoost tyme custome comuned houseled euery day though oft tymes lette sekenes body soo besynes mennes soules suche desyre ofte house led yf hyr body sholde su grete peyne maner sholde feble defayll right body par haboundaunce spyryte affluence habouded fro wythin forth ryght myght yf per eyner anguysshe dysease spyryt suffred thys mater shall de da largely helpe god afterward shall tell meruayllous lyuyng yt leued touchyng hyr body mayster reymond recordeth thus holy mayde knewe well hyr confessyon also wrytyng hyr confessour afore hym yt tyme vysyted ye forsayd vysyon moche plente grace ghoostly comfortes namely whan receyued lord jhesu ye blessyd sacrement autre reboundyd hyr body copyous affluence kyndly consumpcyon dygestyon hyr body place chaugyd kynde hir stomake receyuyng mete ned full hyr myght receyue mete wythout grete torment body yf shold algates te hir body suffred ryght gret peyne myght haue kyndely dygestion nedys must vyolence come ageyne yt etc ther went june lefull wryte wyth penne ofte many peynes holy mayde suffred receyuynge bodely mete maner kynde condycyon lyuyng begynnyng many folke bothe houshold conuersaunt wyth hyr incredyble named synguler gyfte god eyther temp tacyon ellys sottyll dysceyte deuyll errour fyll mayster reymond hyr confessour dyd yt wende disceyued hyr enemy ye whiche oftymes transfygured hym self aungell lyght deceyue soules therfore bad hyr etc hir mete euery day gyue credens suche desceyuable vysyons wold lett hyr fro hyr mete thenne sayd holy may de hyr confessour founde well experyence yt hole body whan receyued bodely mete tha whanne receyued yet suche excusacyons wold cesse precepte badde commaunded hir yt shold ete thenne trewe doughter obedyece obeyed byddyng ete hir mete vnto ye tyme bi sekenes almost dede thenne called hyr confessour mayster reymond sayd thus fader yf moche fastyng cause myn one deth sleer myn one body answered sayd yes thenne askyd eftesones whether grete synne dede bi etyng abstinence sayd etyng thenne sayd sythen ye see wexe feble nere dethe etyng ye knowe well experyence wyll ye fobede etinge ye wolde forbede fastyng suche caas reso coude answere cause perceyued nyghe deth euydent token sayde doughter doo lord taught ben merueylous thynges see lord werke many grutchynges ther housholde agaynste merueylous lyuyng cause knewe gracious werkynge god therto also stered confessour mayster reymound repreue albe tymes agaynst wyll grete dysese suffred none tongue tell cause soo obedyent soo grouded mekenes coude nother excuse self ne wythstond wyll confessonr euer badde doo one wyst well ye wyll god contrarye agaynst dome syde aferd dred god forsake obedyence bode confessour therto lothe notefye trouthe carnell pepse cause coude sauore suche ghostely trouthe therfore sholde doo wyst neuer thus suffred moche angwyshe conflycte amonges alle thyse conflictis ran praye souerayn remedy wepte plentuously afore oure forde teres sorowe hope besechyng hym mekely wyth moche instaunce wolde vouchesaf shewe hys wyll tho contrary ste maner lyuyng specyafly confessour moste lothe offende wolde reherce worde appostles sayde prynces lawe whan sayde thus p oportet obedire deo magi quam homini b sholde rader obeye god man seye lothe lest sholde haue answerd yt fende trans igureth hym ofte tymes angell lyght therfore sholde gyue none credens euery spyrit ne sholde leue moche owna wytte doo counseyll p deuout prayer oure lord herd graciously dyde many ofte tymes illumyned confessour sowle chaunged counseyll shalt sece mater procede processe holy maydens lyuyng fyrst tyme speciall grace befyll soo full holy ghoste fro begynnyng lenton ascencion oure lorde wythout bodely mete drynke euer glad mery none merueyle fruyte spyryte charyte ioye pea saynt pouse sayth lord sayth hym self man lyueth alwaye wyth bodely sustynaunce wyth worde cometh goddes mouth holy wryt sayth juseus exside viuit ryghtwysman lyueth fayth ye ascecio day lorde graunted sholde ete tolde afterward preuely confessour soo dyde ete bred potage wortes rawe herbes also lenton mete meruey lous body kynde myght recey ue none delycat mete day tournyd agayn symple faste yt hadde begunne fore soo lytyll lytill tournyd symple faste costome contynuelly neuer herd tho dayes confessour mayster reymound berith record sayth ofte tymes knewe body comforted none bodely mete ne drynke colde water vnto tyme brought suche febylnesse hym thought moo almost dede assone herd saye ony nede shold done manis soule caught strengthe sodenly wythouten ony bodely comforte able goo mightely euer wythout ony greuauuce boue commune strengthe whiche folowed neuer wae wery wherof came grace trowe ye spryte comforteth quickeneth body merueylously aboue kynde namely suche body subiecte spyryte alle ghostely werkes may euery ghostely man vnderstonde alle thys holy maydens lyf aboue kinde full myracle p tyme whan hadde faste soo longe lyued without mete drinke confessour mayster reymound asked wheder ony tyme ony maner appetyte mete drynke answerd thus haue grete swetnes lord gaue receyuing blessyd sacrament ye aulter owne precio flesh blod yt noo wyse myght desyre none maner bodely sustynaunce mete drynke thene confessour asked eftsones whether ony appetyte mete ye day hosylyd said nay wha happed hose lyd presence syght blessyd sacrament sight ye blessyd sacrmet also presens presie whiche knewe welle hadde day sayd masse touched blessyd sacrament comforted suche wyse hadde none mynde bodely mete p holy mayde stode bothe full fastyng wythoutforth fastynge wythinforth full wythoutforth drye wythinforth moyste flodes quyk water alle mane chaunces euer glad iocu de fende myght suffre shold thus endowed suche gracious gyftes venyms woodnes malycious enuye steryd bothe spyrytuall folke temperall folke relygious seculer againste syuguler gyfte fastynge merueyle though styred ghostely folke relygyous agaynst suche yf theyr owne loue theym self fully quenched grace regnid perylous enuye namely whan see another doo whiche thynketh vnpossybyle theym serche wisely aspye whether soth amonges holy faders dwellyng thebayde seculer man came grete congregacio phatomye abbot receyue habyte amonges theym whan receyued habyte ye holy congregacion couent sawe merueylously lyued myght doo dyde came alle wyth one voyce gretelysteryd agaynste phatomye bad hym eyther put congregacion newe monke elli thei wolde abyde wyth hym loo yf suche enuye regned thenne tho dayes amonges suche yt holde ryht fyght folk enuye tro ye myht regne amoges ghostely folke yt lyue thyse dayes none wonder therfore thou ghostely folke grutched holy maydes fastyng somme said none lyuyng gretter lord oure lorde yet ete dranke while lyued erthe blessyd gloryous moder oure gloryous lady gloryous vyrgyn marye alle appostles also lorde bad shold ete drynke set afore theym soo dyde lyuyng erthe myght passe theym lyke theym trowe none somme ther also sayde afermed saintes afore v taught worde dede shold none take vpon theym synguler lyuyng passyng shold lyue common perfyght lyuyng somme also preuy bachyters saide ende fastynge sholde vicious therfore gaue counseyll take none ensample deceyued also carnal people open bacbyters sayde fastynge fayned thynge wynne therby veyn glory therfore semed fasted preuyly ete thynge enuye agaynst who fals doer fals opynyons purpos reple helpe god fyrste somme legged theym oure lord blessyd lady gracious virgyn mary appostles lyued common lyuyng wythout ony grete fastynge ne sholde sywe saint johan baptyste holy lord jhesu cryste lord sayde hym self saynt johan come neuer ete ne dranke fasted sone man come bothe ete dranke also shold sywe saynt anthony macharye illarion scrapion many holy faders whiche v many merueylous fastynges aboue common lyf appostles shold gretter thenne appostlis ouermore yf thyse forsayde grutchers wyll reple agaynst sayde saynt joha wyldernes thyse hooly faders egypte fasted symply without mete drynke somtyme ete wolde saye mary magdalene whiche lyued roche see xxx yere togyder wythout mete bodely drinke story maketh mencyon place lyued sheweth daye neuer myght come thy der man ne woman brynge mete ner drynke whether gretter blyssed gloryous vyrgyn lady gloryous virgyn mary neuer fasted ne lyued suche roche wyll also saye many holy faders lyued many yeres wythout mete drynke passyd worlde enspeciall one rede yt whan receyued ye blessyd sacrament aulter wythout ony bodely sustynaunce mete drinke lyued many yeres therfore yf suche grutchers neuer lerned lete theym lerne gretenesse lytylnesse holynes mesured ne demed fastynge charite thus lete lerne neuer make juges thynges knowe lyke maner somme sayde saynt johan whan came fasted deuyll wythin hym whan oure lorde come fasted sayde hym deuourer mete drynke grete wyne drynker laste sentence suffyciant ynow stoppe mouthes suche grutchers seconde grutchers whiche hate syngularyte lyuyng may lyghtely e answerd thus though man sholde take vppon hymself ony newe synguleryte neuer held afore yf god werke hym hemaye refuse nedes muste werke vse wyth thankynges ellys e synguler yeftes oure lorde sholde vtterly despysed p holy wryte sayth ryght wyse man sholde serche ne seke curyousey hyghe thynges aboue hym anone afterward folowed many thynges benshewed ryght wyse man aboue wytte mene nothynge ellys man shold seke hym selfe yf lorde aboue hym shewed many grete merueylous thynges sholde resceyue vse wyth thankynges therfore holy mayde dede may sey dyde synguleryte selfe oure lorde vouchesaf gyue ye gyfte synguler ordynaunce suche maner wyse holi mayde answerd whan asked ete dyde answerd termes coueryd mekenes whan asked ete dyde sayde oure lorde hadde smyte synnes synguler passyon infirmytes wherefor let ete mete dyde gladly sayd sholde ete myght therfore sayde praye pray vouchesaf forgyue myn sinnes wherfor suffer thyse sykenesses though hadde sayd thus god doth myn self also le ony maner spyce pryde sholde appyre euer sayde suffred infirmyte synnes yet sayde agaynst conscience supposed stedfastely oure lorst hadde suffred falle grutchynge men punysshe synnes maner euyll fyll wyted synnes good euer wrought put oure lord p sentence good answere thrydde preuy bacbyters sayden euer conseylde ware ende suche synguler fastyng ende muste nedes vycious whiche god may ende holy maydes fastyng bee vycious whiche come god self clerly declared afore also sayde dysceyued fende may soo ofte ouercome dysceytes ye fende sette caas myght dysceyued fende helde kepte body suche kyndely strengthe perauenture wolde saye fend thene wolde wett yf kepte soule suche ghostely gladnes pea sythe soo depreuyd fro maner symple delyte delectacion fruyte holy ghost may none deuyll y power gyue ye appostle sayth yt fruyt ye holy gost charyte ioye pea wolde suppose yt shold directed ye fende therfore suche sclauders bacbyters vertu shold answerd rather silence word euery virtuons man shold eschewe suppose yt ben vnwurthy haue answere holy mayde dyd coude euery daye stoppe mouthes lest sholde sclaudred yt came mete euery day ye meyne ye houshold therbi know whether myght dyde yet otherwhyle wolde assaye ete soo grete payne alle yt sawe hadde compassyon stomake myght defye mete kyndly consumpcion naturall dygestyon none vse alle yt entryd stomake come agayn waye wente caused many dyuerse passyons holy mayde receyued stomak ony mete whiche mete wurthy tyme yet spet fro grete mater flewme folke dyde whiche myght bee nature yf stomake hadde receyued somme substaunce afore thrfoere lord wrought merueylously aboue nature also drynkynking colde water receiued gladly refresshe chykes throte maner lyf lyued vnto aste ende grutchers theym slaundred fastinge confessour mayster reymound perceyued grete peyne suffred vndygestyon stomake stoppe grutchers conforted co passyon hadde vppon sholde leue ete nomore rather suffre suche payne lete theymgrutche ynow answerd smylyngly fader better meto suffrein lyfefor synes thanne suffre payne endelesly grutchyng profytable cause shall delyuerd payne wythouten ende payne suffre lyf sholde fle ryghtwysnes god nay god forbede oure lord doth grete grace cause giueth myn payne lyf soo confessour coude nomore answere helde pea wyse p alle enemyes maistry soo maner fende grutchers taughte euery daye yt tyme whan comynyd wyth confessour gracious gyftes lord sayd soo coude vse grace oure lorde sholde euer haue vyctorye thynges fallen hym thene tourned confessour sayde hym soo wolde ye dyde ofte ony newe thynge byfalleth prosperyte aduersyte thynketh self sayth ofte wyll wanne somwhat ye doo soo ye sholde soone ryche vertu p loo maydens haue mynde thysnotable doctryne thus make ende chapytre wytnes thynges whiche ben wryte therin holy mayde eyther opyn dedes elli wordes also confessour whiche fore maister reymound p wounderfull rauysshyng excesse mynde bodely wyttees grete reuelacions shewed oure lorde capitulum vj right oure lorde graunted spouse holy mayde synguler lyuyng touchyng body ryght soo vysyted soule wyth grete merueylous confortes reuelacions fyrst grete haboudant grace come bodely strengthe yt aboute kynde wete ye right wel yt fro tyme holy mayde dronke oure lordes syde drynke lyf rehersid fo many grete grace haboudant yt ofte time ofte time maner contynuabyl occupyed actuell co templacion spyryte lowyd lord parte lefte wythout felyng bodely wyttes soo rehersed fyrst party armes founde ofte time soo styf tyme suche actuell contemplacion rather sholde breke ne bowe eyen closed eres herde none noyse neuer grete bodely wyttes tyme sequestred fro owne werkynge p sholde none merueyle noman yf wolde take hede yt syweth oure lorde began bee soo homely brennyd sowle wyth soo moche haboundante fyre loue oonly pryuy place also open place well stondyng goyng whiche hadde thyse grete grace knewe playnely confessour coude fynde none wordes telle expressely grace felte p tyme whan prayed oure lord feruentely wyth prophete dauyd seyeng deuoutly thyse wordes p cor meum crea deus et spiritu rectum innoua visceribus mei prayng lorde specially wolde take awaye herte owne wyll gyue newe herte wyll hadde suche comforte semed lord jhesu come opened lyft side toke herte went waye belyfte owne herte p afterward befyll commynyd wyth confessour amonges thynges sayde none herte body whiche wordes co fessour rned maner blamed sayde soo thenne rehersed eftsones confermed wordes trewely fader moche maye fele yet felyng myn body semeth lacke myn herte oure lorde apperyd opened myn leste syde toke myn herte went way thenne confessour sayde vnpossyble shold lyue herte sayde naye nothynge vnpossyble god therfore bad hym gyue credens ofte tymes ward rehersed lyued without herte fewe dayes afterward befyll wente chapell fryer susters penaunce wonte knele whan goo home befil contynued prayer fro self rauysshyng laste awoke rauysshyng went homward wente waye sodenly lyght heuen bicliped lyght aperyd lord holdyng honde reed shining herte lykenes mannys herte commyng thys heuenly lyght aferde fyll doune vppon grounde thenne came lorde openyd lyftesyde eftsones pute body herte whiche hylde hondes seyng thus p loo dere doughter toke awaye thyn herte laste daye ryght soo giue myn herte wherby thou mayst lyue endelesly whan hadde doo closed wounde agayn made open flesshe neuerthelesse left merueylous marke lykenes woude heled place euer afterward felawes tolde confessour mayster reymound ofte tymes sawe coude forsake hym whan askid whether soo meruayllous gracyous herte gyuen hyr lord came many meruayllous werkys yet many moo meruayllous reuelacyons haboundeth wythin forth came neuer afterward hoseled ther shewed hyr many synguler gyftes grace oft tymes sawe lytell chylde prestys handy whyle well growen chylde whyle hote brennyng ouen fyre whan preste receyued blyssed sacrament semed hyr fyre entred hym whan shold houseled ofte tymes tastyd grete odour blyssed sacrament almost hyr body defaylled euermore also whether sawe receyued ye blyssed sacrament receyued newe ioye hir soule many tymes sholde daunce hir body ioye makyng noyse hyr felawes myght hyr whiche tolde afterward hyr confessour enquyred trouthe whether founde trewe soo wrote perpetuell recorde sowne noyse lyke maner comyn sownes men hadde noyse aboue comyn cours kynde meruayll though made ioyfull noyse aboue kynde syth hadde receyued herte aboue kynde tyme hadde receyued newe herte rehersed afore semed afore ofte tymes sayd hyr confessour see ye fader afore rather chauged another persone wolde god fader ye knewe fele trewe veryly yf creatour knewe fele sowle sholde resolued made ryght esye neuer harde sowle full melodye ioye meruayll may abyde body also grete hote brennyng dyuyne loue therin thys outward materyall fyre semeth co paryson fyre rather colde hote also ghoostly hote kynde led sowle semeth soo grete loue neghbours thynketh myght gladdely suffre bodely deth wyth grete ioye ouermore ghoostly hote come soule renewyng purytee mekenes moche semeth brought purytee mekenes chylde foure fyue yere age inne tolde hir confessour preuely none tyme thys holy mayde thus fulfylled hyr sowle suche plente newe gracys many notable vysyons shewed hyr somme shall reherce grace god p fyrste lord jhesu hys blessyd moder marye magdalene appyred gydres hir comforted hyr hir holy purpose whome lord axed sayd doughter desyrest thou wyth wepyng chere answerd sayd lorde thou knowest nedeth better haue wyll thyne ne none herte thyn hert thenne came hyr mynde marye magdalene commytted hyr self fully lorde whan satte wepte fete wyth felte swetenesse loue marye magdalene felte tyme whan wepte wherfore behelde marye magdalene lord ceyued fulfyll hyr desyre sayd loo dere doughter thy solace co forte gyue marye magdalene thy moder whome thou mayst trustely go comforted hir specyally commytte thy gouernaunce grete gyfte holy mayde thanked lord wyth gpete mekenes reuerently deuoutly comended hyr ghoostly gouernaunce marye magdalene prayng hyr wolde wouchesauf take hyr vnder gouernaunce syth lord specyally commytted hyr fro houre euer afterward holy mayde called marye magdalene hyr moder whiche doo wythout grete mysterye semeth marye magdalene lyued xxxiij yere oche wythout bodely mete tyme occupyed comtemplacyon ryght holy mayde fro tyme endowed wyth newe grace vnto age xxxiij yere afterward whiche yere passyd thys worlde occupyed dyuyne contemplacyon hadde neuer nede ye tyme bodely mete yet marye magdalene take vp ayre aungels seuen tymes day herde pryuetees god ryght holy mayde partye hir yeres rauysshed fro hyr bodely wyttes strengthe sowle occupyed contemplacyon heuenly thynges praysed lord wyth aungels moche often tymes hyr body lyfte vp ayre whiche many men wommen sawe hyr tyme bare recorde ouermore rauyssheng sawe many meruayllous thynges spake preuely tyme hyr rauysshyng many hygh wordes contemplacion whiche som shall tell afterward hyr confessour saw hyr one tyme rauysshed fro hyr bodely wyttes wyse rehersed afore herde hyr speke preuely thenne came nere lysten clerely sayd herde sayd formably thyse wordes latyn vidi archana dei sayd often tymes wordes sayde none thoo whanne restoryd ageyne hyr bodely wyttes cessyd reherse wordes co tynuelly nomore say haue seen pryuetres god thenne hyr confessour desyryng knowe rehersed tho wordes ofte axyd hyr thys maner wyse good moder rehersed ye soo ofte wordes wyll tell ye mene ye wonte answerde may say none wyse hyr confessour axed hyr cause ye wont declare many thinges lord hadde shewed wyll ye thene sayde sholde haue grete conscyence therof yf sholde declare haue seen wyth langage soo vnperfyte sholde haue yf blasfemed lord inhonoured hym grete dyffrence bytwene vnderstondyng intellecte sowle illumyned god expressyng wordes seme contrary eche therfore tyme tell haue saye ben vnspekable skylle thynke well commytted dyuyne prouydence lord marye magdalene faster shold knytte faster louer louer hygh contemplacyon hyr soo hyghe contemplacyon also hir confessour rehersed hir tyme saw vysyon lord hys blessyd mo saynt mary magdalene tymeit semed hyr hyr herte went inne syde lorde herte made bothe one felte hyr soule melte relented strengthe hys dyuyne loue yed hyr soule sayd p lorde thou hast wounded myn herte lorde yu hast wou ded myn herte p saynt margaretes day tolde hyr confessour preuytee p hyt befell also another tyme morowe saynt laurence daye holy mayde cam chyrche masse kneled nexte auter wonte see blessyd sacrement sholde lette preste theautre hyr grete sobbynghir confessour came hyr warned shold constreyne hir asmoche mighte fro suche grete sobbynges lest prest lette hyr p th nae anone mekely trewe obedyent mayden satte ferther fro aulter prayed oure lorde wold vouchesauf illumyne hir confessour myght see knowe whether suche sterynges spyryte god myght mesured man p thene vertu prayer hyr contessoure hadde perfyte knoleche feuoure deuocyon experience knewe fully suche feruoures soule myght kepte wythin nedes strenthe dyuyne loue yt muste breke p ferthermore oftyme whan houseled desyred hyr sowle receyue blyssed sacramet aulture p oftymes wold breke say deuoutly thus p wolde receyue lorde jhesu crystys body wyth lorde wolde appyre hyr wont doo fulfylle hyr desyre toke maydens mouthe put hys blessyd wounde hys syde bad hyr receyue flesshe hys bloode moche lyst p thenne receyued plentuously lorde breste semed pure loue sholde hadde dyed cause grete swetnes felte herte p hyt befyll also vpon sanyt exis day holy mayde prayed lorde deuoutly wolde vouchesauf grau te hyr brenyng desyre receyue hys flesshe hys blood p wyth reuelacyon yt sholde houseled morowe doubteles forbeden hyr freres sholde ofte houseled p thenne whane hadde thys confortable reuelacyon prayed lord yt wold wouchesauf clenie hir herte agaynst tyme shold receyue hym myght worthely receyue hym p tyme prayed thus felte reyne comenge doun hyr soule maner grete haboundant flood water suche lyquore onely blood medelyd wyth fyre whiche hyr semed purgyd clensed myghtely rsowie strengthe tyre ded body clensed also hyr body p thys morowe oseek waye semed hyr myght goo one foot p neuertheless doubted thyng ye mysse lord trustyng hym fully began go chyrche whan come thyder knelyd doun chapell besyde aulter p thenne came hyr mynde enfourmed yt myght houseled prest lyst suche ben assygned hyr p wyth desyred hyr confessour sholde say masse aulter anone oure lorde gaf hyr comforte sholde sing sodeynly lord thenne touched herte hyr confessonr wyth deuocio sholdesaye masse day wyll syng day ne wyste holy mayde come chyrche p thenne steryng lorde dysposed masse wente aulter holy mayde abode lordes behest whiche aulter also neuer wont synge p whanne came founde holy mayde axyng houseled charyte p thenne rceyued wyll god sholde syng day p sayd masse ende masse maner came housele hyr holy mayde aulter ende redy receyue blessyd sacrament p hyr confessour behelde sawe hyr vysage shynyng rede al wepre wyth terys whiche grete meruayll wuth deuocion receyued blissed sacrament p tyme houseled plenteuously replete lorde day myght speke worde noo creature p morowe hyr confessour axed hyr hir eyled nowe grace receyued ye day fore cause shynnyng rede whan receyued blyssed sacrament answorde thus p fader colour tyme wote nere thys knowe well wha vnworthy wretche receyued blyssed sacrament hondes drewe som alle thyng saue allone wexed lothesom onely temporall thynges dylectacyons worlde also comfortes pleysaunces neuer ghostly wherfore desyred prayed yt suche ghostly comfortes sholde sequestryd frome myght pleese god ende lesly knytte hym also prayed hym wolde take away wyl gyue hys wyll dede right mercyably sayd thus p loo dere doughter gyue wyll bi whiche thou shalte soo strong euer happe fro thys tyme warde thou shalt neuer chaunged nestyred ryght p euer afterwarde dyspysed sette lytell alle folke neuer styred ne troubled ageynsthem p ouermore yet holy mayde sayd confessour fader well wyll ye wete lorde serued trewely moder serued hyr lytell soukyng chylde whome loueth tenderly p moder suffred hir childe stonde ferre hyr whyle sheweth hym hirtete hir breste suffred hym wepe longe tyme hit tyme lawhed p last whan hath suffred wepe long tyme gothe ther wyth lawhyng beclypped armes kyssed soo gyueth hyr breste tete p ryght ferde lorde wyth day shewed hys blessyd wounde syde stondyng ferre p desyre hadde ther putte mouth blessyd wounde wepte haboundantly p thenne lorde sayd tyme yt hadde suffred wepe came gladdely tooke sowle hys armes putte mouthe wounde p thenne sowle grete desyre entred hole hys blessyd wounde founde moche swetnesse knowleche hys godhede p yfye wystye wold meruayll myn herte gretnesse ioye loue barst ye wolde astonyed myght lyue lyf wyth suche grete passyng hete loue also another thynge befyll hyr next yere se wyng vpon day boute receyue blyssed sacrament aulter whanne prest helde blessyd sacrament hys handes afore hyr taught hyr say thus lorde worthy thou sholdest entre thenne whan de receyued hym hyr semed fysshe entred water water hym ryght hyr sowfe entred god god hir soo felte hyr self drawe lord vnnethe myght come home hyr chambre whan come home layde hyr doune vpon hir harde bedde leyng long tyme styll moeuyd last hyr body take vp ayre stode whyle gyder thre wytnessys bereth recorde whiche name shall tell afterward thenne afterward came doun lay vpon hyr bedde alle weyke feble spake softely many blessyd swete wordes hye contemplatyf wordes steryd hyr felawes wepe whiche herde amonges thoo swetr wordes prayed many folke specyally name namely hyr confessour tyme momente chyrche thought tyme thynge sholde styre hym deuocyon sodeynly hyr prayer felte meruayllous deuocyon neuer assayed afore consyderyng meruayllyng newe grace camto hym soo sodeynly houre whyle thought thus sodeynly came hym one holy maydens felawes sayd trewely fader katheryne hath moche prayed day suche houre thenne anone knowe suche newe denocyon came hym houre katherynes prayer axed hyr felawe prayed tolde prayed oure lorde wolde wouchesauf graunte euerlastyng lyf putt forth hyr honde prayed hym graunte thenne took doune hyr honde ageyne semyng hir al sore wyth grete syghenge sayde thus lord worshypped mote thou euer comyn terme hyr mouthe saye whan seek sore trauaylled whanne hyr confessour herde wente prayed hir tille hym hyr vysyon meke obedyent mayde tolde hole bysyon sayd afore whanne came mater prayed specyall frendes sayd hym fader whanne prayed lord wolde wouchesauf graun te euerlastyng lyf hadde comforte sholde forthwyth asked token lord myght knowe sholde none incredulyte rather notable memorye thenne prayed sholde stoetche myn honde dyde putte honde nayle closed nayle soo faste wyth inne myn honde thenne felte grete peyne myn honde though yren naylle hadde smyten thorugh myghtely wyth hamour soo semed mynowne syght thought jnuysyble haue marke crystys woundes myn honde p also contynuance mater shall tell another meruayllos thyng lyke thys befylle cytee pyse mayster reymond hyr last confessour bereth recorde tyme thys holy mayde came cyte pyse many wyth hyr amonges whome mayster reymond one whyche holy mayde receyued worthy mannes place cyte besyde chappell saynt crystyane whyche chappell mayster reymond sayde masse holy maydes prayer ther houseled hyr hyr desyre vsed contynuelly whanne hadde receyued blyssed sacramente anone rauysshed fro hyr bodely wyttes tyme mayster reymond moo abode tyll hadde hyr somme ghoostly comforte wonte suche rauyssheng sodeynly behelde hyr body laye prostratr vpon grounde reysed vp kneled vpon hyr knee stretchyng vp hyr armes hyr hondes wyth clere shynyng vysage whanne long kneled wyth closyng styf armes laste fyll doun sodeynly though hadde dedly wounded anone sone restoryd ageyne hyr bodely wyttes thenne sente mayster reymond hyr confessour sayde hym preuely thys wordes fader well wete mercy god body markys blessyd woundes oure lorde mayster reymone thenne axed hyr myght stode hir tyme hir rauyssheng answer de sayde sawe lord fastned vpon crosse comyng doune beelyppyng wyth grete lyght whyche gracyous vysyon sowle gretely steryd wyth lorde yt body constreyned strengthe spyryte aryse thenne hole hys holy woundes sawe fyue rede bemys come doune hym fastned vpon body cause body forstoeyned wyth cryed lord sayde lorde god beseche woundes appyre syght men outward thenne sodeynly whyle sayde thyse wordes er thenne thoo rede bemys fully come doune body changed hir colour rede meruayllous bryghtnesse lykenes pure lyght restyd fyue placed body vpon hondes foot herte thenne mayster reymond axed hir whether ony bemys come ryghte syde sayde nay onely vpon lyfte syde vpon herte mayster reymond axed hyr eftesones felyst thou ony maner sensyble pryne thoo place answerd wyth grete sygheng sayde suffre soo grete sensyble sorowe tho fyue place specyaly herte god shewe newe myracle impossyble lyue longe tyme gydres body worde marked well mayster reymond hyr confessour espyed coude see hir ony maner tokenes peyne wha told wold say depted sonder chappell went gyders home theyr inne holy mayde went hir chambre ther lay doun femyng euer aboute hyr drawyng deth thenne mayster reymond called hys feleshyp see ye wound thyng whan come wepte sore cause wend shold depted fro saw hir ne feble nygh ye deth p neuertheles within whyle resorted agayn strengthe receyued mete thenne spake eftsones maister reymound sayde hym sayd fore may longe lyue yf god shewe newe miracle thenne mayster reymound called gyders chyldren men wymmen prayng theym wyth wepyng wold wyth one voyce praye lord wolde vochesaf graunte v holy mayde katherin ghostely vertuous moder oure maystres whiche lythe passing abyde wyth v whyle thys lyf conferme v vertue alle graunted one voyce soo wold wente wyth mayster reymound holy mayde yeng transyte sayeng suche wordes weylyng wepyng moder wete well thou desyrest bee wyth thyne spouse wyth lorde jhesu cryst thy mede thy rewarde reserued fro auf haue rewthe v whome thou forsakest moder leue v freell wythout better enformacion vertu wretchyd worlde knowe well also thy well byloued spouse thou louest wyth soo grete desyre wylle nothynge denye thou askest therfore beseche praye hym vouhesauf graunte v tyme lest thou passe fro v thyn ge lytyll edefyed thy good lyuyng though praye wel coude drede v lest wyll v oure wretchyd lyuynge certayne ben ryght vnwurthy herd thene therfore hast louyd oure helthe soo tenderly feruently praye ye v wynne lord mowe leue yt lyf tyll ben edefyed ghostely vertu many suche wordes sayde amonges theim wyth grete wepynge holy maide answerd ye knowe well haue forsake myn owne wyll ne desyre neuer goddes wyl haue desyred helthe wyth myn herte yet knowe well yt whiche helthe myn better ordeine one creature praye wyll therfore bee done thynges neuertheles yet shall praye gladly vouchesaf hym semeth beste whan hadde sayd word wente syde tyme beyng grete sorowe vnto tyme knowe answer next day afterward called mayster reymounde sayd semeth fader yt lord hath condescendyd prayer hope ye shold soone haue wylle entent sayd sone vpon morowe whiche vpon sonday receyued crystis body ye sacramet ye aulter cofessour hondes ryght sondaye bifore brought greate febylnes rauysshyg tyme hadde receyued blessyd sacrament ryght sonday gretly strengthed rauysshyng blessyd sacrament whiche grete merueyle aboute mayster reymound said hope yt oure lord hath accepted teres codescedyd prayer though thei ben vnwourthy thene wythin litil time afterward quikly reuiued yt none doubte yt shold lyue yt god grauted fulli desire almyghti god fader mercy wylt yu thyn trewe seruaut welbeloued child yu codescendist benigly thyn synfull seruauntis mayster reymound thenne asked sykernes wheder passyo tho woudes contryned alway dede body answerd wise oure lord hu hath herd prayer thefore tho woundes tourment body yde rather comforte strengthe loo maiden ye knowe evcellent grace holy maide hadde also ye mowe lerne oure lord vochesaf synnes whan thry asked ony thyng longeth sowle helthe p yet shall telle another merneylous thyng semeth passeth haue rehersed yet shall make ende chapytre helpe god p tyme lord hadde receyued soule blyssyd wound syde shewed mystery est gloryous trynyte thenne came glorious lady gloryous moder gloryous vyrgin marye fulfylled wyth gloryous mylke gloryous brestes tetes came mary magdalene comynyd wyth ful homely reuelacions yt hadde whan desert thyse thre come togydre gaue many blessyd comfortable wordes yet wanted comforte saytes apperyng namely saynt poule appostle saynt johan theuangelyst saint domynyke saint thomas dalquino oftetymes saint agnes hadde onys reuelacion sholde felawe kyngdom heuen shall declared afterward helpe god shal telle two notable poyntes befyll hooly mayde whan hadde vysyons saynt poule ye apostle befil ye fest co sacio sait poule yt holy mayde merueylously rauysshed self thought spyryt drawe vp heuen soo ferforth thre dayes thre nyghtes vnmeuable wythout bodly felyng soo semed fully dede somme vnderstode better condycion sayde supposed rauysshed wyth saint poule thirde heuen laste thre dayes ende reforted bodly feling spyryte comforted reuelacions stoode longe tyme afterward hadde half slepe yet slepte mene whyle fryer thomas fyrst confessour another felowe whiche called fryer donat flerence hadde desyre goo vysyte hooly myte deserte fyrst wente thei come holy mayde hou founde holy sompnolente cause wolde excite asked whether wolde go wyth deferte vysyte holy man answerd theym hooly slepe sayde ye notwythstondyng yt wyst sayd cause fully evcyted anone perceyued worde hadde suche reuerse conscience lesynge sorowe whiche toke therof restoryd fully bodely wyttes many dayes nyghtes stood afore rauysshyg longe wayled wepte vncessabyly yt sy e sayd self wycked woman hast thou soo well bee feed wyth infinite goodnes god thou muste make lesyng bee thyse trenthe thou haste lerned heuen ye doctryne thou art taught holy ghoste make lesynges p thenne wyst thou ryght well thou woldeste goo wyth tho fryer yete thou saydest thou woldest soo madest lesyng thyn confessour thyn ghostely faders meost wycked synne ce ye maydens meruaylous wayes maners lordis prouydence loo leste reuelacyons sholde haue cause pryde lorde suffred falle suche lesyng yf may callyd lesyng none ntencion deceyte soo mekenes lownes oure lorde couered vertu fend shold entre destroye theym tho thinges sawe tyme reuelacyons tolde confessour wonte doo reuelacyons sayd selfe coude fynde none la guege myght expresse tho reuelacyons wordene lefull noo man speke hem wyth tongue appostle sayth hym selt nonlicet hoiloqui p eut feruoure herte besynes prayer holy exortacyons shewed openly ynowe sawe preuytes god p whiche may comynyd sawe theym ouermore another tyme sait poule appostle arpperid warned shold giue besely prayer whiche tolde afterward confessour therfore vsed moche thenne befyll afterwarde whyles prayed chyrche vygylle saynt domynyke many reuelacyons shewed saynt domynyke sayntes p soo oft occupyed wyth reuelacyons tyme whan wold speke confessour hadde reuelacions thenne nexte day afterward saynt domynyke lytyl afore euen songe tyme whyles occupyed wyth reuelacions sodenly entred chirche fryer whiche bartylmeus confessours felawe trusted moche confessour confessour absens goostely tader p whan perceyued come ar o wente agayst hym sayd hym wolde speke wyth hym certeyn reuela c ons theune satte doun bothetegyders chyrche began reherce many reuelacyons lorde deshewed saynt domynyke laste sayd loo fader see myn holy fader saynt domynyke see nowe yet nerer ye p thenne procedyd forth many merueylous reuelacyons wythin whyle befyll yong brother called also bartylmeus went sodenly caste eye lytyll syde behylde brother left syght saynt domynyke lytyll tyme thenne contynued forth tyste mater dede made moche sorowe whan ceyued doo longe helde pea spake nomore alwaye wepte trespaas whan longe contynued wepyng laste fryer bartylmewe prayed procede forth began migte sobbyng vnnethe speke one worde p yet myght speke sayde p wretche shall doo vengeaunce synnes p fryer bertylmewe synne myght thene sayde sawe ye bowed awaye mynhede myn eyen beholde broder went ryght while lorde wed many merueylous thynges fryer bertyimewe say nay coude perceiue bowed ony wyse hede eyen syde p thenne sayde fader yt ye wyste blessyd gloryous lady gloryous virgyn mary repreuyd ryght synne ye woide wepe also fore soo spake nomore ie reuelacyons euer cotynued wepyng vnto tyme made con e ion thene wente home chamber saynt poule appleryd de afterwarde confessour repreuyd sharpely lokyng tyme whan tourned hede soo syde ferforthe sayd hadde leuer shamed worlde onys stsones suffre shame whyche saynt poule whan repreuyd thene sayd confessour fader bethynke repreuynge cryste shall day dome synners yt cepreuynge one hys appostles soo sharpe make soo moche aferd sayd also yf hadde comforthe fayr lambe stode besyde while appostle repreuyd sholde haue deyed sorowe semed wherefore euer warde meker reuelacyons loo maydens lorde suffred falle mekenes shall telle reuelacyons whyche ofsaynt domynyke whan holy mayde comyned spake wyth freyer bertylmewe hyr reuelacyons sayd sawe dede vysyon imaginacion allmyghty god fader brenging forth semed mouthe lorde thu cryste endeles sone whiche apperid openly hyr lykenes mankynde lodersyde blessed patryarch saynt domynyke comyng brest almyghcy god fader shyn nyng ht p herde mouthe myghty god fader thyse wordes dere doughter haue brought forthe thyle chyldren one kyndely naturall beyng second persone intrynyte oder louyngly swetely adopcion thenne holy made hadde grete meruayle suche comparyson twene sone god saynte domynyke p almyghty god fader put awaye grete meruayle expownyd thyse wordes sayde dere doughter ryght mynowne sone brought forth naturally eternaly euer pertyghtly obedyent vnto dethe takyng vpon hym kynde ryght soo dedes domynyk myn sone adopcyon euer wrought fro hys chyldehode enof hys bodely lyf reuled p obedyence commaude tys neuer brake onys ony maner precepte myn virgynyte ofthis body soule grace hys baptyme kepte euer vndefoylyd p also ryght myn eternall naturall sone endeles worlde mouthe tolde spake ope ly worlde badde hym say therto bare wyttenes trouthe ryght soo domynyke myn sone adopcyon preche trouthe openly worlde welle amonges heretykes amonges faythfus peple onli bi hiself also bi hi whyles lyued erthe amonges also bi successours bi yet precheth shalle preche ryght naturall eternall sone sente dyscyples preche ryght soo domynyk myn sone dopcion sente fryer also ryght myn naturall sone eternall myn word ryght domynyke myn sone adopcion prechour aboute myn word wherfore myn synguler gyfte gyue hym fryer vuderstonde trouthe min wordes passe therfro also ryght myn naturall sone eternall ordeyned dysposyd lyff dedes doctrynes ensample helthe mannys soule ryght domynyke myn sone adopcion put besynes delyuer soules ye sorowe errour synne pryncipall entent whan began ordre say helthe soules therfore may well lyked min natural eternall sone sone ihesu criste reuelacioy whiche comynyd fryer bertylmewe whan sodeyn caas lokyng asyde byfyll rehersyd afore shall procede forth remenaunt lyf holy mayde reuelacions visyons fyrst wolde ye knewe maydens grete haboundance greces open reuelacions visyons gre ene loue therwyth whiche holy maydes soule fulfylled ryght syke body euer encresid sekenes loue soo yt roo nomore bedde laye styll euer newyng loue spose seyng thus aswete louely lord goddes sone sone mayden wyth suche many louyng wordes praised oure lorde spouse beleft wythout bodely mete therto spouse jhesu cryste whiche gyuen fyre loue cause sholde brene sto gely apperyd ofte tymes ne sayd hym febyll fyre loue good louely lord yu sufferest longe abyde wretched body wylt take thyn endeles presence haue none joye wretchid lyf myn ioye seke loue ihesu none wythout euer loue lord ther delayed soo longe fro thyn endeles presence p ha ha mekest myldest lorde delyuer myn soule pryson dedely lif thise wordes sayd soo weylyngly oure lord answerd dere doughter whan liued erthe amonge men besyed neuer fulfylle myn owne wyll myn faders albe desyred ete laste paske wyth myn dysciples wyth myn fader herd ofte tymes saye yet suffred paciently tyme ordeined myn fader soo must thou doo though yu desyre feruently onyd perfightely blesse heuen yet thou muste abyde tyme haue ordeyned theenne sayd lord louely lord sythe soo kynde yet passe lyff thyn wyl done fiat voluntas tua one thinge beseche ye whyles lyue erthe yt sythe may yet onyd yt blysse graute longe lyue lyf onyd ye ye bi parte taking thy blessyd passio ye whiche grauted p asked soo hadde fro tyme forward hadde moche experiens euery day herte iher body passion lorde tolde afterward preuyly maister reymoud neuer felte suche soor wyse ofte tymes wolde sytte talke mayster reymound teche hym passyon criste affermyng myghtely lorde jhesu cryste fro tyme gloryous concepcion tyme ende blyssyd passyon bare euer crosse deth hys soule grete passyng desyre hadde helthe mannys sowle whan conceyued ful grace wysdome charyte none nede hym encrece hym afterward perfyght ynow theym begynnyng therfore sythe loued perfyghtly god fader mankynde herte seyng consyderyng god fader trinite maner depryued honour also mankynde depryuyd f blessyd ende soo tourme ted wyth compassyon hym self vnto tyme myght restore passyon dewe honour god fader inyte endeles helthe mankynde also sayde affliction holy desyre none lytyll payne grete payne thefore sayde hys dyscyples schherthursday soper deside io desideraui manducare vobiscum hoc pascha p haue desyred wyth grete desyre longe afore thys tyme ete paske cause gaue theym soper speciall ernest helthe whiche wolde werke er thenne purposed ete wyth theym eftsones therfore alleggid wordys sauyour sayth another place pater transfer calicem huc fader put awaye passion fro shall drynke whiche wordes expownyd thus sayde perfyght folke sholde vnderstonde thyse wordes symple folke done sauyour asked fader put awaye remeue hye paynefull passio thus fro begynnyng gloryous concepcton vnto tyme deth dranke euer paynfull passyon grete desyre mannys helthe thenne drawe nere deth gredyly desyred drynke asked therfore shold soone fulfylled whiche hadde soo longe tyme desyred helthe mannys soule dryke ye whiche hadde drunke soo longe afore sholde thenne ended thus aske remeuyng awaye deth rader hasti ende deth whiche sauyour declared full openly afterward whan sayde juda quod facis fac cicius frend thou shalt doo doo anone p neuertheles though soo forsayd paynes full drynke desyre hym ryght greuous drynke yet ryght obedyent chylde fader sayde thus veruntamen non sicut ego volo sed sicut tu fader desyre myn wyll fulfilled thy wyll offeryng hym self redy th se wordes suffre dayly payne full desyre longe lyked hys fader soo fyrst wordes sayd transfer hunc calitem c fader voyde paynfull fro vnderstode haue voyded passyon come passyon hys desyre afore suffryng deth helthe mannes sowle endyd thenne sayd mayster reymond moder comynly exposicion doctours lord sayd tho wordes veray hede hys chosen bothe f eel strong who sensualyte naturelly drede deth myght example bothe freel folk strong folk dyspeyre felte theyre sensualyt e kyndely dredyng deth holy mayde answerd sayd actes dedys sauiour yf ben wysely consydered euery creature hys consyderacyon may fynde ghostly felyng spedefull hys helthe therfore syth soo feble freall creature fynden tho wordes comfort ageynst theyr feblenesse ryght necessary thenne perfyt folk myghty shold fynde also ther jnne cofyrmacyon theyr strengthe whiche myght thys exposycyon afore therfore better yt expowned many maners yt al may comforted ther thene maner wyse one maner folk allone whanne mayster reymond herde helde hys pea meruayllyng hyr grete wysdom grace de neuer exposycyon afore p another exposycyon wordes holy mayde mayster reymond founde wryten book hir fyrst confessour wrote ben tyme whan rauysshed lerned lord prayer whiche made fore hys passyon whan watt bothe blood water seynge thus transfer hunc calicem fader remoue peynfull passion fro prayed thenne whome sawe afore wolde haue parte passion whiche peynfull passyon cause loued ryghtwysnesse put condycyon sayd verutamen non mea voluntas neuthelesse fader wyll fulfylled thy wyll yf putto suche condycyon wolde haue folowed ther sayd folk shold haue saued tyme thenne thus prayed herde saynte poule sayd hys reuerence exauditus est pter suam reuerencia exposycion wordes saynt poule comynly doctours vnderstonden ellys meruaylle sone god sholde haue herde also sayd another tyme mayster reymond taught hym passyons whiche lord god jhesu cryst ray god man suffred helthe mankynde myghty impossyble ony man erthe suffre sholde dye possyble many tyme yf suffred ryght loue yt thenne hath yet mankynde vnestymable vncomperable ryght hys passyon suffred constreynyng loue allone vnestymable wolde beleue thornes hys crowne sholde perysshe brayne bone quyk man sholde drawe theyre ioyntes phete sayd lordes passyon thus dinumerauerut omnia os mea tolde nombred bone body thenne may proued yt pryncypall cause hys passyon loue whiche shemed mankynde myght shewed conuenyently hys passyon semed naylles helde hym vpon crosse hys loue onely ne strengthe man ouercame hym ot loue men stronge holde hym worde hys mouthe fyll doune grounde whan came take hym suche hyghe wordes conuenyent wordes lordes passyon holy mayde comyne wyth mayster reymond yet sayd experyence hyr body som maner passyon cryst suffred crosse wold say impossyble ony erthely creature specyally cause grete loue lord passyon peyne yt suffred hyr herte soo semed hyr whyle hyr herte braste cutt sondre fro one ende thys grete peyne loue oftymes dede mennys syght thys bare wytnes many one whiche presente whanne dyed loue crystys passyon allone mayster reymond grete doubte put awaye doubte thought comen wyth holy mayde serche sothe hyr whether whanne axed hyr grete wepyng coude gyue none answer long tyme gydre last sayde fader wolde ye haue grete pyte compassyon sowle delyuered derke pryson lyght tyme see mery lyght eftesones reclused ageyn derke prysone wretche thus happed ordynaunce god synnes ne mayster reymond axed hir hir sowle fully departed fro body whome answerd sayd thus feruent fyre dyuyne loue ghoostly desyre moche hyr herte lyue lord endelesly loued though hyr herte hadde stone yren must nedys breste therfore fader vnderstondeth thys trouthe myn herte myn body thenne vndo opened fro ouermost partye nether onely strengthe pure loue semeth yet fele markys syssure myn herte ye may knowe yt sowle fully tyme deted fro body sette presence god sawe preuyt e god vn efull speke ony man erthe ther speche erthe expresse preuytees ony manis tongue wote well ofte mater tourmented gretly sowle consyderyng thenne tell sorowe wyth wepynge sobbyng thenne mayster reymond prayed hyr tell began hyr answerd sayde tyme fedde comforted wyth many vysyons reuelacyons lordes mercy fell seek pure loue laye doun myn bedde prayed lorde jhesu wolde delyuer wretchyd worlde oned perfytely whiche tyme wolde graunte grauted therfore long lyued lyf shold partyner passyon asmoche possyble dedly body suffre soo tolde hym rehersed afore ouer sayd loo fader suche experyence hys passyon made seke strengthe loue sowle desyred thyng ellys delyuered world fyre encrecyd sowle herte often tymes defayled departed sonder soule vtterly delyuered body neuerthelesse lytell tyme sorowe ne eftesones mayster reymond axed hir long tyme hyr sowle body sayd kepte hyr aboute haue beryed hyr foure houres thene reuyued ageyn yet axed hyr sawe tyme came soule ageyne body answerd thus fader tyme sowle sawe vnderstode ioye blessyd sowles peynes synners myn mynde wold suffre wordes wolde suffyce expresse shall tell sowle sawe diuyne essen cyall beyng god cause soo lothe vnpacyent lyue worlde loue hym loue crysten people whiche sowle restoryd body ageyne sholde defaylled dyed sorowe hyghest comfort haue whan suffre ony dysease haue perfyte vysyon god therfore trybulacyons ben heuysom comfortable ye may knowe ben conuersaunt wyth sawe also peynes dampned sowles peynes sowles ben purgatory whiche expresse perfytely wyth maner wordes yf wretched synners sawe leste peyne leuer chese bodely deth hondred tymes yf possyble thene suffre daye leste peyne specially sawe hem pony shed syngulerly synned matrymony whiche hadde kepte hem gyder honestly sholde folowed dylectacions theyr lustys mayster reymond hir confes sour axed hyr synne specyall greuously punysshed thenne synnes syth greuous synne sayd skylle soo grete conscyence synne ne grete contrycy synnes rather offended synne thenne ony synne whiche synner chargeth remoue penau ce grete synne neuer soo lytell thenne holy mayde proceded forthe hyr mater sayd thus also fader whane seen thyse ioyes thes peynes wenyng self hadde fully delyuered body oure lorde sayde seest thou doughter ioye lacke peyne haue offenden torne ageyn therfore thy body tell peple theyr errour theyr peryll wyth worde astonyed torne ageyne body sore aferde thenne lord sayd profyte mennys soules thou torne ageyne thou shalte lyue lyfe thou hast lyued fore ne kepe solytarie allone chambre thou shalte goo brode wynne sowles shall euer wyth goo wyth bothe goyng comyng thou shalte bere worshyp name ghoostly doctryne afore grete smale laye people clerkys fore relygyous folk also shall gyue bothe mouth wytte speke none may wythstande shall also bryng afore bysshoppys curate sowles confounde pryde whyles lorde spak thyse wordes sodeynly soule restored ageyne body whanne perceyued hadde grete sorowe wepte thre dayes thre hyghtes gyders wythout cessyng yet wyse absteyne ne refreyne ther fro whanne cometh mynde sodeynly come fro grete ioye vnto prysone body wonder therfore fader though myn herte brest euery day consyderyng grete excellent ioye tyme hadde whiche ferre fro done sowle hele therfore ther shall man meruayle though loue passyngly whome lord hath bede warne theyr synfull lyuyng haue lefte grete ioye certeyn tyme wote long therfore saynt poule seyth ben glorye crowne ioye thys saye fader putte youre hertes passyon grutchyng tyme comyng whan shall homely amonges men whan mayster reymond herde vnderstode grace gyue hym ceyued hys herte incredulytee blyndnes men sayde sholde publysshed wherfore bade bothe freres sustres whyle holy mayde lyued erthe sholde pupplysshe matree perceyued also somme folowed fyrst hyr doctryne wente backward coude ne myghte take hyr wordes leste sholde offende god yf hadde hydde hymself wythout wrytyng wrote perpetuell recorde hyr dyssece whyle lyued maydens knowe veraly al sothe shall tell wytnes recorde present wyth holy mayde whan thyse thynges befyll hyr tyme whan holy mayde drewe nye deth semed rehersed afore drewe aboute hyr wymmen ghoostly doughters herys sent hyr fyrst confessour frere thomas present hyr passage prayer holy exercyses comme dyng hyr sowle god came thre freres wyth hym mo present att passyng holy mayde whan passyd semed one freres took grete sorowe therfore vyolence hys wepyng veyne hys brest brosyd wyth caught coghe spatte gebettes blood thenne another sorowe stode aboute bothe wepte holy mayde passyd also hir brother whiche shappely lyue long payne thenne sayde frere thomas hir fyrst confessour seek frere wyth grete feyth trust brother wote well holy mayde grete reputacyon afore god hyr good lyuyng therfore take hyr honde putte place thy sekenes doubte thou shalte hole anone forth wyth dyd hadde helthe whiche tolde afterward al wolde ther also ghoostly doughter herys present thenne whiche called alyxa passyd worlde sone afterward moother came inne see whether passed ther none coude suppose otherwyse also two specyall wyttenessys aboute ordeyne body sholde beryed bothe susters penaunce saynt domynyk one called katheryne whiche hyr felawe longe tyme afore hyr cosyn lysa thus make ende thys chapytre p somme myracles wrought gracyously thys holy mayde aboute helthe sowles capitulum vij yf sholde reherce alle myracles lord shewed holy mayde myght rather make grete book comprehende hem oo chapytre cause wolde put awaye dulnesse sholde rede legende holy mayde aboute asmoche may vnder fewe wordes comprehende one chapytre myghte knowe vnder fewe wordes grete ben whiche passe ouer lyghtely therfore moche sowle passeth body worthynesse shall begynne tho myracles whiche shewed lord hyr aboute mennys sowles bodyes touchyng fyrst whan jamys jacob fader holy mayde perceyued hys doughter katheryne alle gyuen serue please lord rehersed fyrste partye thys legende euer loued tretyd hyr reueretly louyngly bedyng folk hys housholde none soo hardy lette katheryne hys doughter ony maner wyse euer wyll haue done thys grete cause doughter loued fader therfore commended specyally hyr faders helthe oft tymes oure lord suche truste hys doughters prayer supposed well myght haue god wold hys helthe sone fader sykened laye doune hys bedde seek whan holy mayde hys doughter perceyued anone prayed oure lorde hyr spouse helthe hyr fader answerd hyr lorde ende hys dayes worlde come spedefull hym abyde lenger lyf ne wente hyr fader vysyted hym examyned hym dysposed hys sowle founde redy wylfully passe worlde hauyng luste abyde lenger wherefor thanked lord hyghly thenne prayed lord eftesones syth hadde gyuen hyr fader grete grace passe worlde wythout synne wolde wouchesauf graunte hym also flee heuen wythout payne purgatory hadde answere wyse ryghtwysnesse must nedys kepte therfore ryght impossyble sowle haue clerenesse endeles ioye wythout perfyte purgacyon fore thy fader hath ben hys dayes good lyuyng among alle wedded folke also many good thynges well pleased wyth specyally touchyng yet neuerthelesse may sauyng ryghtwysnesse hys sowle must purged fyre brenne duste erthely conuersacyon whiche hardened endured soule thenne sayde holy mayde lord thus dere welbeloued lord may suffre yt fad sowle haue tenderly nourysshed haue many co fortes hys lyf tormented suche paynes praye lord goodnesse euer thou shewdest kynde suffre hys sowle goo hys body vnto ye tyme perfytly purged oo waye yt nede wyse payne purgatory suche wordes lorde shewed hys mercy meruayllously though obeyed voyce hys mayden bodely strengthes hir fader jamys beganne defaylle deth warde yet hys soule passed neuer body vnto tyme yt holy dysputacion betwene lord alledgyng hym ryghtwysnesse holy made axyng grace mercy laste long dysputacion holy mayde sayd lord welbeloued lord yf thys grace may wyse goten graunted without som maner ryghtwysnesse suffre ryghtwysnesse fall redy suffre al maner peyne euer thy goodnesse wyll ordeyne delyuerauce fad sowle thenne lord graunted hyr grace sayd loo doughter loue yt thou hast shall graunte thyne axyng shall delyuer thy faders soule fully payne thou shalbe suffre payne hym long thou lyuest whiche shall assygne holy mayde thanked lord sayde good blessyd lorde yu haste ordeyned wente hyr fader laye deieng comforted hym meruayllously hys endeles helthe ryght ioyefull went hym vnto tyme passyd worlde whan sowle passyd ye body anone forth wyth holy mayde payned wyth sekenes syde whiche called ilica passyo neuer went hir tyme passyd worlde ther neuer tyme afterward ye payne sayde bare recorde ofte tymes mayster reymond vertue hyr pacyence wythout ony com yson passyd hyr sekenes shall declare ye helpe god afterward last chapytre thrydde tye whan hyr faders soule delyuered body holy mayde smyled full manerly sayd wold god ye ben tyme wepte shewed gladnesse chere myght none wyse sawe hys blessyd sowle whan passed ye body receyued endelesse blysse wythout ony taryeng whiche ryght gladde lytell afore exyence ioye rehersed chapytre afore see ye maydens wysely prouydence lord wrought maydens fader lord myght yf wold haue purged soule many maner wy made hym able inough ioyes dyd thefe yt hynge hys ryght syde wold wythout som payne mayde sholde suffre axed hir encrece hir ioye whiche payne euer afterward swete hyr hyr semed wythout cause wyst well yt hir swetenesse shold euer encrece aftward hyr grace blysse ioye therfore myght wyse calle ye payne ilica passio swete peyne holy mayde tolde puely mayster reymond yt long tyme aft hir fad deth soule appyred oftymes hir thakyng hir hir grace yt receyued hir also tolde hir many puy thinges gaue hir warnyng ye assaillyng hir enemy therto kepte hir al ghostly euelys ryght haue tolde maydens myracle shewed ryghtwysmannys soule shall tell myracle shewed synfull mannes sowle p man dwellyng cyte sene whiche called andrewe full ryche man oute wordely thynges world full poure inwardly heuenly thynges vitio neyther dred ne loued god hasarder cursed blasphemer swerer god sayntes wythin afterward take wyth sykenes lay done bedde soo seke euery man leche sayde deed perceyued hys curat come hym comforte hym sholde beshryue take penaunce make testamet maner countre whan hadde herdde preeste counseylled hym despysed bothe hym cou seyll wyf consydered hauynge zele loue soule wente maner relygyous folke men wymmen stere hym god yet counseyll myght bowe hym confession contrycion synnes neyther wyth thretinge endeles paynes ne wyth rewardes endeles ioyes thenne eftsones curate came hym dredyng lest sholde haue deyed defaulte counseyll sayde hym sayd fyrste addynge therto many holsom wordes yet alwaye wretched man dispised hym afterward dyde afore bothe hym wordes p last fyll despeyre synne hooly ghost drewe faste deth afterward tolde frier thomas holy maydes fyrst confessour wente holy mayde hous pursuyng constrayne al vertu obedyens charyte praye lorde wolde vochesaf socour ye wretched soule bee dampned wythouten ende p whan came holy maides hous founde rauysshyd fro bodly wyttes longe occupyed durste occupye ne durst long abyde hous cause yt myght drewe fast vpon hym wherfore charged felowe here tyme wyth ye whiche called katheryn charge holy mayde goddes behalue whan restorid agayn bodely wyttes wolde praye suche mannys sowle lyeth passyng sayd wolde whan holy mayde herde soo greate compassyon soule prayed lord anone deuoutly besechyng hym entyerly soule shold perysshe whiche boughte wyth precious blode lord answerd sayde thus wyckednes hathe asserued payne horrybly blasphemie hath blasphemid myn sayntes wyth mouth also hath throwen table ye fyre despyte whiche paynted ymage myn passyon ymage myn blessyd gloryous moder sayntes therfore worthy ryghtwysnes yt brenne endeles fyre p thenne fyll downe prostrate wepyng foot lorde sayde lord yf thou wylt consydere narowe synnes men may escape endeles dampnacion wherfore comest thou downe born gloryous mayde suffer tourment cruell deth wayte mennys synnes punysshe theym horrybly endeles payne tellest thou synnes lost man barest vppon thyn sholders maner synnes whether come mercy ryghtwysnes haue myn lord blesfulle thou saydest whan yu puttest forthe helthe many mennys sowles haue none refresshinge lyf see myn neybours tourned alone suffer paciently thyn absence yf thou gyue ioye shall doo good meke lord put awaye fro yelde myn brother graciously obstynat herte p thus prayed contynuelly fro begynnyng nyght vnto graye mornynge tyme wepyng wythout ony slepe dysputyng wyth lorde alwaye helpe sowle oure lord aledgyng ryghtwysnes gyue hym vengeaunce synnes hooly mayde asking mercy last lord endeles mercy gaue answere sayde dere doughter shall shewe hym myn grace yu hast prayed andrewe sayde dere chylde whi wylt thou beshreue ye tres pa thou hast done loke yu beshryue redy forgyue thyn synnes thenne harde herte souple grace cryed wyth grete voyce meyny aboute hym sayde sende preste wyll byshryue lord jhesu crist hath warned shold beshryuen p whan meynye perceyued anone went preste preste came perfyghtly confessyd hym made testament wyth greate contrycion passyd thys worlde lord ihesu cryste p fader endeles mercy mercy able ben thy werkes profounde ben thyn prouydence who gracyous werk ben vnscrutable vnto man thou suffredest man hardyd hys synnes vnto laste ende femyng thou haddest none torce hym yet laste thou prouydest helthe thin seruaunt came hym stere hym grace yet al cou seylles myght auayle meke prayer thy meke mayde thou condescendyst mekely mercyabyly gaue boldenes herte thou gaue fyre compassyon herte brother thou gaue meke teres bowed thy mercy tre wely none thou thou aryssydyst vp thy spouse sholde bowe lord thyse ben thy werkes gloryfyest thyn saintes wyll coplued loue seyng thy mercy soo plentuous loo maydens mercy lorde shewed meke teres yet shall telle merueylous myracle p befyll also another tyme cyte seene two famous thefes ryght peryllous whiche take brought byfore temporall juge bee dampned payne mysdedes soo thei put cruell tourmente called tourmente hote yron wyse put carte tourmentours redy wyth hote yrous breune one place another body therto thefes soo obstynat neyther pryson ne pryson myght none creature stere shryue take penaunce trespaas ledde cyte make aferd blasphemed god saintis specyally whan felte brennynge cursed magnyfycence lorde soo semed thei payne temperall fyre drewe faste endeles fyre thenne oure lorde ihesu endeles goodnes whiche wold none body dampned saued thought wolde lete tho wretched sowlis medyacion spouse katheryn dampnacion soo ordenaunce hym hooly mayde quyete daye felawes hous loued vertuously whiche alixa who hous stood waye dampned wretch shold passe sondenly morowe alyxa herde merueylous voyce comyng hous wyth loked wyndowe sawe fyre two men whiche dampned hote yrens thenne wente agayne tolde holy mayde sayde yren whan holy mayde herde wente wyndowe loked tourned agayn prayer sawe sayde afterward mayster reymound confes sour grete multytude wycked spirytes aboute theym brennyd sowles wythin moche tourmentours dyde body wythout therfore stered double compassyon praye lord helpe wretched sowles payne seyeng thus ha ha mekest lord ihesu settest thou soo lytyl thy creature thou madest thyn lykenesse boughtest wyth thy precious blood aboue bodely torment thou suffrest theym cruelly tormentyd spyrytes wythinforth sowles whan thou illumynyst soo graciously theef henge ryght syde al toke tourment crosse wurthely hadde deserued knowleched god tourmente appostles doubte wherfore deserued thyn blessyd voyce whan thou saydest thus hodie mecum eris paradiso daye thou shalt wyth paradyse dedyst thou lorde trewely nothynge ellys yu woldest graunte forgyfnes suche lyke hym thou despysyd mary magdalene grete synner thou drewest graciously thou puttest fro puplycane ne woman cananye ne prince pupplycanis zacher rather thou calledest theym therfore thy mercy beseche thou helpe mercyabyly soules synners lad tourment thenne oure lorde bowed mercy wretch graut holy maide suche gra e wente wyth theym spyryte wepyng weylyng stere theym sonner repentaunce whan fendes sawe cryed alowde vppon sayde katheryne yf thou wylt leue thyn ghostely besynes prayng thyse sholde soo werke agaynste yu shalt trauayle wyth wycked spyryte answerd god wyll wyll therfore shal leue haue bygonne whan thyse wretch outward att gate cyte lord ihesu cryst appyred theym wyth blyssyd blody woundes steryng theym tournyd therto byhete theym forgyfnes soo dyuyne light entryd hertes asked apreste wyth grete instaunce beshryue tyme shryuen turnyd blasphemynge praysyng lord euer accusyng theym selfe seyeng wurthy tho paynes gretter paynes soo wyth grete gladnes went deth hadde gon grete feste consyderyd tho stode merueylyng gretely changynge perceyuyng euermore grete deuocio ye tourmetours yt durst nomore brenne thanked lord grete mercy none knewe wise bi who prayer mercy gyuen p neuertheles deuout preste whiche confessour commaund afterward wyth holy maydes confessour merueylynge grete mercy god soone tourned theym grace thene confessour asked afterward alixa holy maydes felawe thys holy mayde occupyed whan man ledde deth thenne alixa tolde hym processe sayd afore founde well record hour katherin lefte prayer tho dyed passed thys world whiche knewe perfyghtly afterward bi preuy reuelacion holy mayde p yet certen dayes passey felawes herd saye wyth full voyce time prayer thyse wordes lord ihesu thanke ye thou hast delyuerd theym second priso asked afterward ment therby sayd sowles theefes ben restored paradyse albe went purgatory tyme passed yet secid neuer prayer vnto tyme fully delyuerd payne parauet somme ther en set lityl myracle cause inuisybyll yf take hede inwardly wordes saynt augustyn saynt gregory shold fynde well myracle yf bodyes hadde ben reysed deth lyue saint gregory sayd thus bodely resurrexcio flesshe reysed whiche shal deye eftsones whan soule reysed shall lyue wythouten ende yet shall telle another synguler gyfte conuersacion thys hooly mayde wan god one whiche called abes amonges one chylde called james jacob synfull lyuer full pryde creuelte soo yet beyng yonge age kyllyd two men ful cruelly euery man knewe hym aferd hym ne loued hym euery day lyued werse werse suster called shy nochya whiche fully gyuen vanyte world passyng outrage aray body albe mayde bodi moder abes therof grete forowe lest shold dampned ther mysbelyuyng wente foly mayde prayed wolde vochesaf speke somwhat soule hele wyth doughter fracisca shynochya specyally wyth shynochya holy mayde hadde euer sowles grete compassyon graunted wolde gladly soo dyde prayer monycions lord ihesu cryste soo grounded soule shynochya sodenly put awaye fro vanyte ye world vsed pompous araye kyt awaye heer hede wherof woute proude tooke vppon habyte saynt domynyk made suster penaunce euer afterward lyued prayer medytacyons grete sharpe penaunce sone came hir suster francysca took vpon hyr abyte lyued gyder ryght deuoutely herde james jacob brother ye tyme sene whanne sustren torned came ye cyte ward wyth yong brother hys cursyng thretnyng wyth grete pryde tho excyted hys susters abyte seynge cryeng wyth bolde spyryte wolde tere awaye abyte fro back breng theim hys hows dwelled whome hys yonger brother whiche came hym sayd trewely james yf thou come sene thou shalt torned also shryuen thy synnes cursed hys brother bytterly sayde leuer flee bothe freres prestys thenne wolde shryuen ony hem chylde oftymes rehersed hys phecyes ofte cursed last entred cyte wood man forthe wente hys faders hows thretnyng wold grete horryble thynges yf sustren specyally ethynoccyam wolde awaye hyr abyte come home hym vnknowen holy mayde knowe neuer creature erthe god mene whyle moder rabes stylled peased hym prayng hym wolde abyde tyll morow morow sente holy maydes confessour frere thomas wolde wouchesauf come speke hir sone james counseyll hym hys sowle helthe came wyth hym felawe frere bartholomew spake hym speche semed myght profyte tyme holy mayde katheryne prayed lorde hys conuersyon while frere bartholomew spak hym thenne sodeynly oure lorde touched jamys herte contrycyon sayde frere bartholomew well apayed hys suster sholde serue god also prayed hym confessyon wyth grete contrycyon myght shriue hys synnes serue god also thenne perfytely shreuen somme synnes whiche wold neuer knowe ne confessyd noo man confessyd hym soo wyth inne lytell tyme wolfe made lambe lyon
