mayster reymound confessour wente pyse whome folowed afterward mayster reymound wyth certeyn hys bredren confessyons many ther came wha herde speke soo eruent wordes loue steryd therby contrycion le sholde lette fro trewe conuersacyo falle agayn fendes snare suche copuccion wold beidde theim go confession shryue without ony taryeng cause confessyon ofte tymes delayed defaute confessours therfore ofte tymes desyred myght haue confessours myght sende suche repentaunce therfore maister reymound two felawes hadde power pope bull assoyle tho endu ed confessyon holy mayde wha came pyse receyued burgeys hous called gerardus whiche gerad vpon daye brought wyth hi yonge man xx yere age alle seke feuers holy mayde besechinge wolde praye helthe tolde vexid xviij monethes gyders wyth feuers soo none daye hadde therto myghty hadde brought hym soo lowe well sene hys chekes hys body myght neuer none medecyn made hoole thenne holy mayde hadde grete compassyon herte yonge man asked hym longe goo shryue hys synnes toke penaunce sayd many yere therfore sayde lord hath yeue oorge thou hast purged thy soule holy confessyon soo longe tyme therfore sone goo forthe anone confession cast venim whiche enfecteth alle thy body whan confessyd ame agayne put holy honde vpon sholders sayd hym thus goo sone pee lord hesu cryst wyll thou nomore vexed wyth tho feuers sayd fro time forward vexed therwyth within fewe dayes came holy mayde thanked curacion sayde openly afore folke hadde neuer feuers sythe voyded vertu lord ff bereth wytnes mayster reymound sawe myracle wytnesse ynow gerad childes moder many afterward yonge man puplychid miracle e contree suche another byfyll cyte seene moche merueylous cause sikenes perylous p suster penaunce saynt domynyke yte seene called gemina whiche loued well holy mayde sekenes hir throte whiche called ynce contynaunce tyme sekenes encresyd soo made throte soo streyght vnethe might drawe brethe almoost ofte tymes strangelyd thenne wente holy mayde prayed myght speke seyenge thus moder shaldeye ye helpe holy maide hadde soo grete compassyon toke holy honde crossed throte p anone wythout ony taryenge e sekenes avoyded soo come wyth grete sorowe went home wyth grete gladnesse tolde soone confessour cause somme haue tolde curacions done body holy mayde diuerse persones therfore shall telle grete notable myracle lorde wrought blessyd holy mayde p befyll holy mayde wente tyme fro pyse auyoun wyth whome wente two good deuoute yonge men wrote lettres holy mayde wolde sende one called neryus afterward deuoute recluse ca led stephene afterward monke charterhous good vyrtuous lyuer therto yte auyoun wente al mayster reymoud p happed whan entred cyte auyoun forsayd neryus seke wyth merueylou sykenes bowellis myght haue none reste neyther nyght ne daye cryed wayled ofte tymes might lye bedde creped hondes foot sought reste yet myght none fynde tolde holy maide badde mayster reymound sende afleches helpe hym comforte wolde none gyue mayster reymoud dyde soo none leche myght ese rather payned trowe ende allone cause lord wolde worke myrarle spouse katheryn last leche said maister reymoud yt myght prouffyte hym therfore hadde none truste lyffe p whan mayster reymound hadde tolde companye sate mete stephene felowe neryus roos vp wyth grete spyryte went holy maydes chambre sytyng doune knee prayed mekely wyll suffre felowe neryus deye suche straunge contree holy mayde answerde thus sone art thou heui thou sholdest sory thy felawe lorde wyll rewarde hym blysse pacyence sufferyng sekenes thene sayd agayn dere moder yett myn prayer tyme helpe hym wote well ye may ye wyll thenne sayd well sone see well thou art conforme wil god haue tolde therfore sythe see thou art soo tourmentyd hym come morowe whan go masse houselyd reduce mater myn mynde shall sende vp thyn prayer god thou shalt praye maye herde thenne stephen well apayed wyth vyheste erly morowe mette wyth holy mayde goyng masse assone aspyed fyldoune knee prayed wolde forgete hym spake day afore tyme whan ho elyd rauysshed bodely wyttes prayed lord seke man soone restoryd ayen bodely wyttes came stephene smylyng whiche abode answere sayde vnto hym thus sone thou hast grace thou hast asked thenne asked whether neryus shold deliuerd sekenes sayd ye wyth wente gladly felawe badde hym good shall hole soo full tendaunt aboute recouer hym tyme mynystracion aboute hi happed stephene seke lay doune bedde passyng feuer whan holy mayde knewe hadde grete sowwe went hym asked hym sekenes hadde perceyued touchynge hys ponse vexed wyth strong feuer anone wyth greate feruour spyryte sayde thus charge feuer vertu obedyence tho goo man thenne went feuer waye wos vp hole ony taryeng thanked oure lorde grete grace shewed hys spouse katheryne another notable myracle shall telle suster penaunce whiche called johan dwellyng cyte sene tyme holy fader pope gregory lyued tyme cyte sene byddyng holy fader gregorye holy mayde sent florence make pee betwene hym rebell child florece ye whiche mat longe tell mater shall hau chapytre hit self afterward ye helpe god whan come florence wyth hyr felawe here whiche called johan trete pee betwene oure holy fader rebell people people sette lytell hyr wordes laundred hyr meruayllously set hyr nought ne counseylled withdrawe hyr whyle vnto tyme cessyd theyr malyce dyd yet sayd wold neuer passe cyte tyme accorded pee cryed thorugh cyte florence sayde thenne wente syde lodgyd lytell besyde cyte sodeynly hir suster johan seek hyr foot hyr foot forswo land ther wyth payne hyr foot grete eruent ax double wyse tormented myght goo wyth hyr thy holy mayde heuy therof wolde wy e leue hyr behynde le launder sholde spryng prayed lord helpe wold wouche auf mercyably helpe hyr fel whyle prayed hyr suster slepe whan awoke hole though sykenes anone arose vp went wyth holy mayde quykly euer dyd afore p myracle many one thanked lord sawe whiche wrought soo gracyously hys spouse katheryne yette shall tell another meruayllous thynge lord wrought hyr cyte tholetane whan holy mayde entred cyte tholetane took hir inne anone wente hir chambre wonte ye whiche mayster reymond come pope message sodeynly thenne herde stretys cyte wymmen holy womma come entred cyte ne soone cam men wymmen hyr inne axed thys holy mayde inne myght hyde hyr suffred wymmen onely goo hyr speke wyth hyr thenne ther one wommen hadde lytell chylde who whombe meruayllously swolle prayed holy mayde wold take childe hyr armes begynnyng refused cause vayn glorye ast ouercome pyte dyd hyr soone took chylde hir hondes anone ye childe deliuered moche wynde last hys bely aswagyd small euer soo chylde hole mayster reymond sawe myracle yet ther open speche therof cyte tholetane yt came bysshopys ere sent mayster reymond prayed hym myght speke wyth ye holy mayde childe neuewe vycary hys holy mayde came spake wyth bysshop many vertuous mater many moomeruayls lord wrought holy mayde ben wryten book fewe haue wryten maydens cause ye shall sonner gyue credence lord jhesu cryste dwellyd holy maydens soule whiche principally wrought thyse meruayllous werkys wytnes tho mater ye whiche ben reherced chapytre ben reherced afore tho place racles shewed thus endeth chapytre p myracles wrought thys holy mayde boute delyueraunce whiche encombred vexyd wyth fendes capitulum lx owre lorde myghty ihesu cessyd shewe outward ye fertue gaue inwarde hys spouse katheryne many meruayllous werkes vertue therfore lorde ihesu cryst angmented myghtly brest holy mayde onely shewed seek bodyes reherced afore also shewed voydyng wycked spyrytes shall declared chapytre helpe god ther cyte sene man whiche called mychael vsed craft wrytyng whan passed yeres age consent hys wyf purpose leue ye worlde serue lord specyally thenne wonte also make two doughters hys mynchyns monasterye cyte sene endowed worshyp saynt johan enange lyst hys lyst fulfylled last pryue dome god one doughts whiche made myn called laurencyana vill yere age aboute vexed fende yt monasterye vnquyeted hyr vexacyon ye last comyn assent sent hyr fader delyuered ageyne hys doughter wold nomore haue hyr monasterye long vexed whan take monasterye fende spak wythin hir ye childys mouth many wondre thynges latyn wordes many herde questyos ther pupplysshed many pryue synnes sclaunder many folke ye whiche myght well vnderstond yt good spyryte vexacyon hyr fader moder hir frendes ryght sory wente aboute dyuerse relyques sente seke helpe grace doughter myght delyuerd spiryte specyally trusted gretely relyques saynt ambrose whiche frere prechour whome lord graunted synguler gyfte put awaye wycked spyrytes soo hys cope yf layde vpon ony creature vexed wyth wicked spiryte sholde auoyded fore chylde brought frere prechours leyde vpon tombe saint ambrose hys clothes leyde childe fader mod prayed mene whyl helpe ef god ye sente yt chylde myght socourre yet tyme herde synne euer dyd trowe cause yt syguler remedyes reserued holy mayde thenne counseylled fad mod presente hyr doughter pratheryne holy mayde sent ye holy mayde prayenge hyr yt wolde helpe theyre doughter sent ageyn answer sayd often tymes defayled departed sonder soule vtterly delyuered body neuerthelesse lytell tyme sorowe ne eftesones mayster reymond axed hir long tyme hyr sowle body sayd kepte hyr aboute haue beryed hyr foure houres thene reuyued ageyn yet axed hyr sawe tyme came soule ageyne body answerd thus fader tyme sowle sawe vnderstode ioye blessyd sowles peynes synners myn mynde wold suffre wordes wolde suffyce expresse shall tell sowle sawe diuyne essen cyall beyng god cause soo lothe vnpacyent lyue worlde loue hym loue crysten people whiche sowle restoryd body ageyne sholde defaylled dyed sorowe hyghest comfort haue whan suffre ony dysease haue perfyte vysyon god therfore trybulacyons ben heuysom comfortable ye may knowe ben conuersaunt wyth sawe also peynes dampned sowles peynes sowles ben purgatory whiche expresse perfytely wyth maner wordes yf wretched synners sawe leste peyne leuer chese bodely deth hondred tymes yf possyble thene suffre daye leste peyne specially sawe hem ponysshed syngulerly synned matrymony whiche hadde kepte hem gyder honestly sholde folowed dylectacions theyr lustys mayster reymond hir confessour axed hyr synne specyall greuously punysshed thenne ther synnes syth greuous synne sayd skylle soo grete conscyence synne ne grete contrycyon synnes rather offended synne thenne ony synne whiche synner chargeth remoue penau ce grete synne neuer soo lytell thenne holy mayde proceded forthe hyr mater sayd thus also fader whane seen thyse ioyes thes peynes wenyng self hadde fully delyuered body oure lorde sayde seest thou doughter ioye lacke peyne haue offenden torne ageyn therfore thy body tell peple theyr errour theyr peryll wyth worde astonyed torne ageyne body sore aferde thenne ford sayd profyte mennys soules thou torne ageyne thou shalte lyue lyfe thou hast lyued fore ne kepe lytarie allone chambre thou shalte goo brode wynne sowles shall euer wyth goo wyth bothe goyng comyng thou shalte bere worshyp name ghoostly doctryne afore grete smale laye people clerkys fore relygyous folk also befyll yt wedowe yonge woman called alixe whiche wyth greate fauoure drewe holy mayde soo thought hadde soo grete affectyon semed myght liue without therfore toke habite susters penaunce soke owne hous hyred hows syde hooly maydes hows myght ofte bee conuersaunt wyth whan hadde thus hooly mayde ofte tymes hous wyth fledde tyme faders hous happed afterward ye yere cyte sene grete sharsyte breed corn soo ye stynkyng whete drawen erthe dyches whiche bought cytezynes cyte tyme good cause myght none begoten none pryce whiche stynkyng whete alyxe sorsayde wedowe must nedes ye ellys shold wythout br neu rtheles moche nyghe ye tyme herwest olde whete fayled brought marcat alixe wyst therof newe whete comen purpose cast awaye olde ynkyng whete beye newe bycause hole mayde hous wolde nothyng doo wythout counseyll wherfore opened purpos semyng thus moder sythe lord heth mercy wyth v syndyng newe whete wyll throwe myn olde inkyng whete holy mayde answerd thus yf ye wyll ete olde corn gyue ellys poure folke yt hauen none alixe sayd yt sholde haue greate conscitence gyue poure folke soo stynkyng whete hadde leuer gyue theim beste whete thenne holy mayde badde ordeyne water bryng stinkyng whete purposed caste awaye sayde wolde make brede therof poure folke sayde soo fyrst made dowe molded loues lytyll qua tyte whete encresyd soo plentuously moldyng alyxe seruaunt gretely astonyed sagen suche multyplycacio loues theym thought soo many loues myght made suche foure lytyll quantyte whete thys hooly mayde made sette forthe bake also none stynche tho loues made whete afore whan thei bake sette fourth ye table eten ye etyng foude none bitternes stynche thei saide eten therof eten neuer betyr brede alexe sent fo confessonr came wyth certain bretheren see myracle lyke sayd hym quantyte encresyng qualyte ryght well amendyd thyse two acles thyrde addyd breed largely gyuen poure folke yt wolde ete therof yet neuer ye lasse nombre alwaye fou de ynow ye breed hutche trewely thre fayr myracles fyrste put awaye stynche corn afterward encresyd loues muldyng laste multyplyed ye loues etyng breed soo moche myght vnnethe distribued bi many wekes togyders neended soo yt xx yere moo somme yt kepte breed relyke p thenne mayster reymound confessour asked ye myracle done answerd sayde hadde soo grete zele loue pour folke lest shold spylle defaulte soo tender loue lord lest gyfte sholde dyspysed went wyth grete feruour make breed stynkyng whete p thenne blessyd gloryous lady gloryous virgyn mary wyth multytude angelis stood helpe molde vertu holy gloryous hondes trowed loues encresed tho loues oure gloryous lady gloryous vyrgyn mary molded delyuerd holy mayde alixe seruaunt put ouen meruayle maiden though tho loues swete sythe hooly gloryous hondes oure blessyd gloryous lady gloryons virgin mary molded theym consydereth therforre good maydens taketh good heede meryte holy mayde vouchesaf blessyd glorious lady gloryous vyrgyn mary stonde helpe myracle make v vnderstonde come cyte r sted wyth certayn nombre ghoostely chyldren hadde noryssched vertu whiche folowed fro partyes tuskan maner agaynst hooly maydes wyll prechyng ghostely grace holy fader somme pylgrymage visitacions saintes whiche desyred go specyally holy maydes companye cause myght fedde wyth swetnesse blessyd conuersacion p thenne holy mayde hadde made ordynaunce amonges sholde haue aboute neyther golde ne syluer oonly sholde lyue poure almesse sholde herbourd hospytall p also wymmen eueryche theym weke sholde mynys lyflod suche hadde receyued almesse felawes myghten bee occupyed mene whyle prayer holy contemplacyons aboute theyr pylgrymages wherfore come cyte whan ordynaunce made soone happed johan whiche reherced afore mynystred hyr weke who weke befyll casuelly lacked brede whan hyr felawes sholde go mete thenne badde holy mayde afore whan lackyd brede shold warne hir ouer euen myght goo make somme ordynaunce johan forgete whan hyr felawes come mete johan wolde haue sette brede afore founde nomore cantell wolde vnnethe se ue foure theyr mete ther nombre persones xvj thenne johan wente holy mayde knowleched hyr neglygence sory shamefast seyeng ther brede lytell vnnethes wolde suffyse foure eche resteyne lytell whome holy mayde sayd suster god gyue haue ye neglygently brought v last nede myght ye haue warned bad well well byd goddes seruautes go sytte doun thenne sayde mynyster ther lytell brede yet byd sytte doun sayd holy mayde hir serue wyth lytell bydde begynne wyth lytell tyll god ordeyne thyse wordes holy mayde prayed whyle et johan fulfylled hir byddyng deuyded euery man lytell hongry folke gredy long fastyng ete fast wenyng sholde nomore mete haue also suposed lytell brede sholde soone alwaye hadde ete ynough yet brede myght defaylled thenne axed holy mayde dyd tolde prayed thenne sayd vertue hyr prayer lorde fedde fedde fyue thousand men wyth fyue louys thanked god whan hadde ete yet ther suche plente lefte poure folke ynough p yette shall tell another myracle mayster reymond bereth recorde whyche done tyme holy mayde passed worlde blysse heuen tyme hit happed mayster reymond counseyll pryour freres couent wolde doo somme solempne reuerence hede saynt katheryne blyssed virgyne tyme translated cyte rome freres dwelled sene sette daye bad mete hyr ghostely chyldren nourysshed vertue whyche day freres fully auysed gyue hyr solempne reuerence also fede day hyr ghoostly chyldren whan day comen solenpne done frere kepte botrye couent loked brede hadde couent gestys founde scarsely ynough half couent thenne couent fyfty aboute gestys twenty whan pryour herde sory neuerthelesse yet serued gestyn fyrst wyth lytell thenne couent wyth lytell quantyte among yet belefte ynough soo thenne eueryche couent gestys hadde plenteuously ynough vnnethe semed lytell nombre louys myght hadde suffysed fyfe fore whan eten pryour couent came thyder ther mayster reymond satte wyth ghoostly chyldren holy mayde saynt katheryne rehersed fore myracle thenne sayde mayster reymond wordes loo frendes holy mayde saynt katheryne day hyr solempnyte wyll leue v wythout somme myracle wyth whome famylyer whyles lyued erthe ofte tymes whan wyth v lyuyng lyf shewed myracle among v therfore shewe v accepteth oure obseruaunce daye done goddes worshyp herys hadde shewed myracle eftesonys hyr passyng wherfore yelde thankyng te almyghty god yet furthermore lord shewed meruayllous thynges spouse katheryn vnlyfely thynges floures hadde ofte tymes grete delyte cause florysshed vertue hyr self vesselles houshold lost destruyed thoo meruayllous thynges shall tell p thys holy mayde somme tyme cyte pyse herborowed worthy mannes hows cyte whiche man loued well holy mayde tyme ther whyle gretely feblyd body ofte excesse spyryt rauyshyng semed mayster reymond moo sawe hyr brought nye ye deth wherfore mayster reymond fore aferde lest sholde haue dyed bethought hym remedye myght ordeyne restore hyr lenger lyf wyst neuer myght ordeyne hyr egges wyne also letuaryes knewe welle myght ete thenne came hyr prayed hyr wolde receyue lytell suker hyr water drynketh whome answerd thus fader see well ye wyll take awaye fro lytell lyf whiche left suche swete drynkes doo well wete swete thingi dedly thenne mayster reymond souerenys hows bethought hem gydres remedye myght ordeyne ageynst hir feblynes last came mayster reymond mynde hadde see ofte tymes feble folke hadde wesshen somme tyme wyth vernage aboute temple pouses body restored strengthe gretly comforted thenne mayster reymond sayde souereyne hous thus syr sethe soo may putte noo comfortable remedye wythin hyr body lete v vse somme remedye wythout hyr body thenne sayde souerayne hows lytell besyde hys hows neyghboure hadde vessell vernage whome sayde wolde sende haue botell full therof knewe well sholde haue full gladly messenger sent hym tolde holy mayde feble wherfore praied maystrys behalf wold wouchesauf sende hyr botell vernage whome neyghboure answerd thus wolde sende hym redy certeyn sayde hys vessell emptyd therfore prayed hym holde hym excused wote well hows drope wyne ryght sory fore neuerthelesse seker come see thenne bere wytnesse trouth frende thou seest thenne forthwyth took messenger wyth ageynst messenger wyll brought hym hys wyne seler shewed hym vessell vernage whiche vessell semed outwarde tokenys voyde many day afore yet neuerthelesse good man dyd see trouthe voyde drewe spygot vessell drewe hys presence sholde see noo wyne inne soone hadde done soo vernage came ranne vpon grounde plentuously sore astonyed stopped vessell ageyne callyd hys meyne axed whether hadde putte ony wyne vernage vessell sayde naye knewe wyne thre monthys fore hadde grete meruayll wythoute ony lyquor putte ther inne thys af rward notefyed neghboures aboute sayde myracle messenger came ageyne wyth grete meruayll gladdenes bryngyng wyth hym botell vernage tolde myracle soo thoo herde thanked lord wrought suche myracle hys holy mayde katheryne many one aftward whan holy mayde hole came see hyr seyeng wyth grete meruaylle suche wordes may drynketh noo wyne myracle suche wordes people holy mayde caught grete sorowe hir herte knowleched afterward mayster reymond wyth suche sorowe waylyng prayed lord hyr sowle thenne hyr mouthe seyeng suche wordes good lord suffrest thou tormented herte shall folke shame reproue seruauntes thyne may lyue among people saue allone good lord axed thy myldenes wyne inspyracyon thi grace haue kept fro wine long tyme made people wyne orne reproue praye lord thy grete pyte make wyne vanysshe awaye whiche deuulgyd amonges men cesse lord hys mercy herde hyr prayer made vessell wyne decrece sodeynly ther semed full mennes drynkyng whiche drank therof deuocyon cause myracle decrecyd lye tho praysed afore myracle helde ther pe afterward shame mayster reymond moo hyr ghoostly chyldren ashamed theyr grete praysyng afore holy mayde jocunde gladde thankyng lord hyr spouse hadde delyuered hyr suche open praysyng men p praye maydens taketh de oure lorde kepte holy mayde vayne glorye sette hyr perfyte grounde mekenesse thyse two myracles fyrst gaue hyr mater worshyp wrought myracle wythout hyr wetyng fylled ye vessell wyne secounde gaue hyr mater folowe hym mekenes puttyng awaye vayne glorye whiche putte vpon hyr fyrst lord shewed vertue myracle endowed wyth secounde shewed wysdome fulfylled wyth mekenes wysdom neuertheles yet secou de myracle emptyng vessell gretter thenne fyrst fyllyng vessell semed well simylytude saynt gregorye makyth hys dyaloges betwyne vertue pacyence shewyng myracles whether seyth vertue pacyence passeth shewyng myraclee thenne may vertue trewe mekenes whiche neuer wythout wysdom passe ony comparyson shewyng myracles whiche come well pryde mekenes bestely man may wyse perceyue meruaylle saynt poule sayde prudence flesshe wyse subiecte god loo maydens haue tolde myracles lord shewed spouse katheryne vnlyfly creature thus make ende chapytre wytnesse chapytre also ben expressyd afore wyth inne chapytre myracles ben declared p ofte receyuyng holy sacrament aulter meruaylles whiche lord dyd hyr touchyng holy sacrament relyques sayntes capitulum xij knowen knew holy mayde whyle lyued erthe excellent loue hadde reuerence deuocyon aboute worshypfull sacrament aultre oure lorde hys flesshe hys blood often receyuyng therof hit comyn seyeng among people katheryne holy mayde houselyd euery day lyued ther allone wythout ony bodely mete sayd alwaye trouthe yet suppose tolde mekely gyuynge honour god euer apperyth meruaylous hys chosen neuertheles cause receyued ofte euery daye yet ther somme grutched wyth ageynst whome may brought wytnes ynough holy faders dyd fyrst shall tell vse holy chyrche olde tyme saynt denys seyth book made de ecclesiastica jerarchia begynnyng holy chyrche feruoure holy ghoost haboundaunt hertes feythfull creature bothe men wo men receyued sacramente aulter euery daye furthermore doctryne holy chyrche techeth euery feythfull man bounde dedely synne yf haue actuell deuocyon lefull hym also merytorye receyue excellent worshypfull sacramente whoo thenne durst forbede suche feythfull persone suche holy lyuer ony maner wise wynne ofte grete mede receyuyn worshypfull sacramente trewely doubte therof suche creature grete wrong yf denyed whan mekely vxed yf wolde say vtterly lefull creature neuer feythfull ne neuer soo perfyte ne deuote receyue blyssed sacramente ofte shall tell answere holy mayde gaue bysshop presence mayster reymond sayd wordes aforsayd hyr alledgyng hym wordes saynt austyn seyth thus euery day receyue sacrament aulter nother prayse ne blame obyeccyon answerde holy mayde wyse bysshoppe fader yf saynt austyn blame ye alled ge holy doctour ageynst youre selfe ouermore shall tell saynt thomas uyne seyth thys doubte whether spedefull crysten man ofte tymes euery day receyue sacrament aulter answereth thus therto ofte receyuyng blyssed sacrament encrecyth deuocyon hym receyueth lessyth whyles hys reuerence sholde haue blyssed sacramente therfore euery feythfull crysten man sholde haue bothe reuerence deuocyon blyssed sacramente whan feyleth hys reuerence lessened ofte receyuyng blyssed sacramente sholde absteyne whyle myght go therto afterward wyth reuerence yf fele hys reuerence euer hole neuer lessened encrecyd wyth deuocyon euer receyueth thenne may sekerly receyue truely wythout ony doubte suche sowle well dyspesed wynneth moche mede receyuyng blyssed sacramente thys holsom doctryne deuoute holy doctoure saynt thomas kepte holy mayde katheryne ofte tyme receyued blyssed sacramente somme tyme absteyned hyr ther fro hadde euer desyre knytte hyr spouse medytacyon blyssed sacrament brennyng charyte drawe hym moche whyle desyred houseled hadde receyued day whan desyred blyssed sacrament shold haue passion syknes hir body though hadde vexyd long tyme afore wyth contynuell sekenes feuer sykenes body came fro passyon soule many came auyon cyte sene thoughte loke holy mayde ferde entred hyr hous aboute none dayes founde hyr hir oratorye saynt markys day euangelyst soone sawe hym rose ageynst hym sayd hym wordes wolde god sawe hyr face lyke face angell sendyng bemys bryghtnesse soo moche meruaylled sayd hym self ou e lord thus thys katheryns face certeyne lorde thy dere spouse wyth torned hym aulter sayde thys wordes tarye whan cesyd rauysshyng mayster reymound toke asyde tolde dysese vnder fewe wordes cause man frende sholde lette anone smylyd vppon mayster reymound askyng hym thus gladly fader sought ye aboute sayde yes thenne sayde haue ye soo grete sow therfore wyth yt smiled ft went soo forth speke wyth pryour charterhous mene tyme mayster reymound abode somwhat comforted fully vnto ye tyme wyst myght leue well maydens whan holy mayde perceyued moche dysease encrecyd holy chyrche scysme yt begonne perceyuyng also crystys vycarye suffred grete dysease wept day nyght prayed lord pee wold wouchesauf set pee holy chyrche thenne lord comforted hyr som maner wyse yere afore half dyed oure lorde gaue double vyctorye holy chyrche crystys vycarye pope well castell saynt angell cyte rome whiche scysmatykes hondes daye people helde castell name scysmatykes ye daye take castell yolde holy fader pope myght dwelle rome wonte cause enemyes castell saynt aungell knowe cam holy mayde axed hir counseyll sholde thenne gaue hym counseyll shold go barfoot people rome wyth hym mynster saynt peter thankynge lord god wyth good deuocyon grace benefetys whiche thus holy chyrche beganne quyken holy mayde hadde therof grete comfort soone hir sorowe began encrece eftsonis fende myght strayn gers assayed cyte rome made dysoorde bytwene ye people cyte pope perceyued holy mayde prayed lord wolde wouchesauf put hys mercyable honde suffre cursyd synne done prayed sawe cyte full fendes styryng excytyng people kylle theyr ghoostly fader cryed horrybly holy mayde whyle prayed seynge hyr thus thou cursed wretche thou arte aboute lette v therfore shall slee wyth horryble deth whome answerd worde prayed besyly feruently axyng lord wold wouches auf worshyp hys holy name remedye holy chyrche thenne stood grete meshyef kepe hyr hys vycarye wythout harme suffre peple suche synne put awaye fendes fro theyr purpose whiche steryng people ther hadde answere lord doughter suff e peple euery day blasteme myn holy name falle synne myght soo dystruye theyr cursed wretchydnesse ryghtwysnes axyth shold suff e theyr wyckydnes thenne prayed feruently wyth suche wordes sayde mekest myldest lord thou knowest well thy spouse holy chyrche dyseased tormented almost thorugh world routhe thou knowest well also sewe helper defender hath therfore yf slee thy vy carye ben purpose hit shall onely greuous people rome crysten people thempre therfore good blyssed lorde thy ryghtwyse honde dyspyse thy people yu haste bought soo de wyth thy precyous blood torne thy mercyable honde cesse myshyef prayer contynued many dayes gyder wrote mayster reymond letter euer lord alledgyng ryghtwysnes axyng mercy tyme fendes cryed ho ybly vpon hir rehersed afore feble afflyccyon yt yf lord kepte hyr strengthe hyr e shold borste last sayd lord wordes lorde syth yt mercy may graunted wythout ryghtwysnes beseche despyse prayer maner payne people sholde haue put body shall glad dely eceyue worshyp thy name sauacyon holy chyrche thenne lord alledged nomore hys ryghtwysnes helde hys pee gaue hyr vyctorye fro houre forthward grutchyng cessyd peopl ly lytell hyr passyons encreced ferforth serpentes hell power god rmented hyr body cruely vncredyble man byleue yf hadde seen sayden sawe ther p esente whanne hyr body au tyshed sawe serpentes fretted deuoured maydens body therin lefte bone without skynne though ben consumed wasted long lyeng erthe yet neuerthe walked prayde wonte whiche many folke wonder thyng semed rather wonder thyng loke vpon ne naturell thyng hyr tormentes payne encreced contynually whyche consumed yet cessyd prayer prayed ore feruently len er thenne wonte hyr ghoostly chyldren hadde nourysshed vertue tyme sawe openly markes stroke endes helle gaue hyr hyr bodye myght therto remedy two skylles one wyste well hit wyll god whome myght wythstonde another cause sawe hyr gladde ioyfull hyr paynes prayed hyr bodely payne yet wolde cesse therfore tormentours helle faylled cryed vpon hyr alle tyme sayde hyr thus cursed wr tche thou hast euer ageynst v therfore thy tyme come auenged vpon thou haste putte v oft tymes praye therfore shall neuer cesse vnto tyme thou arte oute thys yf thys sente letter mayster reymond soo contynued payne sondaye septuagesme vnto ye last daye apryll saue one day ye whiche day passed world ye whiche tyme meruayllo thyng happed hyr sayd wrote mayster reymond cuery daye befyll hyr custome hadde passyon syde callyd lyca passio moo vnto none tyme wherfore ofte tymes desyred heryng hyr masse therfore euery daye morowe thenne payne came vpon hyr wente saynt peter chyrche thorugh oute alle lenten soo herde hyr masse abode tyll euensong thenne came home ageyne laye hyr doune hyr bedde whiche bedde who hadde seen hyr wolde haue sworne myghte neuer remeue hyr then yet next mo wse vp wente eftsonys f place called via pape saynt peter chirche soo fast hyr journey sholde haue made hole man wery thys contynued lenten wythin fewe dayes laye styll hyr bedd myght remeue hyr then feblenes last oure lorde called hyr passyd thys worlde p daye rehersed afore aboute none dayes nyne twenty daye apryll whiche vpon sondaye yere lord thousand thre hondred foure ore whyche daye feste saynt peter martyr ordre frece prechours solempnysed holy chyrche p many notable thynges wroughte thenne hyr passyng whyche lefte chapytre shall declared openly ynough helpe god next chapytre thus endeth chapytre p mayde desyred vnbounde fro body wyth cryste prouyd deuote prayer made putte ende another book whiche mayde book generally short ly wryten book wyth oryson capitulum ij whanne ende bodely lyf blyssed mayde katheryn drewe faste vpon hyr oure lorde shewed ioye hyr hyr passyng dyuers token whiche ioy glorye purposed rewarde hys spouse hyr labour sykenes heue answeryng gyftes grace receyued erthe among token whiche shewed perfeccyon hyr owl thoo wolde consydere quy kened hyr desyr euery daye desyre vnbounde body wyth cryst skylle myght clerely openly beholde blysse uthe whiche sawe lyfe myrour feyth whiche desyre soo moche encrecyth hy herte moche lyght aboue kynde shyned hyr herde heuen therfore aboute yere halfe afore thenne passyd worlde oure lorde shewed hyr suche cle e knowyng uthe constreyned shewe openly oute wrytyng cause prayed wryters rehersed afore whan sawe hyr rauysshyng sholde dy wryte whiche sholde speke mouthe tyme soo lytell tyme compyled book conteyneth maner dyaloge bytwene soule axynge oure lorde foure petycyons oure lorde ihesu cryst answeryng soule enformyng many profytable trouthys last ende whiche book two thynges ben sette semeth nedefull reherse well grete profyte rederys sholde fynde therin declare blyssed maydens desyre hadde soo perfyt ly hyr soule p neuerthelesse cause noo body sholde mysdeme wenyng wolde translate wyse thenne sayd hyr owne language therfore purpose translate none wyse thenne sayde worde worde tho two thynges fyrst recapytulacyon book sette ende whiche rehersed shortly tho thynges ben dyffusely sette book afore seconde prayer whiche holy mayde made whanne hadde endyd hyr book whyche prayer openly shewed desyre hadd vnbounde loosyd oute hyr body wyth cryst afore recapytulacyon thys holy mayde reherseth ende oke almyghty god fader oure lorde ihesu cryst spekyth soule atte e ende dyaloges tyme hadde long tyme spoke afore obedyence perfyte folke wyse p welbeloued dere doughter haue made sythe thy desyre ro begynnyng laste ende whiche haue made spekyng obedyence yf thou haue good mynde begynnyng thou axest wyth grete desyre herte made axe sholde encrece fyre charyte thy soule thou axest also foure petycyons whyche one thy selfe whiche petycyon made sethe illumynyng whiche lyght trouthe shewyng alle maner whiche maner medytacyon lyght feyth wyth knowele chyng thy self thou come e knoweleche trouthe secounde petycyon thou axest sholde mercy wyth worlde thrydde petycion mystery body spouse holy chirche prayng sholde wythdrawe derkenesse perfeccyon hyr suffreth thou axest sholde punysshe wyckydnes vpon therfore declared paynes fynyte gyuen tyme fynyte selfe allone maye make satysfaccyon trespas doone ageynste whiche god infynyte maketh seeth well yf oned wyth contrycion herte desyre oule maner maketh dewe satysfaccio declared yet euermore answere wyll mercy worlde shewyng mercy appropryd wherfore grete mercy vnestimable loue hadde mankynde sente myn begoten sone declare openly lykenyd brydge stretchy atteyneth heuen erthe hede whiche made hym dyuyne nature mankinde also make clere lyght trouthe shewed wyth yt may ye vp brydge iij degree whiche en thre myghtes owle also worde brydge made another lykenes fygure myn owne body thyrde sayde degree thou knowest well fyrst e foot wounded seconde syde wounded thyrde blessyd mouth whiche putte thre state ye soule yt vnperfgiht state ye fight state vnperfyght state ye whiche perfig state soule atteyneth comyth perfyghtly ye excellent vnyte loue shewynge also euery forsayd state thynge wythdraweth putteth away inperfeccion waye men maye goo therto also tolde e preuy deceytes fendes properte ghos ly loue spekynge also reprehencions thyse thre state whiche mekenes doth maketh first reprehencion put yt done er lyue soule go body second deth eym deyen dedely synne wy hope saide wente vnder brydge way ye fende tellyng mysery wretchednes suche dampned soules reprehencion shall bedone generall dome tolde somwhat paynes dampned soules ioye whiche blyssed soules haue wha shall receyue owne bodyes also promytted eftsones promytte wyth moche sufferaunce shall reforme myn spouse byddyng theym suffre playnyng wyth wickednes mineuyll seruauntes wyug excellens wourthines haue sette theym reuerence requyre wyl seculers done shewyng also defaute theym reuerence ought done shold lesned suche lesnyng reuerence ysplesaut contrarye myn wyll also spake vertu theym lyue vertuously er e angellis touchinge also wyth excellens reuerend sacrament aulter also cause spake fosayd iij state soule thou woldest wete knowe also estate teres whens come tolde ye accorde ye statis ri wyth ye state ye soule sayde al come well herte ordeynatly assygned cause suche teres ye iiij state eres ye firste state r yt causeth deth also tolde answerd also thyn fourthe petycion whiche petycion yu praydest yt wolde prouyde euery partyculer ca might happe prouyded purueyde therfore thou knowest well aboue declared told prouydence well generall speciall begynnynge begynnyng creacion mankynde vnto ende worlde made alle thynges make yet wyth hym dyuyne pro ydence gyuyng promytting euer gyuen bee ybulacions elli temperall comfor spyrytuall comfortes thynges done good ye maye bee made holy myn trouthe may performyd trouthe haue made nought ye maye receyue euerlastyng whiche touthe made open blode myn begoten sone also laste made seeth thyn desyre promyssyon made tellynge perfection obedyence whens cometh may wythdrawe awaye obedyens put obedyens generall key tolde also partyculer obedyens bothe perfyght folke vnperfyght folke well wythin lygion wythout relygyon spekyng eche theym dystynctly ee obedyens yeueth wer yt inobedyens maketh moche inobedyent man disceyu th hym selfe addyng puttyng inobedyen adam eth entred alle world souerayne gloryous euerlastynge fader endeles trouthe veryte conclude obedyens myn go n sone ye shall haue euerlastynge lyff ryght ye token de fyrst olde man synne soo alle ye wyllen keye obedyens haue take lyf newe man whiche swete ihesus st haue made bridge af tyme ye waye heuen booke yt ye mowe goo swete ryght waye whiche one ryght veryte shynyng wyth keye obedyens ye maye passe derkenesse worlde outen offence laste wyth keye myn obedyent sone ye maye op ne heuen stere alle myn seruauntes wepe wyth wepyng meke contynuell prayer pray ng wyll mercy worlde renued ye worlde waye trouthe yt yu shalt afterward bee repreuyd wyth lyght steryng shall aske mor haue doo afore sythen soo haue shewed myn selfe myn trouthe take hede thou goo celle knowlec thyn self therin spende conserue tresour haue gyue whiche tresour one doctryne trouthe gronuded vppon stedfaste quycke stone whiche ihesu cry e doctryne also clothed wyth yght whiche derkenesse ben destroyed therfore welbeloued doughter bee arayed wyth lyght trouthe thenne soule holy mayde katheryn tyme sawe wyth eye vnderstondyng medyacion lyght faythe knowe ryght yly trouthe excellens obedyens herd wyth ryght felynge tastyng wyth affection wyth vnspecabyll desyre beholdyng dyuyne reuerend mageste thanked hym sayeng thus p thanke gloryous fader almyghty god thou aste despysed thyne hondwerke ne thou haste tourned awaye thyn face oo ne despysed myn desire thou endele lygh considerest myn deth ne thou leche despisest mi gr sekenes ye endeles puryte despysest full fylthe moche wretchednesse thou infynmyte consyderest fynite thou wysdom wysdom beholdest foly thyse moo infynyte wretchydnesses innumerable defautes yt ben thou hast despysed ne thyn wysdom thyn goodnes thy mekenes thyn endeles goodnes hathe dyspysed rather thou hast gyue lyght thyn lyghte thy wysdome haue knowe treuthe thy mekenes haue founde charyte loue min neyghbours styred therto none vertu thyn chary thyn loue alone co yneth illumyne myn vnder stodyng lyght aythe sholde vnderstonde knowe thyn u whiche thou hast made open p good lord graunte myn mynde mouth bee capax catchyng helpe conserue alle thyne benefaytes also myn wyll maye brenne wyth fyre thyn charyte whiche fyre maye make myn body gyue gyfte martyrdome loue thyn precyous blood maye opene yates heuen wyth keye obedyens aske euery resonable creature welle generalle partyculer also mysteri body holy chyrche p knowlec denye yu hast loued fyrste thenne thou louest soo vnspecable thynne creature thou art lykened somme maner wy e man sat loue endeles eternyte god de whiche vnyon dyuyne natri e ast made bloode thyn oonly goten sone moche wourthe p e yt suffyseth rawnsome mankynde thou endeles trynyte art deepe see whiche eke f nde fynde seke thou fulfyllest many maner vnsaciabyle thyn depthe thou fulfyllest soo soule euer byleu th hongry hongryng endeles gloryous inyte desy eth see lyght thyn lyghte yght erte desyreth welle wa r soo desyreth soule passe derke body see w e thou art longe shalle thyn swe louely face behyd myn eyen p endeles gloryous trynyte depthe fyre charyte dyssolue beseche tyme forward clowde myn dedely body knowlec yt thou hast gyue thyn wthe coarteth co streyneth desyre deposycion greuous body maketh gredy gelde mxn lyff praysyng ioye thyne worshypfull name haue tasted seye wyth lyght vnderstondynge thyn lyght thyn depthe endeles gloryous trinyte ye fayrenes thyncreature goo whan see myn self see lyke thyn image endeles gloryous fader gyuyng thyn myght thyn wysdome myn vnderstondyng whiche wyssdome apperyd thyn oonly begoten sone holy ghooste cometh gloryous fader thyn owne begoten sone hath gyue wyll whiche hath made able loue thou endeles gloryous trynyte art maker thyn honde werke wherby haue knowe illumy yng myn recreacion thou dydest precious blood thyn onli begoten sone thou maner sotted wyth loue fayrenesse thyn creature depthe endeles godhede depe see myghtest thou gyue thy self thou art fyre yt euer brennyste thou wastest neuer thou art fyre consumest alle propyr loue soule thyn heete yu art also fyre doost awaye coldenesse illumyniste soulys thy lyght wyth whiche lyght thou hast made knowe thyn trouthe thou art lyght aboue lyght whiche thy lyghte gyuest hyghenes vnderstondynge su naturall lyght soo grete habu daunce perfyghtnesse also lyght faythe clarefied whiche faith see myn soule haue lyfe lyght hath receyued lyght lyght fayth seke wysdome thyn goten sone lyght fayth made stronge stedfast perseueraunt lyght fayth seke hope yu shalt suffer defayle waye also lyght techeth waye wherby sholde walke wythout lyght sholde walke derkenes therfore haue asked endeled gloryous holy fader thou sholdest illumyne wyth lyght moost holyest faythe trewely lyght see ye whiche norysshed soule vnto tyme peasyble see endeles gloryous holy trynyte water see troubled water therfore gyueth drede rather giueth know leche trouthe ti water dystylled maketh opyn pryue thynges therfore habundaunt lyght thyn habundeth soule maner clarefied tho thynges byleueth see endeles glorious holy trinite maketh knowe mirrour whiche whyle holde wyth honde lou afore eyen soule representeth thyne creature lyght myrrour represented knowe moost hyghest infirmyte god good good aboue good blessed good incomprehensybill good vnestymabyll good fay nesse aboue fayrnesse wysdom aboue wysdom thou art wysdome thou art angelys mete hast gyuen thyne self men wyth fyre charyt thou clothyng hast coueryd myn nakednesse thou fydest v hungry thyn swetnesse yu ete wythout ony bytternes endeles swete gloryous trynite thyn light hast gyue haue receyued medytacion lyght holyest sight declaracion haue knowe waye thyn grete perfe tion many merueylous declaracions sholde serue fro thys tyme forward wyth lyght wyth derkenes maye myrrour good ensample holy lyuyng maye aryse wretchyd lyff whiche hyder alwaye haue serued derkenesse haue knowe thyn trewthe afore thefore louy nought knewe trewely see ye wyth lyght holyest moost gloryous fayth trewely clowde myn owne ou hathe derked eyen myn vnderstondyng thou endeles swete gloryous holy trynyte thyn lyght hast dissoluyd derkenesse may att yne ye heyghthe yelde thankyng grrte gyftes soo large benefeytis yt thou hast gyue thyn doct yne treuthe yu hast gyue nowe whiche doctrine partyculer grace aboue generall grace thougyuest creature thou vouchedest sat condescende myn necessyte necessite creature whiche tyme comyng wyll beholde reuthe myrrour p therfore reuerende lord answere thyn self yu haste gyue gyftes make satysfactyon thyn gyftes answer theym gyuyng lyght grace thou maye yelde thankynge wyth lyght grace clothe make maye bee arayed wythe thyn endeles trouthe maye renne dedely waye wyth obediens wythg lyght moost holyest teytn loo maydens nere myght coude haue translated worde worde wordes booke prayer holy mayde whiche gyfte ye besely take hede ye maye wors ippe excellence thys blessyd mayde maner yuyng also doctryne trouthe whyche ryght meruelous sayde namely woman p furthermore ye maye perceyue thy se wordes desyred gretely bee vnbounde body cryste knewe vnderstoode well moche beter wyth cryst lyue lyf therfore desire euer encrecyd vnto tyme fulli desire full weddyng oned swete gloryous holy ghost whiche promytted vnto yonge age whan receyued gloryous lorde almyghty god rynge spousa le rehersyd afore laste chapytre fyrst party nexte chapytre shall declared holy mayde virgyn passyd world p tyme whan h oly mayde passed world sermen made ghoostely dy yples susteren ore er passyng p nd enformed generall enspecyall sholde gouerne whan goo p vy n whiche shewed matrone houre passyng capitu um v whanne holy mayde perceyued vnderstode reu lacy n ye houre dethe drewe nygh drewe ghostely dyscyples spa e generally longe notable sermon exortacion encrece vertu whyche exortacyon expressyd somme certayn notabylytes whiche purpos wryte boke p te notable doctryne taughte thys whatso euer bet cometh ye seruyce god yf wyll haue good e ely nede ull hym make herte naked sensyble loue certayn persones euery creature yt euer hold stretche vp soule reuerend lord maker symply wyth alle desyre herte herte may holy yeuen god fre fro loue opyn symple wythout doub lnesse soo affermed selfe yt alle principall labour besynes fro yong age vnto ye tyme euer come fection also sayd knewe well suche state fectio whiche al ye herte gyue gloryous lord almyghty god soule may come fyghly whyles answerd whyles smyled though hadde soorned wordes herde hyr enemyes whyles enflammed loue holy ghost one worde marked well herde hyr whan spak ghoostly batayll tyme styll cert yn tyme hering semed wordes put ageynst hyr hyr enemyes wyth gladde chere answerd thus mayne glorye neuer ray trowe glorye honour forde jhesu cryst wordes dysposycyon oure forde sayde wythout cause ther many ghoostly men wymmen wened ye grete grace lord gyuen hir sought praysyng ye peple ellys som maner dylectacyon inne therfore sayd desyred conuersaunt among men moche yt som wold saye mayster reymond hir confessour thus enneth womman thus yf desyre serue god abydeth home hyr celle herto may answeryd answeryth afore hyr ghoostly enemyes hir passyng thus vayne glory neuer ray trewe glory lord ihesu cryst though myght answere thus ranne aboute ne dyde none maner ghostly werke vayne glorye honour glory lord ihesu crystis name mayster reymond bereth recorde treuthe herde hyr confessyon bothe generall specyall wherfore recordeth sothe euer dyd hit done worthyp god praysyng men moche yt thou noo man ye tyme whan prayed ordeyned theyr bodely nede myght veryfyed hyr wordes ye apostle seyth thus nostra conuersatio celis est oure conuersacyon heuen yt euer dyd erthe hyr con sacion heuen tyme thenne long contynued long ghostely batayll wyth hyr enemyes resorted ageyne hyr self made generall confessyon openly whiche callyd confytro axyng forgyuenes eftsonys lowyng doctryne exsample saynt martyne saynt jerom saynt austyn shewed bothe hyr dedys hyr wordes man neuer excellent vertue lyf shold passe world wythout waylyng hertely penaunce hys synnes token saynt austyn hys last ende whan shold passe worlde ordeyned wryte hym seuen psalmes penaunce sette vpon ye wall myght see tho psalmys laye hys bedde whiche psalmes radde ofte wepte plenteuously seyeng also saynt jerom whan sholde dede made generall open confessyon hys synnes defautes saynt martyne also laste ende taught hys dyseyples crysten man shold deye asshys heyre token meke hertety penaunce holy mayde folowed maner tokenes shewyng hertely penaunce axyng mekely many tymes oft absolucyon bothe hyr synnes paynes thenne soone beganne wexe febler febler yette cessed neuer holy exhortacyon hyr dysciples bothe presente absent specyally tyme charged hyr dysciples axe counseyll mayster reymond doubte euer hadde furthermore saye whan came home yt faylle ne aferde noo thyng shall falle euer contynue vertuously sayd wolde wyth hym delyuer hym peryll whan doth ony thyng sholde shall gyue hym warnyng sayde amende thyse wordes sayd often tymes tha last ende hir passyng last worde sayd domine manus tuas comnendo spiritum meum blyssed soule paste body complyd knytte hir spouse ihesu loued hyghly wyth indyuysyble perpetuell hede vnyon yere lord thousand threhondred foure soore nyne twenty daye apryll whiche cyte rome fyll vpon sonday houre tyerce houre sowle holy mayde appyred mayster reymond tyme ferre contreys open bodely apparycyon mentall apparycyon seyng hym soule suche wordes comfort drede heuen may helpe defende seker therfore drede wyth whiche cofortable wordes mayster reymond maner astonyed ameruaylled myght wenyng comforte hadde come oure blyssed lady moder mercy cause stood fore ymage here sayd aue maria yet neuertheles aferde thinke cause thought vnworthy haue suche comfort hyr myght mene myght whennys myght come nyst neuer afterward heryng another reuelacyon holy mayde shewed deuoute matrone vnderstood better myght mene soo whens myght come whiche matrone shall tell tyme whan holy mayde passyd worlde rome deuoute matrone called semya whiche hadde two men hyr sone whome euery daye bothe moder seruant makyng theyr mete thys deuoute matrone tyme hyr husbonde dede purposed euer serue god visyte pylgrymage holy sayntes rome continued many yeres hadde also custome ryse mydnyght praye afterward take lytell rest syttyng lenyng wyth hyr hede myght quycker morowe erly go hyr stacyons rome befyll soone whan holy mayde katheryn come rome deuoute matrone took knowleche hyr often tymes edyfyed hyr good exhortacyons soo hadde good ghoostly affeccyon hyr ofte tymes homely wyth hyr hyr hows almost euery daye neuertheles ytell afore holy mayde deyed came hyr bycause certeyn besynes hadde done hyr pylgrymages purueyaunce mete hyr sone therfore wyst holy mayde passyd thys deuoute matrone semya arose vp atte mydnyght wonte doo praye longe tyme gydre purposed reste lytell cause wolde vp tymes morowe nasse thenne besye aboute hyr chyldren mete dyde soo euer trayueylled hyr slepe sholde wretche fende hath deceyued se vp thenne wente seke paryshe chyrches somme hole mass aseyeng wente herde le rynge masse hows nonnys gladde thenne thyder wente lefte hyr wortys vnpy kyd vnwashe hast shytte hir e bare keye wyth hyr whan came masse ye begynnyng wyth sayd hyr self thus wote well fende hath deceyued wende neuertheles moche wyste well mete hyr sone myght redy came home mete sory comforte yt hadde hyr ma e commytted god prayeng hym wold wouche sauf kepe hir day fro heuy wordes hyr chyldren whyche growen men sore aferde dysplease soo herde forthe hye masse whan hye masse done went home mette wyth hyr sone comynge homward mete seyeng hyr thus moder hye faste tyme go mete answerd ageynefull esely sayd good sone abydeth whyle ye shall go mete anone whanne entred hir hous founde hyr mete redy ynough wortys redy potte well soden full astonyed ked lord herde hyr masse badde hir sone sytte done mete ye name jhesu thynkyng hyr self none wolde go vysyte holy mayde katheryne mete tyme thought moche vysyon cofermed wyth grete myracles mene whyles hyr sone commended theyr mete sayd beter sesoned tyme ony mete hadde eten afore many daye deuoute matrones erte alwaye vpon vysyon seyeng wythin hyr selfe thus moder katheryne crystis spouse yet thys wende hadde dede whan hyr sone gone hadde et wente katherynes hous knockyd dore herde none answere sayd hyr ye neyghboures yt walkyd vysyte holy place yet treuthe hir susters wythin waylyng wolde suffre none entre tyme hadde axyd counseyll shold body last determyned amonges morowe body shold ladde frere prechours ye seruyse god wold ordeyne counseyll done soone body come ye chyrche ye people folowed touche hir fet hir clothys bothe ye freres also hir sustres hir dysciples aferde lest sholde haue borste toren hyr clothys therfore sette body wythin chauntell chapell endued worshyp saynt domynyk fyll afterwarde thynke declare nexte chapytre helpe god casuelly whyles thys adoyng semya matrone came inne mene tyme axyd noyse concourse people myghte mene hyt tolde hyr katheryne sene passyd oute thys worlde hyr body chyrche wherfore people gadred soo faste see anone whanne herde wayled wept wente inne body aye seyeng ghoostely chyldren thys holy mayde katheryne p vnpytuous woman haue ye hydde fro called ye passyng excusyd theym myght certayn cause prayed theym telle wha departed body sayde yester daye aboute vnderne daye wyth ye semya wepte sayde thus tyme sawe myn gloryous moder lad vp heuen ang li wyth thre precious crownes hede wote well sayd reuerend lorde almyghty sent angelys shewed passyng myn glorious moder gloryous saint katheryn sene ouer mynystred merueylously myn kytchyn moder gloryous moder vnderstoode whan hadde gloryous visyon thou tyme passid worlde thenne respyred tolde susters ghostely child here vysyon suche tyme al rehersed thus endeth chapitr p token myracles whiche reuerend lord almyghty god wrought de h hooly mayde vyrgyn gloryous saynt katheryn sene bothe tofore beryeng saye tho myracles knowe many ther yt knowe capitulum whan blessyd soule holy mayde keuerchefe thene gyue gayn dyd assone hadde keuerchefe agayn put arme hole anon wyth yt cryed people sayde arme hole myracle holy mayde vyrgyn gloryous katheryne thenne peple made moche noyse thankyng lady slepe bad sey lady sholde doo nomore medecyns sight euery daye morowe shold goo chirche ye seruyce reuerend lorde almyghty god thene shall hole whan seruaunt tolde lady thus dede soo laste lytil wythouten ony wrytyng openly ynoto ye ymages waxe offred vp sepulcre soone buryed neuertheles one myracle shall telle mayster reymoud bereth recorde befyll soone holy mayde vyrgyne buryed quene johan dere frendes th endeth chapitre ye maye see many fayr myracles whiche ye may vnderstonde hooly mayde virgyn dere spose lord reuerend lord almighty god th make ende boke saue cause holy chirche commendyth vertu pacience thenne shewyng myraclis saint gregrye sayth therfore thynke wryte chapytre vertu pacience holy mayde virgyn hadde wherin ye maye gader flonres fruyte encrece vertuous lyuyng helpe socour reuerend lord almyghty god swete ihesu cryste qui cum patre et spiritu sancto viuit et regnat deus per omnia secula seculorum amen p myght stronge paciens whiche holy mayde virgyn gloryous saint katheryn sene shewed openly fyrste yonge age vnto deth bi whiche virtu clerly prouyd ryghtfully worthy haue name godes chirche erthe whan made soo fayr glorious goddis chirche heuen chapytre recapytulacion holy fyll gloryous saint virgyn afore sayde werynesse reders also yf eche may haue ye hole holy lyf gloryous saint virgyne afore sayde thenne maye haue ye substau ce compendyously rehersyd capitulum vltimum holy doctour saynt gregorye seyth hys dyalogus yt vertue pacyence commendable thenne shewyng myracles cause moder holy chyrche wha wodel canonyze ony saynte fyrste enquyreth vertue pacyence thenne shewyng myracles two skylles one many euyll lyuers haue wond thynges shall yt semeth myracles though none symon magus dyd antecryst shall hys tyme another cause som ther hath ben haue done shewed myracle tue lord ihesu whiche haue dampned afterward juda tho yu lord speketh gospell sayth som shall stande ye lyfte syde day generall dome saye hym excusyng self lord haue thy name shewed wonderfull myracles whome lord shall answere ageyne say go ye werkers wickydnes thyse two skylles ye may vnderstonde ye holy chyrche erthe may certyfyed myracles whether ye sone holy shewed yt shewe presumpcyon holynesse namely tho myracles ben shewed deth sone sayntes who graues myracles ben shewed yet possyble yt mercyable lord sholde haue excused yelde theyr meke beleue whiche beleuen sayntes ben beryed glorye ioye hys owne name lest whiche beleue hym defrawded theyr desyre wherfore mod holy chyrche erthe gouerned holy ghost desyryng certefyed tho merites holy sayntes moche possyble lyf enquyreth specyally theyr vertuous lyuyng tho thynges yt wrought whyles lyued erthe soo lord ihesu hyr spouse taught hyr whan sayd ex fructi bus eo rum cognoscetis eos hyr werkys ye shall knowe folowed aftward place clause wryten afore yt good tree may bryng forthe euyll fruyte ben thyse fruytes trewely thyng ellys werkys loue charyte bothe god neyghbours cause werkys charyte ryght plesaunt lord ryght ben dysplesaunt fende yt may lette dedes charyte bothe hym self also worlde worldly lyuers wherfore full necessarye holy lyuers haue pacyence ceuerauce yf wyll rewarded theyr mede blysse whiche pacyence may conserue kepe good loue god theyr good neyghbours notwythstodyng maner secucyons therfore saynt powle assygned fyrst condycyon charyte pacyence whan sayd caritas paciens est charyte pacyence loo maydens cause oure moder holy chyrche erthe requyreth pacyence saynte yf sholde canonyzed thenne myracles among tuous werkys yet pacyens grettest wytnesse holynesse sayd maydens cause ye shold doubte holy maydens holynes vertue pacyence full blyssedly shall tell helpe god good prayer rehersyng hir dedes pacyence recapytulacyon hole legende namely wery reders thynken houre deuoute redyng lenger daye yf occupyed tale tryfles thenne semeth ye long day hort thenne houre vnderstonde well maydens holy mayde katherin ceyued v er tue pacyence myyt haue gracious werkyng soule fyrst vnlefull thynges remeuyd awaye namely suche vnlefull thyngys ben e ytable lustes ye flesshe wherfore thenne came age exyence flesshly lustes emeuyd awaye myghtly suche suche thynges sholde styre hyr wh n came age yet dyd wythout inspyracion notable vision lord ye whiche inspiracon whan j yere age saw lord arayde bisshop sytting ry fayre chambre ouer chirche f ere p echours wyth whome sawe saynt johan euangelyst whyles behelde lord lokyd vpon hyr full benyngly mekely blyssed hir holy vysyon hyr soule fulfylled wyth e loue putte awaye chyldren condycyons gaue hyr selfe anone prayer penaunce therin encrecyd fytly nexte yere whan vij yere age made vowe madenhode afore ymage lady sode ly wyth grete delyberacyon afore openly declared seconde thrydde chapytre fyrst tye furthermore cause holy mayde wyst well abstynence necessary kepe ye purpose maydenhode therfore gaue hir grete abstynence hyr yong age fourmed meruayllously reher thrydde chapytre fyrst ye vj chapytre partye largely began preuely leue flesshe thenne encrecyd age lytel lytell lefte maner etynge flesshe therto dranke wyne whan medled wyth wat r lost hys ast hys colour wyne whan xv yere age lefte bothe wyne flesshe maner mete take brede rawe herbes also whan xx yere age lefte brede took hir onely dyetyng rawe herbys soo contynued maner lyuyng vnto tyme lord gaue hir newe maner gracious lyuyng whan lyued without ony maner mete whan xxv xxvj yere age openly declared vj chapytre fyrst partye rehersed cause maner wherfore came suche estate also answered suffycyentely grutched maner lyuyng whan holy mayde hadde thus fully come styryng synnes came fyte vertue pacyence shall tell helpe god fyrst proue pacyence hyr moder lapa wold wedded whan came age xij yere whan sawe myght brynge hyr doughter well therto thenne putte hy hir chambre assygned hyr afore honeste putte hyr maner defoule kechen nother myght haue lesyr praye ne haue medytacyon ne contemplacyon wonte pacyence hadde secucyons gladde ther inne clerely declared fourthe chapytre fyrst partye meruayllously vertuously alwaye stode purpose maydenhode yet serued housholde wyth gladde chere neuer suche occupacyons pryuacyons hyr pure chambre cessyd fro prayer ghoostly excercyses vn tyme hadde ouercome bothe hyr persecucyons hyr pursuer rehersed fourthe chapytre yet ouermore whan fende styred hyr moder lapa sette holy mayde holy dyscyplynes wakynges also herde lyggyng thys holy mayde thenne wyth myghty pacyence meruayllous tempred ryght dyscretely hyr moders heuynes ageynst hyr yet neuerthelesse kepte forthe hyr hardenes lyuyng declared vj chapytre fyrst partye fully ynough moreouer impediment suffred hyr sowle fende tyme prayer ghoostly excercyses tormentyng hyr flesshe almes dedes dyd openly shewed many dyuers chapytres thys legende afore shall declare fende besyed hym myght fyrst remeue thys holy mayde awaye hyr spouse jhesu afterward wythdrawe hir fully hym ellys laste lette hyr namely tyme wyth myghty feruour fyrst ouerthrewe hyr enemye fende afterward wytte counseyll holy ghoost ouercome hym last wyth stedefast vertue shamed hym aboute lette hyr fyrst fende began remeue hyr fro hyr holy purpose fyrst hyr suster bonauenture whiche wedded curyosyte clothys declared openly fourthe chapytre fyrst partye seconde tyme hyr brethern hyr moder full purpose marye hir hit shewed chapytre thrydde tyme hym selfe puttyng hyr dyuers heuynes temptacyons dyuers illusyons thenne receyued habyte penaunce rehersed vij chapytre fyrst partye also mayster reymond hyr besyde enfourmed trewe folke tyme wha prayed afore crucifyxe lordes passyon fende stood afore hir hauyng hys honde clothe sylke aboute araye hyr wyth clothe whiche illusyon curyosyte dyspysed blyssed hyr torned hyr crucyfyxe fende vanysshed awaye yet lefte hyr mynde temptacyon curyosytre clothyng thenne anone hadde myne hir purpose maydenhode spak lord wyse dere lord swete spouse thou knowest well desyred neuer husbonde therfore praye helpe may ouercome temptacyons curyosyte vertue thyne holy name axe lord thou sholdest take awaye fro yt thou wouchesauf gyue vyctorye thy mercy soone hadde sayde wordes blyssed lady quene maydens apperyd hyr syght semyng hyr syght took oute ryght fayre clothe hyr sone syde wyth whiche clothe arrayed hyr afterward sayde thys holy mayde thus well wete doughter clothes whiche comen oute sone syde passen clothes fayrnes beaute thenne alle hyr temptacyon wente awaye gretely comforted seconde fende wythdrawe hir fully lord wytty counseyll holy ghoost ouercome hym lette hym hys wycked purpose pesyd hir moder lapa wyth grete wytte cessyd hir hir hastynes whan aboute lette hyr hyr penaunce doyng contynued afterwarde neuerthelesse hyr penaunce began also whan bare hir self wysely hir confessour counseyllours whiche counseylled hyr leue hyr grete abstynence lyue comyndyete declared fyfthe chapytre seconde partye also wysely meruayllously pesyd hir soueraynes forbode hir go place thyder lorde sente hyr yet fulfylled goddes byddynges esely pesyd hyr soueraynes pacyence hadde werke ther noo tongue tell ne penne wryte furthermore fende saw myght noo whyle remeue ne wythdrawe thys holy mayde hir deuoute purpose besyed namely certeyne tyme lette hyr onely hym self dyuers persones whiche shall tolde specyally wythinne forthe fyrst hyr owne moder lapa brought hyr ageynste soo greate benefactour god seyeng hyr euer waxe meke thorught gyftes receyueth took hede gyue hyr moogyftes grace soo moche fulfylled hyr desyre worlde soo hyr thynketh hyr dwellyng heuen wyth god erthe wyth men thynked also hath paradyse hyr self soo knowleche befyll wyth whyle lyued erthe whanne alle brennyng goddes loue felyd soo moche swetenes hym hym alle worlde vyle one whan lone wyth deuocyon preuy chambre loo sodeynly aungell gabryell stood gospell seyth sheylled sayde aue gracia plenum c whiche salutacyon whanne herde fyrst fer e afterwarde comfor ed wyth hys holy swete speche made seker doubtyng thyse thynges sothe shewed fyll erthe knelynge wyth hondes ioynde honoured sayde ecce ancilla domini fiat michi secundum verbum tuum saye loo seruaunt god done thy worde whiche worde sayd anone rauysshed soo grete fulnesse goddes grace enbasshed neuer felte soo moche swetenesse comforte soule rauysshyng goddes sonne took flesshe puryst blood wyth oute ony wem delyte cause god dede grace feyth mekenes wyth whiche troweth fulfeyth aungellys wordes meked dressed goddes wyll therfore wouchesaue gyue soo moche grace soo thou doughter alle thynges god heteth dothe haue thou mistrowyng ne yenstod hym seyeng lord doest thou exsample saye ecce ancilla domini c ony tyme fulfylled hyght ellys taken fro gyuen god blame thy owne self thynke thou hast done somme trespas syghte goddes mageste whiche goddes sentence chaunged hath wyll purchace lyf wythouten ende nedeth buxom herte commaundementes loue hym self god veray mekenesse obedyence contrayous tho synnes pryde inobedyence fore faders adam eue whiche lost grace dygnyte made p ouer thenne another tyme vygyle natyuyte oure lorde whan elysabeth crystys seruannt duryng longe prayer asked mekely god wyth moche de ocyon fallyng terys wolde gyue hyr grace ye whiche myght loue hym wyth hyr herte blyssed mayden besyde sayd hyr loueth god wyth hys herte whe e ye elysabeth whan ede af erme sayd loued god wyth hyr herte therfore styll answerd noo thyng thenne blessyd mayde sayd hyr wolde thou say loueth god perfytly certeyn bartholomew thapostle loued hym well laurence tyr johan euan gelyst apostle martyr therto sayd woldest thou loue hym ben slayn rostyd drynk venym whan durst afferme ne denye wolde suff e thynges name cryst thenne blyssed mayden sayd stedfastnesse say doughter yf thou wold loue god spoyled worldly thynges garmentes thy mynde wyll soo yt yu wyll noo thyng haue ne oueyte world wyll procure sonne mede bartholomew hath fleyeng yf thou paciently wronges reproues maner wronges born thou shalte haue mede laurence rostyng body whan thou art reproued soorned se nought yf thou e gladly mekely thou shalt haue mede johan euangelyst drynkyng venyme yf thou wolde ewe buxom wolde nyghe fulfyll sayd wold wyth euer helpyng whan spedfull ouer another tyme saynt elysabeth prayed hir prayeng thought wyth deuocyon sowle wyse blyssed mayde prayed shewed hyr sayde blyssed mayde answerd hyr prayeng doughter dyde wyll newe make fayre well fyrst gothe roote hyll vnder whiche water spryngeth herken th besyly vn syde veynes water gothe whan sought hym herkynge thenne begynneth delue syde hyll tyll fynde able begynnyng welstede fro spryngyng veynes afterward dressyth water well stede whiche maketh large fayre clene maketh wall well myddes well stone pylar fastned pypes aboute thorugh whiche water may passe eche half prop tably vse men dyd ghostely thenne wente hyll besyly herkened lerned lawe moyses x commandementes thenne fonde veyne water whan lerned redyng thynkyng prayeng wellhede begynnynge good loue god wyth herte wyth strengthes yt wa ye well shewe whan coceyued styff desyre loue thinges god loueth hate hateth forsothe kept shynyng water clere whan studyed kepe ye desyre myn herte ye affeccion ye sensualyte vnhurted fylth synne reysed wall aboue well wha besyed kepe al tues vnhurted namely mekenes pacyens myldnes wyth hope charyte mi liues ede tha reised ye echosen come god hath gyue hym take hath hym self wherfore doughter wolde thou praye besely thyn owne heale also ther shall grace bee encresyd thy prayer shall fruytfull happened elysabeth mornyng spyrytuall dysese duryng thre yere thought myght haue confessour ofte wolde bee confessyd wherfore god hauyng compassyon desolacyon assygned saynt johan euangelist confessour commaundynge soo ofte wolde shryuen sholde besely hir assoyle auctoryte shop soo goddis grace whan shroue saynt johan hadde full mynde synnes whan shroue ony confessour hadde vnnethes mynde sholde saye glad iocunde assoyling wha shroue saynt johan p befyll daye elysabeth goddes seruaunt suffred grete notable wronge another wycked woman wherfore mennys syght gretely dysplesyd last whan came agayn self thought hadde suff ed wronge thenne sodenly lyghtned wyth eruent spyryte charyte gaue prayer wyth passyng mornynge flowynge teres deuoutly prayenge besought god forsayde woman whiche taken ony wronge brast thyse wordes swete ayde hastynge god gyldest goode yll beseche thou ye de bereth wronge notable gladnesse holsom comforte soo haue joye therof sholde joye yf thy good doughter sayde voice sodenly soned erys sayde elysabeth though neuer made prayer pleased soo moche dooth therfore make knowen thy synnes forgyuen whan began telle hym one one trespaces hadde fresshe mynde sayenge suche suche haue prayer thynge yt myght ye plesauce god herde voyce sayng p spera domino fac bonitatem et cetera hope god doo goodnesse dwelle e thou shalt fede ryches delyt lord shall gyue thyn askyges thyn herte hope hym shall werke shall lede lyght thy ryght wysnes thy dome myddaye thou suggette lord praye hym daye whyles elysabeth lastyng prayer full bytterly wepte synnes lorde jhesu cryste confortatour theym ben soroufull sayde apperyng dere doughter trouble ne sory mynde thy synnes thy synnes ben forgyuen whan answeryd contrary sayde certayn yf wolde doo wyth rightfully mercyfully worthy dampned paynes helle thenne lorde jhesu cryste answered sayde doughter ryghtuosnesse done god fader synnes satysfaction fully made hym theym ryghtuousnesse asketh yf thou haue offen dyd god wyth membrys thy body ormentyd membris body thyn man kindes synnes yf thou trespased wyth honde wyth fete handy foot nayled crosse wyth harde nayles yf thou haue trespased wyth thy eyen myn eye blynfyld wyth clothe yf thou haue trespased wyth thyn erys myn rys herde blasphemes grete wronges yf yu haue trespased wyth thyn herte herte persed wyth spere yf thou haue offendyd wyth thy body body shorged soo sole fote vnto tope hede apperyd noo stede hole p therfore doughter thynke dew satysfaccion thy synnes doo full ryght wysly god fader sothely uffred paynes synfull wronges theym bare herte dyde synne ne gyle founden mouth p another tyme whan elysabeth goddes seruaunt prayeng sodenly sawe wyth ghostely eyen full fayre honde hadde longe fyngers palme large brode myddes palme wounde redde blode soone vnderstode honde cryste wondrede soo small soo longe also ne answerde small whiche cryst lyued flesshe nyghtes prayed helde hondes streyth forth dayes aueyled wyth hondes fete body tounes castellys prechynge kyngdome god herde voyce sayeng elysabeth loo thyrde tyme saye thy synnes ben fogyuen thou hast grace whiche voyce answerde lord yf bee halowed thou sayste whero maye wythholde offende thy mayeste eche daye somme thynge voyce sayde yf thou noo tyme offended thou sholde mocho mekyd folowed thou woldest loue soo moche thus thou sholdest waxe worse thenne fendes trusteth dredeth p therfore haue soo haloweth ye thou maye synne suffyseth haue gyue soo moche grace wolde suffre thy self slayne rather thenne thou sholdest offede dedely whan thys sayd cryst apperyd openly thought thyke lopred
